Replaces the slice-2 **60 s bell poll** with near-real-time **server-push**. **Publisher:** a ~10 s Celery Beat `pubsub_sweep` (`services/notifications/pubsub.py`, task **co-located** in `tasks/notifications.py` — no new task module) scans `read_at IS NULL AND created_at > now()-LOOKBACK(120 s)` notifications and `PUBLISH`es a **content-free** per-user nudge to `notify:user:{id}`, **de-duping on the immutable `notification.id`** via Redis `SET … NX EX` (TTL 240 s = 2×LOOKBACK). **Subscriber:** `GET /api/v1/notifications/stream` (`api/_sse.py::event_stream` + `api/notifications.py`) — authenticated-self, a pure per-user Redis subscriber returning a `StreamingResponse(text/event-stream)`. **Consumer:** `features/notifications/stream.ts` (`parseSseFrame` CRLF-tolerant · `openNotificationStream` — a `fetch`/`ReadableStream` reader carrying the bearer on the `Authorization` header [native `EventSource` can't set headers; **no token in any URL**] · `sleepWithSignal`) + the `useNotificationStream` hook (mounted in `NotificationBell`); `useNotificationCount` `refetchInterval 60_000→300_000` (the 5-min backstop kept). **Infra:** a Caddy `@sse` block (`path /api/v1/notifications/stream`) with `flush_interval -1`, **before** `@api` (first-match-wins); the dead `/events` token dropped. openapi documents the path (`text/event-stream`/401). **NO migration** (head stays `0066`), **NO new permission key** (authenticated-self, catalog `102`), **NO WORM**.

⚠ **THE crux the pre-code spec-validation (5-lens / 15-agent) caught BEFORE code:** a `created_at` **watermark is BROKEN** — `created_at = func.now() = transaction_timestamp()` (the txn *START*), so a notification enqueued via the SAVEPOINT inside a long/SERIALIZABLE caller txn (the ack sweep mints an org's whole DOC_ACK batch in ONE multi-second txn; `_cutover` is SERIALIZABLE) carries a `created_at` far behind its eventual COMMIT → a monotone watermark advances past it → **permanently missed** → would regress the highest-volume awareness source from 60 s to the 5-min backstop. **Fix = id-de-dup in Redis** (migration-free, immune to the txn-start clock, read-only sweep [no `FOR UPDATE`/lock], self-healing; over-publish harmless, under-publish caught by the backstop). Regression-tested.

⚠ **The DB-session crux:** `get_session` is a yield-dependency held until the `StreamingResponse` body exhausts — and an SSE body is **infinite** → a route streaming on `Depends(get_session)` would **pin a pooled DB connection per open stream** (`psycopg3`/QueuePool default 15/worker). Fix = auth in a **short-lived session** via `_stream_caller` (`async with get_sessionmaker()()` that CLOSES before streaming); the generator touches **NO DB**; `caller.id` captured into a local (`expire_on_commit=False` → detached-safe). `get_current_user`'s body extracted to a reusable `resolve_current_user` (byte-identical; the existing auth suite is the backstop). `event_stream`'s **nested** `try/finally` always `unsubscribe`+`aclose`s the pubsub AND `aclose`s the redis client on **every** exit (the **heartbeat write** is the real abrupt-drop detector; `: ping` every 20 s).

⚠ **The FE reconnect storm:** resetting backoff on *open* lets an accept-then-close server (a worker recycle / a build that trips gunicorn `--timeout 60`) spin a ~1 s reconnect+refetch loop (the on-connect nudge fires an invalidate each time). Fix = reset only after a **healthy duration** (`HEALTHY_MS`) + a hard **`MIN_RECONNECT_MS=3000` floor** (cap `30000`); `sleepWithSignal` is abort-aware so an unmount mid-backoff cancels the pending reconnect. ⚠ **A base MSW handler** (`test/msw/handlers.ts`, a **closeable** `: ping` stream) is load-bearing — without it the mounted hook fires an unhandled `/notifications/stream` fetch that breaks all 4 bell/shell suites under `onUnhandledRequest:"error"` (and a never-closing stream hangs the serial `maxWorkers:1` pool).

⚠ **The 2-UvicornWorker fact makes the Redis bus REQUIRED, not optional** (in-process fan-out wouldn't reach a connection on the other worker); Redis pub/sub fans one `PUBLISH` to all workers. The gunicorn `--timeout 60` × async UvicornWorker survives the long stream (smoke-verified >60 s idle). ⚠ **httpx's in-process `ASGITransport` BUFFERS an infinite SSE body** → an HTTP-200-stream integration test **HANGS** (even `resp.status_code` never arrives — empirically `PYTEST_EXIT=124` twice) → reworked to a direct `event_stream`-against-real-testcontainer-Redis test + the 401 test; the full HTTP 200 stream is **live-smoke-only** (the reviewer's named structural gap).

**Process:** brainstorm (3 owner forks: Beat-sweep→Redis pub/sub · nudge-only · keep a backstop) → pre-code spec-validation (caught 3 majors before code) → spec+plan → 9-task subagent-driven build (one stall on the ASGITransport-hang test, controller-reworked) → 3-lens whole-branch review (whole-branch opus **YES** · diff-critic **CLEAN** vs pinned Starlette 1.2.1/redis-py 6.4.0 · web-test-trap **CLEAN, mutation-verified** [4 prod mutations each went red]) → a fix wave folding the 2 recommended nets (cross-user channel isolation + the unsubscribe-raises teardown) → full gates green → **live-smoke PASS** (bell **0→1→2 via SSE without a refresh**, ~10 s sub-backstop; notification rendered in the popover; mark-all-read clears; **no token in URL**; >60 s idle survival; a dev Keycloak token-expiry correctly showed the three-state "(count unavailable)") → PR #285, **Codex 👍** (no findings).

**Named residuals (not faked):** full-payload push (owner: nudge-only — would add a 2nd count source + an R32 surface) · drop the backstop / a faster degraded cadence / a server `sse_enabled` kill-switch · a **`pushed_at` stamp column** (+partial index) for exact non-window de-dup (eliminates the LOOKBACK scan + the dedup-key churn; owner: migration-free for 5c) · a `created_at`/partial index to make the look-back scan index-served · push for **other surfaces** (the admin Health panel, the `/tasks` inbox count, register summaries) · a **`Last-Event-ID`** replay buffer · the publish-fails-mid-loop unit test (diff-critic, low-value) · the slice-4 timer-sweep claim-threshold filter (unrelated). **With 5c the whole Notification family (slices 1 → 5c) is COMPLETE.**

**Tests:** api unit **996→1005** (+9: `test_notification_pubsub` 5 [id-de-dup-once / same-user-collapse / flush-re-nudge / dedup-key / registration] · `test_sse` 4 [`sse_event` format · `event_stream` initial+message+heartbeat+teardown · aclose-teardown · unsubscribe-raises-teardown]) + **6** new integration in `test_notification_stream.py` (3 sweep [recent-unread nudges · read/old skipped · txn-start-clock-within-LOOKBACK still nudged] · `test_stream_requires_bearer` 401 · `event_stream`-against-real-Redis · cross-user isolation); web **1273→1286** (+13: `stream.test` 9 · `useNotificationStream` 3 [nudge→invalidate · storm-floor · mid-backoff-abort] · `NotificationBell` +1 mount). (S-notify-5c, BE+FE+1 Caddy line, NO migration [head `0066`], NO new key [catalog 102], api unit 996→1005 +6 integration, web 1273→1286, PR #285 squash `7505e58`.)

### S-notify-5b — notification delivery-health panel + the first admin Config tab (slice 5b; FE-heavy + one new read-only BE endpoint; NO migration [head stays `0066`]; PR #283 squash `45dff1e`)

**What shipped — the first admin Config tab + a read-only notification delivery-health panel, made discoverable by the first admin nav entry.** **BE:** a pure, org-scoped aggregator `services/notifications/health.py::get_delivery_health(session, org_id)` — conditional `count(*) FILTER(...)` + `min(created_at) FILTER(...)` over `notification_email` (failed / pending-now / scheduled-retry / suppressed + oldest-pending) + a count/min over `awareness_event` (the fan-out backlog) + the org's `notifications_email_enabled` echo + the last-10 `recent_failures` (`failed_at DESC NULLS LAST`) — behind `GET /admin/notifications/health` in `api/config.py` (gated the existing SYSTEM-domain `config.update`; org from `caller.org_id`, no org_id param → strict isolation) + the openapi path + the `NotificationDeliveryHealth`/`NotificationEmailFailure` schemas. **NO migration (head stays `0066`), NO ORM/model change, NO new permission key (catalog stays `102`), NO WORM touch.** **FE:** `lib/types` (`OrgConfig`/`OrgConfigUpdate`/`NotificationDeliveryHealth`/`NotificationEmailFailure`, pinned to the BE serializers) + `admin/hooks.ts` (`useOrgConfig` [derives a `forbidden` flag], `useUpdateOrgConfig` [PATCH; invalidates BOTH `["admin-config"]` AND `["notification-health"]`], `useNotificationHealth`) + `admin/NotificationHealthPanel.tsx` (read-only: stat cards, the recent-failures table, the email-off banner, AsOf+Refresh) + `admin/ConfigAdmin.tsx` (the two org toggles, working-state+dirty-diff+partial-PATCH save, renders the panel) + wiring (the AdminShell **Config tab**, the `/admin/config` route, a `config.update`-gated TopBar **Administration** entry). **Load-bearing (the spec-validation MAJOR):** the page no-access gate keys on the GET `/admin/config` **403 forbidden flag** (the `ProcessesAdmin`/`CapaBoardPage` precedent), NOT `usePermissions().can()` — a `can()` page-gate FLASHES NoAccessState to a legit admin on a cold `/admin` deep-link (the `/admin` subtree never warms the `/me/permissions` cache); `ConfigAdmin` imports NO `usePermissions`, while TopBar uses it ONLY for affordance-hiding (a transient `false` merely hides the menu item — harmless). `pending_now` mirrors the drain's real claim predicate (`PENDING & (next_attempt_at IS NULL OR ≤ now())`); `pending_scheduled` is its exact complement. `recent_failures` is operational-only (recipient + `last_error` = the SMTP error `str(exc)[:1000]`, R32-safe — a near-subset of the existing `system.email_delivery_failed` admin payload), rendered as a React text node. The Failed count carries the danger glyph `✕` + AA `--es-danger-text` ONLY when `>0` (DP-5) with a dedicated ZERO-count negative test (anti-tautology). The integration-test cleanup **UPDATE-neutralizes** the seeded rows (status→SENT / fanned_out_at→now), NOT `DELETE` — the app role has `REVOKE DELETE` on `notification_email`/`awareness_event` (0063/0066). **Owner forks (AskUserQuestion ×4):** Moderate health depth (not Minimal/Rich) · notification flags only (not all 6 org-config toggles) · read-only panel (no requeue) · add the TopBar admin entry (not URL-only).

**Process:** spec → a 6-lens pre-code spec-validation workflow (authz/cross-org/leak · query-correctness · contract/scope ALL clean with zero findings; the MAJOR data-403 finding + 2 minor + 2 nit folded) → a 7-task subagent-driven build (each TDD + task-reviewed) → a 3-lens final whole-branch review (opus whole-branch **Ready-to-merge YES** · diff-critic **CLEAN** · web-test-trap **1 MAJOR + 1 MINOR**, both test-infra: the DEFAULT PATCH `/admin/config` MSW handler echoed the request body → de-echoed to return the static fixture [a module-level mutable `current` would LEAK across tests — `resetHandlers` doesn't reset base-handler closures]; the AdminShell tab test asserted mere existence → `{ selected: true }`) → the full `/check-api` (caught + fixed an E501 + 2 unformatted test files the per-task per-file runs missed) + `/check-web` + `/check-contracts` all green → a live-smoke verified end-to-end. ⚠ **Codex round 1 — 3 P2s, ALL genuine + ALL fixed (`4030291`):** (1) the `config.update`-gated Admin entry linked to `/admin` whose index redirects to `/admin/users` (a `user.read`-gated page) → relink to `/admin/config` (open the surface the gate authorizes); (2) the health aggregate's WHERE filtered only `org_id` with all status checks inside `FILTER`s → it scanned the org's ever-growing `SENT` history (the `(status,next_attempt_at)` index can't help while status isn't a WHERE predicate) → add `status IN (FAILED,PENDING,SUPPRESSED)` to the WHERE (lossless — no bucket counts SENT — and lets the index skip sent rows); (3) the awareness backlog rendered only the count → add the oldest-pending age line. All 3 threads resolved; Codex 👍-approved.

**Live-smoke (dev stack, org AHT, `demo` login):** the rebuilt web+api images served the slice; the new TopBar **Administration** entry rendered (gated `config.update`, granted to all AHT users) → the **Config** tab → `/admin/config`; both toggles reflected the real config (email OFF, pierce ON), Save disabled-until-dirty; a seeded FAILED `notification_email` lit **Failed: ✕ 1** + the recent-failures row (recipient/error/attempts/relative-when), and a seeded PENDING row drained → **Suppressed: 1** (org email off — the panel reads real engine-processed state); the email-off banner showed; the **save round-trip** (toggle→Save→"Saved."→dirty-reset, both directions) PERSISTED across a full reload (server-side), and flipping the toggle hid/showed the banner (the dual `["notification-health"]` invalidation, live); bonus — S-deeplink-login preserved `/admin/config` through the full-reload SSO round-trip. **Named residuals (not faked):** a **requeue/redeliver** action for FAILED emails (read-only for 5b) · the other 4 org-config flags in the UI (own slice) · **rich delivery stats** (latency histogram, per-`last_error` distribution, digest backlog, last-drain timestamp) · a more-inclusive admin-nav gate (mostly moot now the entry links to `/admin/config`) · **5c (SSE)** replacing the slice-2 60s bell poll (the LAST Notification-family slice) · the slice-4 timer-sweep claim-threshold filter (unrelated). **Tests:** api unit **996 (unchanged — the new BE tests are integration)** + 3 new integration tests (`test_notification_health` [delta + org-isolation, UPDATE-neutralized cleanup] · `test_admin_notifications_health` [200 for a `config.update` holder / 403 without]); web **1261→1273** (+12: NotificationHealthPanel 5 [glyph ±, empty, email-off, error] + ConfigAdmin 4 [reflect+axe, save-partial-PATCH+stays, no-access-without-probe, load-error] + AdminShell Config-tab 1 + TopBar shown/hidden 2). (S-notify-5b, FE-heavy + 1 read-only BE endpoint, NO migration [head `0066`], NO new key [catalog 102], api unit 996 unchanged +3 integration, web 1261→1273, PR #283 squash `45dff1e`.)

### S-notify-5a — awareness events: `doc.released`, read-scope-filtered (slice 5a; BE-only; migration `0066`; PR #279 squash `7e5ffaf`)

**What shipped — the FIRST awareness event (doc 10 §9.2): a new Effective version (`doc.released`) now reaches exactly the users who can READ the document — a broadcast filtered by `document.read`, never a blast to all org members.** Architecture = a transactional **awareness outbox + read-scope fan-out worker** (the family's R53 "decouple the expensive 1→N off the release hot path" applied to a 1→N event): (1) a best-effort **SAVEPOINT emit hook** in the SERIALIZABLE `_cutover` (`services/vault/lifecycle.py`, after the RELEASED/SUPERSEDED audit, before the single commit) writes ONE `awareness_event` outbox row, atomic with the release; (2) a **`awareness_fan_out` Beat** (@120s) claims pending events (`FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` + `populate_existing`, fresh session per event, ONE commit per event, **NO per-event advisory lock** — the `outbox_drain` precedent), resolves the read-scoped audience, subtracts the actor (self-suppression), and creates per-recipient notification (+ digest/email) rows via the slice-3a machinery. **The crux = `services/authz/audience.py::resolve_document_readers`** — the per-user `gather_grants` + `authorize(document.read)` loop (deny-wins, ABAC-complete; a SQL join can't honor DENY overrides or time-windowed predicates), built on a new `services/authz/resource.py::build_document_resource_context` extracted from `api/documents._document_scope_by_id` (now a thin delegate; the api gate + the resolver share one builder; services never imports api). `source_ip=None` (the worker has no request IP) → an `ip_allow`-gated grant fails to match → fail-safe UNDER-inclusion; the resolver NEVER over-includes. Migration **0066**: an `awareness_event` outbox table (**REVOKE DELETE** — operational, INSERT/SELECT/UPDATE only — the 0010 ALTER-DEFAULT-PRIVILEGES trap) + a nullable `notification.subject_version_id` column + two migration-managed partial indexes (`ix_awareness_event_pending` WHERE `fanned_out_at IS NULL`; `uq_notification_dedup_awareness` on `(recipient,event_key,subject_type,subject_id,subject_version_id)` WHERE `task_id IS NULL` — both in `env.py`'s `_MIGRATION_MANAGED_INDEXES`, absent from the ORM) + the seeded `doc.released` template (raw `ON CONFLICT … WHERE is_effective`, NOT-EXISTS-guarded downgrade). **NO new permission key** (R38, catalog stays **102** — the resolver only *consumes* `document.read`), **NO web/openapi change**. The welded task path (`dispatch._enqueue_one`) was kept behaviour-identical via a DRY-extracted shared `resolve_delivery` helper (the slice-1..4 `test_notification_*` suites are the parity backstop — 60 unmoved). **Owner decisions (AskUserQuestion):** fire `doc.released` for ALL FSM releases incl. OBJ/MR + the singleton register heads (read-scope keeps each relevant); the re-release dedup fix = a **`subject_version_id` discriminator**; the send-time read filter = an accepted **R32-bounded fan-out-time residual** (no send-time re-check).

⚠ **A pre-code SPEC-VALIDATION workflow (8 agents: code-anchor verifiers + an adversarial refute panel) caught 3 real design flaws BEFORE any code** — the headline being the **version-LESS dedup**: the originally-specced `(recipient,event_key,subject_type,subject_id)` key (no version) would SILENTLY suppress every RE-RELEASE (the same doc_id re-enters `release()`/`_cutover`; the surviving release-#1 notification row dedups release-#2) — WORST for the singleton register heads (RSK/CTX/IPR) + OBJ/MR which republish through one stable head id → notified ONCE EVER → fixed by the `subject_version_id` discriminator so each new Effective version re-notifies; plus the **SERIALIZABLE-aware swallow** (`record_awareness_event` runs inside the SERIALIZABLE `_cutover`, NOT the Read-Committed task-creation txn the family's `enqueue_task_notifications` assumes — a blanket swallow of a `40001/40P01/23505` would mask a serialization conflict + turn a clean 409 into a 500 → it RE-RAISES exactly `_is_race_loss`'s SQLSTATE set so the race loser gets the clean 409, swallows only non-serialization); and the §4/§9.2 wording downgraded from "send-time-accurate" to fan-out-time. ⚠ **The final 4-lens whole-branch review (migration-reviewer + diff-critic + opus whole-branch + worker-safety/authz) probed the four crux mechanisms — no over-inclusion · exactly-once fan-out · R53 SERIALIZABLE emit · version-discriminated dedup — and ALL HELD; it found ONE real defect the per-task reviews missed: the fan-out template-miss path `await session.rollback()` THEN read `event.event_key` → the S-ing-4 `MissingGreenlet` trap (rollback expires the ORM instance → a synchronous lazy-refresh on an async session) — fixed by capturing the scalars into locals + dropping the rollback (reads-only branch; the lock releases on context exit, `fanned_out_at` stays NULL → re-claimed), mirroring the escalation no-template precedent, + a regression test that was green-suite-invisible before.** ⚠ **Codex — 2 P2, BOTH genuine + fixed** (round 2 = 👍): **P2#1** the per-recipient template-miss TOCTOU (the pre-loop probe covers probe-time absence, but if the template vanishes mid-loop `enqueue_awareness_one` returns `no_template` and the loop ignored it → still stamped → missed recipients never retried) → the loop now treats `no_template` as a retry (return without commit/stamp → re-claimed); **P2#2** the 3a digest renderer grouped by `(event_key, subject_id)` only → two Effective versions of one doc in a digest window collapse to the first title `×N`, omitting the later version → the grouping key += `subject_version_id` (NULL-safe → task-row digests unchanged).

**Live-smoke (BE-driven, dev stack org AHT):** the populated dev DB upgraded 0065→0066 (the real upgrade CI's fresh DB can't prove); the `awareness_fanout` Beat registered+scheduled; a real `doc.released` emit for IPR-GEN-001 (Rev A) → the REAL `fan_out_awareness` → `{events:1, notifications:3}` (Mara/Priya/Demo, title "IPR-GEN-001 Rev A is now Effective" — template + version-label SUBSTITUTED, deep_link `/documents/{id}`, `task_id=None`, `subject_version_id` set); VERIFIED actor Ken **self-suppressed**, every recipient a `document.read` holder, idempotency (2nd sweep `{events:0,notifications:0}`). (All 4 dev users hold `document.read` on the head → the non-reader EXCLUSION is e2e-covered not shown live; the self-suppression exclusion IS shown live.) **Named residuals (not faked):** the spec-§11 resolver edge-case tests (PROCESS/FOLDER/time-windowed/`ip_allow` — de-risked: the resolver reuses the shared request-path PDP, the deny-wins backstop IS tested) · a dedicated concurrent-fan-out test + a serialization-injected-at-INSERT test (idempotency + the SERIALIZABLE re-raise are structurally proven + naturally-raced/unit-covered) · the unused `_pending_event_ids(now)` (the deferred slice-4 claim-threshold filter) · `_is_serialization_error` vs `_is_race_loss` not DRY (agree under psycopg3) · imported-baseline awareness (the ingestion path bypasses `_cutover` — a deliberate exclusion) · the **remaining awareness event keys** (`doc.approved`/`doc.obsoleted`/`dcr.raised`/`audit.scheduled`/`finding.assigned`/`capa.stage_changed`/`mr.scheduled` — these rails carry them, several with non-read-scope role/stakeholder audiences) · **5b** (the Health delivery-failure panel + the net-new admin Config tab) · **5c** (SSE replacing the slice-2 60s bell poll). **Tests:** api unit **988→996** (+4 `_is_serialization_error` classifier, +2 Beat-registration, +2 digest-version-grouping render) + the awareness integration suite (`test_audience_resolver` [deny-wins/SYSTEM/inactive/self-suppression], `test_authz_resource_extraction` [parity], `test_awareness_enqueue` [created/deduped/re-release], `test_awareness_emit` [one-event + concurrent-release 409 + version-id], `test_awareness_e2e` [read-scope filter + self-suppression + idempotency + re-release + org-off + template-miss]); web unchanged (**1261**). (S-notify-5a, BE-only, migration **0066** [head `0065`→`0066`], api unit 988→996, web 1261, PR #279 squash `7e5ffaf`.)

### S-notify-4 — escalation timers: reminders + overdue + escalate-to-manager (slice 4; BE-only; migration `0065`; PR #276 squash `6c41c90`)

**What shipped — the durable `timer_sweep` Beat (doc 10 §9.5, R29): off a `Task`'s `due_at` + an `SlaPolicy` it sends a pre-due REMINDER (`task.due_soon`), marks/notifies OVERDUE (`task.overdue` — which finally makes the S-notify-3a quiet-hours PIERCE reachable end-to-end, the named 3a/3b deferral), and ESCALATES an overdue workflow task to the assignee's manager (`task.escalated`, QMS-Owner fallback), idempotent + audited.** Migration **0065**: a new `sla_policy` table (keyed by `TaskType`, INTERVAL reminder/escalate offsets, **SELECT-only for the app role** — REVOKE the `0010` ALTER-DEFAULT-PRIVILEGES auto-grant since it's a TABLE — seed-managed reference data, one active row per type) + 4 nullable task timer-stamp columns (`remind_1_sent_at`/`remind_2_sent_at`/`overdue_notified_at`/`escalated_1_at`, the idempotency guard) + a migration-managed partial index `ix_task_timer_pending` (in `env.py`'s `_MIGRATION_MANAGED_INDEXES`, absent from the ORM) + an additive `ALTER TYPE event_type ADD VALUE TASK_ESCALATED` (autocommit_block, appended-last → auto in `EVENT_TYPE_VALUES`) + seeds (12 policies + 3 `en` templates). **NO new permission key** (R38, catalog stays **102**), **NO web/openapi change** (BE-only). **The sweep mirrors the 3a digest-sweep safety VERBATIM** (`services/notifications/escalation.py`): pure step-math in `timer.py::due_steps` (threshold-passed AND stamp-null, chronological, OVERDUE always-on at `due_at`); `process_task_timers` = a per-task `pg_advisory_xact_lock(hashtext(task_id))` → `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` + `populate_existing=True` [the S-drift-1 stale-attr trap] → per step: reminders/overdue via `resolve_recipients`, escalate via `resolve_escalation_recipients` (manager → QMS-Owner holders → []) + a `_recipient_for_user` builder + ONE `TASK_ESCALATED` `AuditEvent` (`actor_type=system`, `object_type=workflow_instance`, `scope_ref=task.id`, hashes NULL → the `audit.chain_link` Beat) + the stamp — **all in ONE per-task commit** (atomic stamp+enqueue+audit → idempotent under `task_acks_late` redelivery + concurrent sweeps); `sweep_task_timers` = a fresh session per task + per-task try/except. **N9 (locked): the sweep ONLY reminds/notifies/escalates — NO auto-decide, NO auto-reassign, NO task-state flip** (the `escalated_1_at` stamp is the only "already-escalated" marker). Wall-clock (the `working_calendar` business-day refinement is a documented R29 reconcile-defer; the offsets are INTERVAL so it slots in with no schema change). Beat `easysynq.notifications.timer_sweep` @300s (registered in `tasks/app.py` + a task-registration unit test). **Owner decisions (AskUserQuestion ×2, review-surfaced):** ONE pre-due reminder for the MVP (`remind_2_before` seeded NULL — a distinct second reminder is a named follow-up); WORKFLOW tasks only escalate (`escalate_1_after` NULL for personal `DOC_ACK` + `PERIODIC_REVIEW` — they get reminders/overdue but don't ping a manager).

⚠ **The 4-reviewer final whole-branch pass (migration-reviewer · diff-critic · opus · worker-safety) found two real bugs the per-task reviews' fixtures had MASKED:** (1) both pre-due reminders shared `event_key=task.due_soon`, so the notification dedup partial-unique `(recipient, task, event_key)` COLLAPSED the second (`ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` → no row, no email) yet the step still stamped → on the default seed `remind_2` DELIVERED NOTHING; the test had PRE-STAMPED `remind_2` (a false-PASS that hid it) → owner-resolved to the one-reminder MVP; (2) the seed escalated ALL 12 task types incl. personal `DOC_ACK`/`PERIODIC_REVIEW` to managers → owner-resolved to workflow-tasks-only. ⚠ **a CI-BLIND downgrade abort** (migration-reviewer + diff-critic): the downgrade `DELETE FROM notification_template` aborts on a POPULATED DB once the sweep has run (`notification.template_id` RESTRICT FK) — the fresh-DB round-trip is GREEN → fixed with a `NOT EXISTS` guard (the 0023 precedent). ⚠ worker-safety verified the 2-session `asyncio.gather` concurrency test would genuinely FAIL without the advisory lock (escalates exactly once). **Codex — 4 ROUNDS, 14 findings, ALL genuine + ALL fixed** (a migration+worker slice does NOT converge — the engineering-patterns rhythm; the owner chose to "merge at end of round 4"): **R1** (multi-org seed loop · cross-org manager → QM · no-stamp-on-template-miss · audit `escalated_to`=notified-only · re-upgrade-safe `ON CONFLICT` templates); **R2** (FREEZE the migration's task-types to a frozen tuple — a from-scratch replay with newer code would seed a future `TaskType` the DB enum lacks · stamp a no-recipient TERMINAL step via `should_stamp = notified or attempted==0`, else infinite re-claim · keep the IN-APP row for a no-email active recipient — only the email SEND needs an address · org-check the QM FALLBACK too, not just the manager); **R3** (reject a SELF-manager `manager_id==assignee.id` → QM · a DEDUP means the notification EXISTS — `_enqueue_one`'s dedup branch returns emitted, not a delivery-miss; only a template-miss retries — else infinite re-claim after a 0065 downgrade→re-upgrade drops/recreates the stamps); **R4** (write the `TASK_ESCALATED` audit ONLY for a genuinely-NEW escalation — `_enqueue_one`→a 3-state `created/deduped/no_template`; audit on `created_ids`, stamp on `exists_ids`, so a deduped re-sweep stamps WITHOUT a 2nd WORM audit row · correct `via=qm_fallback` for the self-manager-is-sole-QM edge). ⚠ **a CI-RED I introduced** (the R2-4 cross-org test): it created a 2nd `Organization` without cleanup → `test_restore.py`'s `select(Organization.id).scalar_one()` aborted `MultipleResultsFound` once the data-driven shard rebalance landed it after my test → fixed with FK-ordered org cleanup in a `finally` (the don't-pollute-the-shared-DB rule; the offending test is in OUR file, not `test_restore`).

**Live-smoke (BE-driven, slice 4 has no UI):** migration 0065 applied cleanly to the POPULATED dev DB (0064→0065 — the real upgrade CI's fresh DB can't prove); the per-type seed verified (12 policies, `remind_2` NULL all, `escalate` NULL only for DOC_ACK+PERIODIC_REVIEW, 1d for the 10 workflow types); a real `timer_sweep()` on a 2-day-overdue APPROVE task → `{tasks:1, steps:3}` → notifications `task.due_soon`+`task.overdue`→assignee, `task.escalated`→manager (templates SUBSTITUTED, no literal `{{}}` — the slice-3b `VARIABLE_WHITELIST` lesson, live), a `TASK_ESCALATED` audit (`via=manager`, `escalated_to`=[manager], notified-only), stamps remind1+overdue+escalated set (remind2 NOT); the 2nd sweep `{tasks:1, steps:0}` (idempotent, no dup notification/audit). 📌 **The live-smoke SHARPENED a deferral:** with `remind_2` unused, `remind_2_sent_at IS NULL` is a TAUTOLOGY in `_due_task_ids`'s OR-of-4 claim + the `ix_task_timer_pending` predicate → every open due task is re-claimed each sweep (a 0-step no-op; correctness-safe + bounded — this is the deferred Codex P2 "claim-threshold filter"; v1.x should drop the `remind_2` disjunct or remove the unused column). **Named residuals (not faked):** the **claim-threshold filter** (above) · `escalate_2` (reassign / NEEDS_ATTENTION) · `working_calendar` (business-day SLAs) · `capa.overdue` · the escalation/Health **UI + SSE (slice 5)** · the distinct **second reminder** · flipping the task state to `ESCALATED`. **Tests:** api unit **980→988** (+timer step-math + task-registration); +the `test_notification_timer_sweep` + `test_notification_escalation` integration suites (idempotency · the 2-session concurrency · no-email→in-app · no-recipient→stamped+no-reprocess · cross-org→filtered · self-manager→QM · dedup→stamped-no-2nd-audit · template-miss→no-stamp guard); web unchanged (**1261**). (S-notify-4, BE-only, migration **0065** [head `0064`→`0065`], api unit 980→988, web 1261, PR #276 squash `6c41c90`.)

### S-notify-3b — the preference matrix UI: per-class cadence + digest hour/timezone + quiet hours (slice 3b; FE-only; no migration [head `0064`]; PR #273 squash `9d03390`)

Puts the face on the 3a digest engine — `/settings/notifications` is rebuilt from the slice-2 master-email stopgap into the full **per-event-class email-cadence matrix**, consuming the already-shipped (S-notify-3a) `GET/PUT /me/notification-preferences`. **No migration (head stays `0064`), no new permission key (catalog `102`, authenticated-self), NO contract/openapi change (the 3a schemas already exist), NO `apps/api` change.** The page is one form (local working-state + a `dirty` diff + a single partial-PUT Save): an in-app-vs-email **banner** ("Your in-app bell is always immediate — these settings control email only"), the master email kill-switch + an "email off" note, **"Email cadence by type"** = 4 stacked class rows (name + helper text + an `Immediate/Daily/Off` SegmentedControl; `admin_ops` tagged "in-app only today"; distinct `aria-label`s; categorical NEUTRAL styling, never RAG), and **"Daily digest" timing** = a 24-slot hour Select, a curated-shortlist + searchable IANA timezone Select, and a both-or-neither quiet-hours Switch + two `TextInput type="time"` + a soft "digest hour falls in quiet hours" note. Data layer: widened `lib/types` (`NotificationDigestMode`/`NotificationClass`/`NotificationPreferences`/`…Update`), `useUpdateNotificationPreferences` (partial PUT, invalidate `["notification-preferences"]`), new `classMeta.ts` + `timezones.ts` helpers, and a `satisfies`-pinned + **stateful** MSW. **4 owner forks (AskUserQuestion ×4):** defer the admin pierce-flag toggle to its own slice (there is NO admin-config FE surface at all today — `grep notifications_email_enabled` over `apps/web` = zero; AdminShell has only Users/Roles/Processes → the toggle needs a net-new Config tab); stacked class rows + SegmentedControl; curated shortlist + searchable all-zones; top banner + per-row helper copy.

**Build + review:** subagent-driven (3 TDD tasks, fresh implementer + spec/quality review per task: helpers on haiku, the page on sonnet) + a **6-reviewer final whole-branch pass** (`diff-critic` · `web-test-trap` · opus whole-branch · a11y/DP-5 · gating-scope · MSW-fidelity) + 2 fix waves. ⚠ **THE bug the per-task tests MISSED, caught by the final pass (diff-critic, empirically) + verified LIVE: the curated timezone resting list was DEAD in production** — Mantine v7 drives a CONTROLLED `searchValue` to the selected option's label ("UTC") on mount, so `tzData` always took the search branch and the user never saw the ~12 curated zones at rest; the `timezones.test.ts` helper test passed in isolation (classic false-PASS). FIX = `onDropdownOpen={() => setTzSearch("")}` (open resets the search → `tzData` returns `restingZones`) + a rest-state test. ⚠ **a test-driven `onClick` + imperative `tzRef.current.value=""` hack** (added to stop `userEvent.type` appending) was caught + removed — the TEST does `user.clear(tz)` instead (the house rule: never alter a production component to pass a test). ⚠ **the save path was over-built** — a dead optimistic `qc.setQueryData(merged)` (its structural-sharing rationale didn't hold + it made the "Saved." test hollow) → reverted to the spec's invalidate-only + made the save tests STATEFUL (a `statefulPrefs` GET+PUT sharing `let current` so the refetch models production) + a post-save "stays checked" assertion. ⚠ **the "redundant" Switch `aria-label` finding was empirically REJECTED** — removing it breaks the accessible name (Mantine v7 folds the `description` into the label's text node → name becomes label+description verbose); the `aria-label` IS the concise accessible name, kept. ⚠ **live-smoke caught an ENV gap (NOT a 3b bug):** the owner's dev stack ran the pre-3a backend (DB `0063`, the old `{email_enabled}`-only API) → the page white-screened on the old response shape (`TypeError reading 'action_required'`) → fixed by rebuilding `api`/`worker`/`beat` + applying `0064`; then verified live (matrix → effective view; save → PUT 200 → persisted across a hard reload; the curated timezone dropdown + a non-curated search). **Codex round 1: 3 P2s, 2 fixed + 1 false-alarm:** P2 #1 the load-error gate (`prefs.isError` must be checked BEFORE `isLoading || !working`, else a failed GET spins forever — `working` stays null on error; FIX + a regression test); P2 #2 the bare prod `QueryClient` (`main.tsx`) → `refetchOnWindowFocus`/`Reconnect` default true → a focus refetch could clobber unsaved edits → disabled both on the prefs query (post-save invalidate still resets); **P2 #3 (timezone aliases) = FALSE ALARM, adversarially verified vs the running backend** — `zoneinfo.available_timezones()` = 599 zones and INCLUDES `Asia/Calcutta`/`Europe/Kiev`/`America/Buenos_Aires` (the Intl set ⊂ the backend set → no 422); all 3 threads replied + resolved.

**Named residuals (not faked):** the **admin pierce-flag tab** (`notifications_escalation_pierce_quiet_hours` + the org `notifications_email_enabled` need a net-new `config.update`-gated AdminShell Config tab — its own slice, alongside slice 4) · **slice 4** escalation timers (`SlaPolicy`/`working_calendar`/`timer_sweep`) → the `critical`-class events that exercise the quiet-hours pierce end-to-end · **slice 5** awareness events + the Health delivery-failure panel + SSE (replacing the 60s poll) · **hourly/weekly cadences** (enum-reserved, not added) · a **robustness gap**: the page has no error boundary / defensive guard against a malformed prefs response (white-screens the whole app — can't happen in prod since api+web ship together). **Tests:** web **1246→1261 (+15)** (classMeta 3 · timezones 3 · the rebuilt `NotificationSettingsPage` suite: cadence/master/error-gate/disabled-save + the timing 5 + the curated-rest-state test); api unchanged (FE-only). (S-notify-3b, FE-only, no migration [head `0064`], web 1246→1261, api 980, PR #273 squash `9d03390`.)

### S-notify-3a — the digest engine: preferences + digests + quiet hours (slice 3a; BE-only; migration 0064; PR #261 squash `93b8a57`)

**What shipped — the BE notification DIGEST ENGINE (doc 10 §9.4, R54): per-user per-event-class email cadence + a daily-digest Beat + quiet hours, running off seeded code defaults (the matrix UI is the deferred 3b slice).** Migration **0064** (additive, **NO new table** → 0010's `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES` GRANT trap doesn't fire → no REVOKE block), **NO new permission key** (reads stay authenticated-self, catalog **102**), contract = the widened `/me/notification-preferences` schema + a `NotificationDigestMode` enum + the admin `notifications_escalation_pierce_quiet_hours` flag. **Owner forks (AskUserQuestion ×4):** split BE-first (engine now, matrix UI = 3b) · per **event-class** matrix (a code map, NOT per-event-type) · **org-gated escalation pierce built now** (predicate unit-tested; exercised end-to-end once slice-4 `*.overdue` events fire) · cadences = **Immediate/Daily/Off** only in v1 (hourly/weekly reserved). **Schema (0064):** 2 enums (`notification_digest_mode`, `notification_email_kind`); `notification_preference` += 4 per-class mode columns (NULL ⇒ the class code default) + `digest_hour`/`timezone`/`quiet_start`/`quiet_end`; `notification` += `digest_due_at`/`digested_at` + a partial index `ix_notification_digest_pending` (Codex); `notification_email` += `email_kind`/`recipient_user_id`/`item_count` with `notification_id` now nullable (partial-unique `WHERE notification_id IS NOT NULL`); `system_config` += the pierce flag; seeds the `digest.daily` template. **Engine:** an event-class code map (`services/notifications/classes.py`) → `action_required`/`awareness`/`critical`/`admin_ops` (defaults daily/daily/immediate/immediate); class-aware enqueue (`dispatch.py`: `immediate` → email now, held to `window_end` in quiet hours unless a critical pierce; `daily` → set `digest_due_at`, NO immediate email; `off` → in-app only — the in-app row is ALWAYS created, the mode governs EMAIL only); the hourly `notification_digest_sweep` Beat (`digest.py`: bundle a user's due rows into ONE summary email, idempotent via a `digested_at` stamp in the same txn as the email insert, **a per-user `pg_advisory_xact_lock`** + `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED`, a fresh session per user [the MissingGreenlet guard], re-check eligibility at send-prep → stamp-without-email when ineligible; the existing `outbox_drain` sends it); `drain.py` resolves org/user from the email row's own columns for a digest (`notification_id IS NULL`) — sends, doesn't SUPPRESS, and `_emit_failure` uses a `digest:<id>` ref. **Fold-ins:** **DOC_ACK email switched on** (drop the slice-1 `subject_type != DOC_ACK` exclusion → bundled into the daily digest by the `action_required` default); **OBJ/MR subtype deep-link routing** (`subjects.py`: a DOCUMENT whose `document_type.code` is OBJ/MR → `/objectives/{id}` ÷ `/management-reviews/{id}` — both shared-PK subtypes — **after probing the satellite row exists**, else fall back to `/documents/{id}`). The preferences `GET` returns the effective view (NULL → code defaults); `PUT` is a partial, `model_fields_set`-driven, validated update (422 on bad class/mode/hour/timezone/time + value-level both-or-neither quiet hours).

⚠ **Behavior change (owner-confirmed, spec §13):** `action_required` defaults to **daily**, so `task.assigned` no longer emails immediately by default — the bell stays immediate, the email bundles into the daily digest (the §9.4 anti-overwhelm intent). Slice-1 regression tests were updated (opt a test user into IMMEDIATE, or assert `digest_due_at`); the obsolete unit DOC_ACK-suppression case was dropped. ⚠ **THE migration trap (CI-BLIND, caught by migration-reviewer + diff-critic, MISSED by the opus whole-branch + the Task-1 sonnet reviewer):** `op.create_check_constraint("ck_notification_preference_digest_hour", …)` passes the FULL name → the `ck_%(table_name)s_%(constraint_name)s` convention **re-tokenizes it into a DOUBLED, hash-truncated** `ck_notification_preference_ck_notification_preference_d_991e` ≠ the ORM's bare-token `ck_notification_preference_digest_hour`. `alembic check` does NOT compare CHECK names + the up↔down round-trip is wrong-both-ways → **GREEN despite the bug**; only a live `pg_constraint` query surfaces it. Fix = the **bare token** `"digest_hour"` in BOTH create + drop (matching the ORM). ⚠ **a migration-managed partial index** (the new `ix_notification_digest_pending` + the existing `uq_notification_email_one_per_notification`) must be in `env.py`'s `_MIGRATION_MANAGED_INDEXES` AND absent from the ORM model (the `uq_notification_dedup_task` precedent). ⚠ **a digest's `notification_id` is NULL** → `_still_eligible`/`_emit_failure` must resolve org/user from the email row, not `session.get(Notification, None)` (else the digest is wrongly SUPPRESSED). ⚠ **concurrent sweeps can SKIP-LOCKED-SPLIT one user's rows** → each sends a digest (sequential idempotency held, concurrent did NOT) → a per-user advisory lock serializes them. ⚠ **the prior OBJ/MR routing tests were FALSE-PASSING** — they created OBJ/MR docs via `POST /documents` (which never seeds the satellite) → they asserted the dedicated route on orphans the whole time; the satellite probe forced seeding the satellites directly + an orphan-fallback test.

**Build + review:** subagent-driven (10 tasks, fresh implementer + spec/quality review per task; 5 pure helpers on haiku, the integration/API tasks on sonnet) + a 3-way final whole-branch review (opus cross-task-coherence + `diff-critic` + `migration-reviewer`) that caught **2 real defects** (the CI-blind CHECK name; a stale DOC_ACK test passing only incidentally) — both fixed + verified (live `pg_constraint` = the single name). **Codex: 2 rounds, 7 P2s, ALL genuine + ALL fixed** (r1: one-sided quiet-hour update, the missing sweep index, the first-write upsert race, a blank-display-name `IndexError` aborting the whole sweep; r2: empty-string quiet hours, the OBJ/MR orphan-reroute 404, the concurrent-sweep double-send) — each re-verified by diff-critic/migration-reviewer + replied/resolved on-thread; no defer, no loop (every round surfaced real issues). **Named residuals (not faked):** **S-notify-3b** (the per-class matrix UI on `/settings/notifications`) · **hourly/weekly cadences** (enum-reserved) · **slice 4** (`SlaPolicy`/`working_calendar`/escalation events → the `critical` class + end-to-end pierce) · **slice 5** (awareness-event emission + the Health delivery-failure panel + SSE) · the dead `Recipient.email_enabled` re-read (a harmless 2-file cleanup) · an MR-orphan-fallback test (symmetric to the shipped OBJ one). ⚠ A pre-existing `-k "notification or config"` batch `test_setup.py::test_configure_auth_*` ordering flake reproduces on `main` (CI shards apart) — NOT this slice. **Tests:** api unit **956→980 (+24)** (classes 6 · preferences 2 · quiet 6 · schedule 4 · digest-render 2 · subtype-deeplink 3 · task-registration +1, minus the dropped DOC_ACK unit case) + new integration (`test_notification_digest.py` enqueue/sweep/drain/concurrency, `test_notification_preferences_api.py` ×~16, `test_notification_subtype_routing.py` OBJ/MR/plain/orphan); web unchanged (**1246**). **R53 was backfilled into the decisions-register with R54** (S-notify-1 recorded it only in its spec §13). (S-notify-3a, BE-only, migration **0064** [head 0063→0064], api unit 956→980, web 1246, PR #261 squash `93b8a57`.)

### S-deeplink-login — preserve the requested path through the Keycloak login round-trip (FE-only; PR #259 squash `61dc442`)

**What shipped — closes the Codex #257 P2 (the named Notification-track follow-up): a logged-out deep-link now lands on its route after sign-in, not Home. FE-only** (`apps/web/src/lib/auth.tsx` + its test): no migration (head stays `0063`), no new permission key (catalog 102), no contract change, **no Keycloak-realm change** — `redirect_uri` stays `${origin}/`; the path rides the OIDC `state`, which the oidc-client-ts *stateStore* already round-trips across the full-page redirect (only the *userStore* is in-memory; that's why PKCE works today). The SPA holds tokens in memory, so a logged-out open of any deep route auto-`login()`d through Keycloak — but `login()` was a bare `signinRedirect()` and the callback restored via `replaceState(window.location.pathname)` (= `/` at callback time) → the email `prefs_link` (`/settings/notifications`) + every notification-email deep-link landed on **Home**. Fix: `login()` stashes `window.location.pathname + window.location.search` in the OIDC **`state.returnTo`**; the `signinRedirectCallback` handler restores it via react-router `navigate(safeReturnTo(user.state.returnTo), {replace:true})` (also strips `?code&state`); **`safeReturnTo`** is an open-redirect guard accepting ONLY a same-origin absolute path (`//host`, absolute URLs, `/\`, non-strings → `/`; navigation is via react-router, never `window.location` → defense-in-depth). The `catch` branch is unchanged (a failed callback still strips the query + falls through logged-out — never wedges sign-in); `setReady(true)` is always reached.

⚠ **Traps (load-bearing):** (1) **the bootstrap `useEffect` must stay once-on-mount** — the initial `[navigate]` dep re-ran it on EVERY in-app navigation (react-router's `useNavigate` returns a function whose identity changes per pathname → redundant `getUser()` + AuthContext value churn across every consumer); fix = a `navRef` latest-ref (`const navRef = useRef(navigate); navRef.current = navigate;`, call `navRef.current(...)` in the effect) + `[]` deps. **`exhaustive-deps` is NOT enforced in this repo** (no `eslint-plugin-react-hooks` in `eslint.config.js`), so `[]` is lint-clean — do NOT add `[navigate]`. The whole-branch (opus) review caught this; a regression test confirms it (navigate once → `getUser` stays at 1 call; the test FAILS 2-vs-1 against the old `[navigate]`). (2) **the login path is load-bearing — the unit tests (MemoryRouter) CANNOT exercise the real `BrowserRouter` + Keycloak round-trip; the LIVE re-login is the gate** (verified live: `/settings/notifications` + `/risks` deep-loads land on-route via a silent SSO round-trip; `/` lands Home — no regression to normal login). (3) react-router `navigate` itself collapses an off-origin value to a same-origin path (`//evil.com`→`/evil.com`), so `safeReturnTo` is belt-and-suspenders, not the sole boundary.

**Build + review:** subagent-driven (Task 1 the `safeReturnTo` pure guard · Task 2 the `login()`/callback wiring + the vi.mock tests · Task 3 gate+review), fresh implementer + spec/quality review per task; a fix wave for the opus Important (the `navRef`) + 2 safety tests. `diff-critic` **CLEAN**, whole-branch (opus) **Ready-to-merge** (its lone Important fixed), the fix re-review **Approved**; full `/check-web` green; the live re-login passed (owner Keycloak login). **No named residuals** — the slice is self-contained. **Tests:** web **1238→1246 (+8)** (`safeReturnTo` ×3, login-capture, callback-restore, guard-applied, catch-path fall-through, no-refetch-on-navigation regression); api unchanged (**956**). (S-deeplink-login, FE-only, no migration [head `0063`], web 1238→1246, api 956, PR #259 squash `61dc442`.)

### S-notify-fe — the SPA notification bell + center (slice 2; FE-only; PR #257 squash `6893c3e`)

**What shipped — the in-app awareness UI for the slice-1 spine, FE-only:** no migration (head stays `0063`), no new permission key (catalog stays **102** — the reads are authenticated-self, so the SPA adds ZERO gating beyond signed-in), no contract change (the endpoints were already documented in S-notify-1's `openapi.yaml`). A new `apps/web/src/features/notifications/` dir consuming the existing self-scoped endpoints:
- `deepLink.ts` — a pure `toRoutePath` relativising the **absolute** `deep_link` (`app_base_url`+fragment) → `pathname+search`, with a `/tasks` parse-failure fallback; navigated **in-app** via react-router (no open-redirect surface).
- `hooks.ts` — `useNotificationCount` (the badge — the ONLY polled query, `refetchInterval 60_000`, `unread_only=true&limit=100`, mirrors `useAckCount`'s **never-confident-zero** [count read only behind `isError`]); `useNotifications("recent"|"all", enabled)` (popover gated `enabled: opened`); `useNotificationPreferences`.
- `mutations.ts` — `useMarkRead`/`useMarkAllRead` invalidate the `["notifications"]` prefix (badge + lists refresh together); `useSetEmailEnabled` invalidates `["notification-preferences"]`; **no optimistic updates**.
- `NotificationItem` — one row: unread = a **dot glyph + a `VisuallyHidden "Unread"` + bold title** (never colour alone, DP-5); the row is a `Link` with **NO explicit aria-label** (so the nested "Unread" isn't swallowed by the ARIA name computation); the "Mark read" `ActionIcon` is a **SIBLING** of the Link (no nested-interactive); body rendered as a **text node** (XSS-safe, no `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`).
- `NotificationBell` — the merged TopBar bell: an `Indicator`-wrapped `ActionIcon` (badge three-state — numeric / gray indeterminate dot on a failed count / nothing on a true zero; "99+" cap) opening a `Popover` (recent 15 + Mark-all-read / Notification settings / See all).
- `NotificationsPage` (`/notifications`) — full list (50), Mark-all-read, calm `lib/states`, a "showing the 50 most recent" honesty footnote.
- `NotificationSettingsPage` (`/settings/notifications`) — the minimal master email toggle on `GET/PUT /me/notification-preferences`, **un-breaking the email `prefs_link`** slice 1 left dangling.
- Shell wiring: `TopBar` swaps the standalone ack-count `Indicator` for `<NotificationBell/>` (the **Tasks** icon stays the WORK entry; `useAckCount` is **KEPT** — Home's `DoCard` still imports it) + an Account-menu "Notification settings" item; `App.tsx` +2 routes under the AppShell layout.

**Owner decisions (AskUserQuestion ×4):** **merge into one bell** (the ack-count badge is retired — DOC_ACK assignments now flow as notifications, so the one bell's unread badge encompasses new-ack awareness; the durable open-ack work-count stays at `/tasks`) · **popover + full page** · **ship the minimal master-email-toggle now** · **60s poll + refetch on open**.

⚠ **Traps carried (load-bearing):** (1) **the strict-`tsc` trap** — `HttpResponse.json(body)` where `body: unknown` fails the full `/check-web` `tsc` gate (`JsonBodyType`) but a **per-file `vitest` run is GREEN** (the classic blind spot); cast `body as Record<string, unknown>`. (2) A Mantine `Menu`/`Popover` opened in a test needs `userEvent.setup()` + an **async** `findByRole("menuitem", …)` (the ingestion-test idiom) — do **NOT** add `transitionProps={{ duration: 0 }}` to the **production** component to force a test green (caught + reverted in review). (3) The count query uses `limit=100`, so the badge shows "99+" only at ≥100 unread (cosmetic; spec §5.1 said 99). (4) A new routed page needs a jest-axe smoke (24/28 page-tests carry one — added in the review fix wave).

**Build + review:** subagent-driven (7 impl tasks + a test-coverage fix wave), fresh implementer + spec/quality review per task; **whole-branch (opus) = Ready-to-merge**, `diff-critic` + `web-test-trap-reviewer` **CLEAN** (0 Critical/Important). **Live-smoke (Chrome MCP, owner login, org AHT):** the core loop verified end-to-end against the running stack — badge (incl. a **REAL** `task.assigned` notification, the IPR-GEN-001 approval, rendered alongside seeded rows), popover unread/read distinction, deep-link click → mark-read + **navigate to a distinct route** (`/risks`) + badge decrement (DB-persisted), mark-all-read → silent-zero (DB unread=0), the settings toggle → "Saved." (DB `email_enabled=false`), ErrorState-with-retry on token expiry, silent SSO re-auth. The `/notifications` page + the Account-menu item were **covered-by-tests-only** (the documented Mantine-portal Chrome-MCP flakiness — menus/popovers focus but don't reliably open under automation); the `/settings/notifications` route itself WAS reached live via the popover footer link.

**Codex (1 P2, owner-DEFERRED — not faked):** the SPA **loses the requested path through the Keycloak login round-trip** (`redirect_uri=${origin}/`, bare `signinRedirect`, callback `replaceState`→`/`) → a logged-out open of `/settings/notifications` or ANY notification-email deep-link lands on **Home** (so fork-3's `prefs_link` goal + all email deep-links are only half-realized). Confirmed valid end-to-end; deferred to a focused **S-deeplink-login** follow-up (a cross-cutting shared-`AuthProvider` change — benefits the `prefs_link` + every notification deep-link + bookmarks, out of this FE-only slice's scope). Spec drafted: `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-22-s-deeplink-login-design.md` (stash `pathname+search` in the OIDC `state`, `navigate(returnTo, {replace:true})` after `signinRedirectCallback`, same-origin `startsWith("/")` open-redirect guard + an auth test). Replied + resolved on the PR thread.

**Named residuals (not faked):** **S-deeplink-login** (the Codex P2, above) · **objective/MR subtype deep-link routing** in `subjects.py` (a small BE follow-up; `/documents/{id}` is correct + reachable today) · the **digest matrix + quiet hours + DOC_ACK email** (slice 3) · **SSE** replacing the 60s poll (slice 5-ish) · the **retired header ack-work-count** (an intentional consequence of the merge). **Tests:** web **1210→1238 (+28)** (deepLink 4 · hooks 8 · NotificationItem 5 · NotificationBell 6 · NotificationsPage 3 · NotificationSettingsPage 3, minus the rewritten TopBar suite's net); api unchanged (**956**). (S-notify-fe, FE-only, no migration [head `0063`], web 1210→1238, api 956, PR #257 squash `6893c3e`.)

### S-notify-1 — the BE notification spine + email delivery (R53; migration 0063; BE-only; PR #255 squash `766dc55`)

**What shipped — a transactional-outbox notification spine, BE-only (no SPA).** `migration 0063` (head
`0062→0063`) creates **4 operational/mutable tables** (`notification` in-app durable · `notification_email`
the email delivery ledger · `notification_template` versioned+seeded · `notification_preference` the
per-user toggle), a fresh `notification_email_status` enum, the per-org `system_config.notifications_email_enabled`
opt-in flag, and **2 seeded `en` templates** (`task.assigned` + `system.email_delivery_failed`). A new
`services/notifications/` package: `render` (a **logic-free, HTML-escaped, whitelisted** renderer — `{{var}}`
+ `{{var|date}}`, **no eval/Jinja**, single `re.sub` pass so an injected value can't re-expand) · `subjects`
(polymorphic resolver + deep links, 7 subject types + a `/tasks` fallback) · `recipients` · `dispatch` (the
**SAVEPOINT enqueue**) · `mail` (a `MailSender` protocol + `aiosmtplib` `SmtpMailSender` + a test fake — the
`LoggingRenderSink`/`GotenbergRenderSink` split: the api never sends) · `drain` (the worker core) · `admins`.
The `outbox_drain` **Beat task** (120s). Self-scoped `GET /notifications` + mark-read + `read-all` +
`GET/PUT /me/notification-preferences`; the admin opt-in flag rides the existing `config.update`-gated
`/admin/config` (audited `CONFIG_UPDATED`). OpenAPI updated. **NO new permission key** (R38; catalog stays
102 — reads are authenticated-self, the `GET /tasks` posture). **NO WORM touch** (the 4 tables are
operational like `task` — no hash chain, no `signature_event`, no blob bytes).

**The load-bearing contract (spec §4, the crux).** Enqueue runs **inside the caller's task-creation txn under
a SAVEPOINT** (`begin_nested()`): atomic-on-success, and ANY failure (missing template, render bug) rolls
back ONLY the savepoint + logs → the **parent task txn is untouched, so a notification bug can never block a
workflow transition**. The in-app row inserts via `pg_insert(...).on_conflict_do_nothing(index_elements,
index_where="task_id IS NOT NULL").returning(id)` (the dedup partial index — the ON CONFLICT needs
`index_where` to match it); the email row inserts **only if the notification returned a new id** (a dedup hit
→ no orphan). **Send is the async drain**: it **claims ONE row at a time** (`SELECT … LIMIT 1 FOR UPDATE SKIP
LOCKED` per iteration — the lock is held until *its own* lease commits, so no sibling-lock-release
double-send), re-checks eligibility at send (org flag + recipient active + opt-out + `smtp_host` →
`SUPPRESSED` for a mid-window change), then a **count-before-send lease** (`attempts++` + a `next_attempt_at`
backoff + commit BEFORE the SMTP call, so a post-send crash can't loop unboundedly); on exhaustion → `FAILED`
(durable BEFORE the best-effort emit) + a **`system.email_delivery_failed`** in-app notification to admins
(operational-only body — NO subject title/identifier, since admins hold no `document.read`; R32). **Email is
opt-in per org (default OFF)** and carries **summary + deep link only — never controlled content** (the
deep_link resolves back into the vault). **DB-backed versioned templates**; the producing template
id+version is snapshotted per message.

**`task.assigned` wired at all 6 task-creation sites.** The engine `_materialize_stage` enqueues per-task
after its flush but **skips `DOC_ACK`/`PERIODIC_REVIEW`** — those two sweeps patch `due_at` AFTER
materialization, so they re-notify post-patch (else the email shows `Due: (none)`); the 3 direct-add sites
(`instantiate_approval`, MR cadence, MR-action spawn) enqueue inline. **DOC_ACK email is deferred to slice 3**
(in-app only now — a `subject_type` gate at the email-enqueue; avoids an onboarding email flood with no
digest yet). The welded single-stage `test_approval` stayed green (12/12). Recipients = assignee else each
pool member, **org-scoped + active-only**.

**R53 (binding) recorded** + **doc 10 W2/§156 reconciled** — the in-txn SAVEPOINT outbox **supersedes** the
older "enqueue side-effects after commit" wording (it closes the commit→enqueue crash gap; still
non-blocking). Reads add **no new permission key**.

⚠ **Traps a future session must carry.** (1) **`0010`'s `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES … GRANT … DELETE` grants the
app role ALL DML on EVERY new table** → an explicit `GRANT` block is a no-op; to enforce the intended posture
you must **`REVOKE`** (ledgers `REVOKE DELETE`; `notification_template` `REVOKE INSERT,UPDATE,DELETE` →
SELECT-only). The migration-reviewer "confirmed SELECT-only grants" in the first pass — but that was only the
explicit grants; the default-privileges override was caught by **Codex**. (2) The empty-`smtp_host` →
`SUPPRESSED` short-circuit (added so an org that enables email without configuring SMTP doesn't storm FAILED
rows) **broke 3 `test_notification_e2e` drain tests in CI** (CI has no `SMTP_HOST`) — while a **local `.env`
with `SMTP_HOST=mailpit` MASKED it** (the e2e tests called `drain_once(…, get_settings(), …)`; the sibling
`test_notification_drain` had been updated to a `_configured_settings()` helper, the e2e file was missed).
**Lesson: a settings-dependent test must pin the setting, not read the ambient env; re-run the WHOLE touched
suite after a fix, and reproduce CI by unsetting the env (`env -u SMTP_HOST`).** (3) The drain's original
**batch `LIMIT N` claim + per-row commit released sibling `FOR UPDATE` locks** → an overlapping drain
(runtime > 120s beat) could double-send a sibling — flagged by THREE reviewers (Task-8/opus/Codex) before
being fixed (claim-one-row). (4) Email **header CR/LF** in a rendered subject raises `ValueError` → the drain
mis-handles it as transient → false `FAILED` → fold CR/LF (`_header_safe`).

**Process.** Spec-first under `docs/superpowers/specs/` + a **5-lens pre-code refute panel** that killed 6
design flaws before any migration (unbounded-resend, an admin-metadata leak, the polymorphic-hook scope, the
post-flush `due_at`, the DOC_ACK flood, the canon-timing reconciliation). **13-task subagent-driven build**
(`docs/superpowers/plans/`), each spec+quality reviewed; final reviews migration-reviewer + diff-critic +
opus whole-branch all CLEAN (the opus review's lone "Important" — a `cadence.py` missing flush —
**empirically refuted** by the diff-critic: SQLAlchemy restores a parent-pending object after a savepoint
rollback). **Live-smoke** on the rebuilt image: the real `aiosmtplib`→Mailpit delivery verified (`SENT`,
the rendered email with `|date` + deep link, no controlled content). **2 Codex rounds, 9 findings → 7 fixed
(both P1s round 1: claim-one-row drain + the REVOKE; round 2: recipients org-scope + the CR/LF fold; +
inactive filter + at-send opt-out re-check), 2 deferred** (the `prefs_link` `/settings/notifications` route →
slice 3; objective/MR subtype deep-link routing → a UX refinement, the generic `/documents/{id}` is reachable
by the approval recipient who holds `document.*`).

**Named residuals (not faked):** slices 2–5 (above); the deferred objective/MR **subtype deep-link routing**;
the **`prefs_link`** route (slice 3); the informational **INVITED-not-in-`_INACTIVE`** note (a faithful mirror
of `auth/dependencies.py` — an INVITED account could be emailed; reconciled to ACTIVE on first login).

(S-notify-1, BE-only, migration **0063** [head 0062→0063], api unit **952→956** [+4 mail header-fold tests; +
notification unit across the slice] + many notification integration/e2e, web unchanged, PR #255 squash `766dc55`.)

## REGISTER STEWARD ROLE — the reserved role making the three register-steward consoles self-service (R52; migration 0062)

> Closes the **F-1 deferral** named across R49/R50/R51: the in-app register-steward consoles (Risk 6.1 / Context 4.1 / Interested Parties 4.2) shipped FE-only (S-risk-5 · S-context-fe · S-interested-parties-fe) gating on the SERVER-computed `register_capabilities`, but their lifecycle acts (start-revision / publish / **release**) were exercisable **only via a SYSTEM override** in v1. This seeds a dedicated reserved role so stewardship is self-service end-to-end — a cross-cutting authz capstone serving all three register families.

**S-register-steward = a reserved `Register Steward` role (R52; migration 0062 [head 0061→0062]; BE-only).** The role holds the full stewardship set at **SYSTEM** scope — `register.read · register.manage · document.release · document.read · document.read_draft` — and deliberately **EXCLUDES `document.approve`** (SoD: the approver stays a separate Approver/QMS-Owner; register publish still routes its approval to that pool, and release stays releaser ≠ approver). **It is the FIRST seeded role to hold `document.release`** → v1 release authority becomes **role-grantable**, not SYSTEM-override-only (R52). **NO new permission key** (catalog stays 102; R38-additive covers a new role + grants on existing keys), **NO contract change, NO FE change** — the consoles already gate their Publish/Start-revision/Release affordances on the server-computed `register_capabilities`, so the role lights up the affordances automatically + auto-appears in `GET /roles` for an admin to assign. ⚠ **THE reframe a future session must carry: `register.manage` was ALREADY seeded to QMS Owner @ SYSTEM (`0004` line 185) — so start-revision/publish already worked for a QMS-Owner user; the genuine gap was `document.release`, granted to NO seeded role (`seed_personas.py` says it outright) → release of EVERY document (normal docs, POL/OBJ/MR, the register heads) is SYSTEM-override-only by deliberate v1 posture. The slice's substance is therefore role-grantable RELEASE authority, not register.manage.** ⚠ **Migration trap: the seed MUST use the resilient name-agnostic org lookup (`SELECT id FROM organization` → the sole org, D1) — NOT `0004`'s bare `WHERE short_code='DEFAULT'` `scalar_one()`, which aborts on a renamed OPERATIONAL install (this install: `AHT`; `services/common/org.py` + the 0053/0054/0057 resilient-lookup precedent).** Data-only (no DDL / no ORM change → `alembic check` clean); idempotent `on_conflict_do_nothing` on `(org_id, name)` / `(org_id, role_id, permission_id)` (the live UNIQUE constraints); downgrade deletes the steward's `role_assignment` → `role_grant` → `role` (both FKs to `role.id` are `ondelete=RESTRICT`), scoped by name — the migration-reviewer **empirically round-tripped this on a live PG16 incl. the CI-blind populated-DB downgrade [attached a real `role_assignment`, downgrade EXIT 0, `permission` held 102→102, the 8 starter roles intact] + the renamed-`AHT`-org path.** **4 owner decisions (AskUserQuestion ×4): next slice = this; release authority = a NEW dedicated role (over extending QMS Owner — which conflates approve+release and collides with the approval stage — or a narrow new `register.release` key — R38 catalog-open + a backend gate change across the 3 release endpoints); the FULL stewardship key set; record as binding R52 + a spec.** **Tests (all integration, testcontainer PG16): `test_authz` seed assertion (the exact 10-role set [+ Register Steward] + the steward grant map [5 keys @ SYSTEM via exact-equality, no `document.approve`]; catalog stays 102); a role-ONLY Risk lifecycle end-to-end in `test_risk_lifecycle` (`s5.grant_role` only, NO `_grant` override → publish → a SEPARATE Approver approves → a third-party steward releases → Effective; the steward is 403 self-approving [role excludes `document.approve`]; SoD-2 gives the author-steward `can_release:false` while the third-party steward releaser gets `true`); a new `test_register_steward_role.py` (the role reaches CTX/IP `can_manage`; + the LEADERSHIP NON-REGRESSION — a role-only steward releasing an Approved OBJ with the flag ON is still `409 leadership_authorization_required`, asserted by the EXACT code [a generic non-200 would false-pass a 403] with the flag reset in `finally`, proving `document.release @ SYSTEM` does NOT bypass the Top-Management gate).** ⚠ **Authz facts proven end-to-end (diff-critic + the whole-branch review traced these): the approval candidate pool is resolved by ROLE NAME (the workflow stage `assignees.roles`), so excluding `document.approve` genuinely keeps the steward out of the pool; SoD-2 is an app-level overlay independent of the grant (the author-steward computes `can_release:false`); the leadership preflight runs inside `_cutover` AFTER the `enforce(document.release)`, so a role-only releaser passes authz but is blocked by the gate.** **Named-not-faked deferrals: a narrow `register.release` key (least-privilege — the owner chose the role-grant lane); NO 9th persona / `seed-personas` steward (the role is left for an admin to assign — the live-smoke assigns it to a fresh user).** Built via **subagent-driven development** (5 tasks, each implement → spec+quality review → fix-loop; 1 Important docs finding [the new `docs/14 §3.1` roster omitted Top Management] fixed-forward to all 10 roles). diff-critic + migration-reviewer + a whole-branch senior review **ALL CLEAN** (0 Critical/Important); full `/check-api` green (925 unit). (S-register-steward, BE-only, migration **0062** [head 0061→0062], api unit unchanged [925], +1 integration assertion [`test_authz`] / +1 integration test [`test_risk_lifecycle`] / +2 integration tests [new `test_register_steward_role.py`], web unchanged [~1210], PR #253 squash `284d6e1`.)

## INTERESTED PARTIES REGISTER — clause 4.2 Needs & expectations of interested parties (the THIRD register family; R51; migration 0061)

> The third "register" family and the second half of clause 4 "Context of the organization" — reusing R49/R50's register-as-Document pattern **verbatim** (a near-byte-identical clone of the Context register, the simpler categorical sibling of Risk). SPEC-LIGHTER than S-risk-spec (the architecture is settled) — owner decisions surfaced via AskUserQuestion before code. **Org-level, NOT process-scoped** (clause 4.2 interested parties are strategic/org-wide; the Context divergence from risk). **Core + lifecycle (S-interested-parties-1) + the read consumers (S-interested-parties-2 — the `GET /summary` governing read + the MR 9.3.2(b) consumer sourcing BOTH the 4.1 + 4.2 halves, finally closing the `CONTEXT_CHANGES` sourceless gap S-context-2 carried here) are now SHIPPED; **S-interested-parties-fe ships the SPA → R51 is COMPLETE end-to-end (core · lifecycle · the governing summary + MR consumer · the SPA + steward console).**

- **S-interested-parties-fe** (the `/interested-parties` SPA — the LAST register-family residual; **with it R51 / clause-4.2 Interested Parties is COMPLETE end-to-end**; FE-only, a verbatim clone of `features/context/` adapted to the 4.2 content model) — **the register page + a 7-card party-type BOARD + scorecard + drawer + New/Edit modals + the `RegisterLifecyclePanel` steward console + a Home PLAN line + the `/interested-parties` route + an ungated LeftRail entry.** **What shipped (FE-ONLY — NO migration [head stays `0061`], NO new permission key [rides `register.read`/`register.manage`/`document.release`, catalog 102], NO contract change — every schema [`InterestedParty`, `InterestedPartyRegisterStatus` incl. the optional `can_release`/`can_manage`, `InterestedPartyRegisterSummary`, the create/update/publish bodies] already shipped in S-interested-parties-1/-2's `openapi.yaml`):** (1) **`features/interested-parties/`** mirroring `features/context/`: `InterestedPartiesRegisterPage` (the register-triage toolbar + party_type/influence/status filters + the `?party=` drawer wiring synced to the param's REMOVAL + a `New party` button gated on the SERVER `can_manage` × head-editability + a state-correct read-only banner that does NOT instruct the steward action [the S-risk-4b banner-copy trap]); **`InterestedPartyTypeBoard`** (the clause-4.2 viz analogue of context's SWOT board / risk's 5×5 matrix — the owner-chosen **party-type BOARD**: the live working rows bucketed by `party_type` into the 7 FIXED ISO-4.2-spine cards [customer…partner], `board.ts` `PARTY_TYPE_ORDER` + `bucketByPartyType` golden-pinned; **NO "uncategorized"/overflow strip** [party_type is NOT NULL → every row buckets]; an empty card renders "None recorded." [a completeness prompt, the SWOT fixed-frame analogue]); `InterestedPartyScorecardBand` (the CLIENT-side working-view rollup — active/total + the high/medium/low/unspecified influence distribution + never-reviewed amber); `InterestedPartyDrawer` (NO CAPA seam — clause 4.2 has no treatment axis; shows party_type/influence/status badges + `party_name` + `needs_expectations` + last-reviewed + Edit); `New`/`EditPartyModal` (a 7-way `party_type` Select [NOT a SegmentedControl] + `party_name` TextInput + `needs_expectations` Textarea + a clearable ordered `influence` Select + native `type=date`; partial PATCH — omitted ≠ null, explicit null clears influence/last_reviewed_at); `RegisterLifecyclePanel` + `PublishRegisterModal` (the steward console — start-revision/publish/release gated STATE × the SERVER `can_manage`/`can_release` caps; approve/decide rides the existing `/tasks` DOCUMENT arm, ZERO new FE). (2) **The influence encoding** (the one genuinely-new design call): `influence` is an ORDERED 3-level + unspecified axis, NOT a RAG alarm (a high-influence party is not a "problem") → NOT mapped onto the danger/warning RAG tones; a colour-blind-safe **filled/half/empty ordinal glyph ramp `●◐○`** (distinct from the canonical RAG set `✓◔✕●○★`) carries the magnitude, the LABEL carries the level, the tone stays calm (info for high, neutral else); the null case is a dimmed `·` + "Unspecified". (3) **Wiring**: the `lib/types.ts` `InterestedParty*` block; the `/interested-parties` route; an **UNGATED** LeftRail PLAN entry (filter-not-403, the risk/context precedent — a PROCESS-scoped reader still sees the link); the Home PLAN line (`useInterestedPartySummary` → `N active interested parties` [neutral] + `N never reviewed` [amber when >0, drives the RAG], the S-context-fe pattern, folded into `PlanCard.allForbidden` + `useHomeAsOf`); the MSW fixtures + handlers (static `/summary` + `/register*` before `/:id`, **pinned via `satisfies`** to the real `_interested_party`/`_register_status`/`summarize_register` shapes). **3 owner decisions (AskUserQuestion ×3):** (D-1) **viz = the party-type BOARD (7 cards)** — group by the ISO-4.2 spine, influence per chip (vs an influence-banded view / a table-only view); (D-2) **one slice** (full SPA incl. the steward console — the backend is fully ready, unlike risk's 4b→5 split; the S-context-fe precedent); (D-3) **Home line = active + never-reviewed amber** (mirror context, NOT a high-influence headline — influence is relevance, not an alarm). **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry (all carried from S-context-fe + verified clean):** (1) **the DP-5 aria-label fold** — the board chip's explicit `aria-label` OVERRIDES descendant content per the ARIA name computation, so a nested influence/Closed badge is SWALLOWED → the name MUST fold party_type + influence + `(closed)` (`"{Party type}: {party_name} — {influence_label}{ (closed)}"`) or the signal strands as glyph/strikethrough/colour ALONE (the `axe`-invisible WCAG break); (2) **distinct accessible names** — the filter `Select aria-label="Filter by party type"` ≠ the modal's `"Party type"`; the two SegmentedControls share an "All" radio (never query it); the board chip name (type-prefixed) ≠ the table anchor (plain `party_name`); (3) **influence sorts by RANK not alphabetically** (a numeric `INFLUENCE_RANK` low<med<high, nulls last — `sortRows` compares numbers numerically); (4) the MSW fixtures pinned via `satisfies` to the REAL serializer (the #1 false-PASS — `by_influence` carries an `unspecified` bucket, `by_party_type` all 7 spine keys, influence nullable); (5) every new test file `import { expect, it } from "vitest"` (the bare global is jest-typed → tsc-only catch); (6) the orthogonal-read trap — BOTH the PlanCard all-forbidden AND the HomePage bare-demo test gain a `/interested-parties/summary` 403 (else the default 200 fixture renders the IP line and `allForbidden` is never exercised). **Reviews:** diff-critic CLEAN (line-by-line vs the context template + the serializer + openapi) + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN (every trap in the catalog) + a 3-lens adversarial Workflow (FE-gating/deny-wins · a11y/colour-safe-RAG · read-of-record-vs-working-view) → **0 raw findings (nothing even to verify)**; ## CONTEXT REGISTER — clause 4.1 Understanding the organization & its context (the SECOND register family; R50; migration 0060)

> The second "register" family, reusing R49's register-as-Document pattern verbatim (the first reuse the pattern was explicitly set for). SPEC-LIGHTER than S-risk-spec (the architecture is settled) — 4 owner decisions surfaced via AskUserQuestion before code. **Org-level, NOT process-scoped** (clause 4.1 context is strategic/org-wide; the deliberate divergence from risk, matching the doc-14 §6 contract that omits `process_id` on `context_issue`). **Now COMPLETE end-to-end** — core+lifecycle (S-context-1) · the governing-summary read consumer (S-context-2) · the SPA + steward console (S-context-fe). The clause-4.2 Interested Parties register (R51) core+lifecycle now ships as **S-interested-parties-1** (its own family section above); the remaining context-adjacent residual is **S-interested-parties-2** (the MR 9.3.2(b) input wired sourcing both the 4.1 + 4.2 governing summaries — `CONTEXT_CHANGES` stays a sourceless gap until then).

- **S-context-fe** (the Context register SPA — the LAST clause-4.1 slice → the family is now COMPLETE end-to-end; BE+FE, mirrors the S-risk-4b SPA + the S-risk-5 steward console verbatim) — **the web SPA the register lacked, plus the carried server-computed `can_release`/`can_manage` capability residual on `GET /context/register` AND (parity) `GET /risks/register`.** **What shipped (NO migration [head stays `0060`], NO new permission key [rides `register.read`/`register.manage`/`document.release`, catalog 102]; contract = optional `can_release`/`can_manage` on the byte-identical `ContextRegisterStatus` + `RiskRegisterStatus` openapi twins):** **Part A (BE)** — a NEW shared `services/authz/register_caps.register_capabilities(session, caller, *, release_scope, source_ip)` computes `can_manage` (= `register.manage` @ `ResourceContext.system()`) + `can_release` (= `document.release` over `_register_release_scope` [artifact + folder + level + lifecycle_state + SoD-2], with `sig_hook=True` + `sod` + `allow_approver_release` + `source_ip` threaded — the `_document_capabilities` PURE-PDP pattern verbatim, `gather_grants`+`authorize(...).allow`, NEVER `enforce` → no authz-audit row), wired into ONLY the two `GET …/register` endpoints (caps are OPTIONAL + GET-only → the byte-identical action endpoints stay UNTOUCHED; the FE refetches the GET after each mutation). **Part B (FE)** — `apps/web/src/features/context/` mirroring `features/risk/`: `ContextRegisterPage` + the **SWOT 2×2 board** (`ContextSwotBoard` — the clause-4.1 viz analogue; `canManage`/the New-risk process-OR gate untouched). **3 owner decisions (AskUserQuestion ×3):** (D-1) the viz analogue = the **SWOT 2×2 board** (vs a classification×category count grid / no-viz); (D-2) **`can_release`/`can_manage` for BOTH registers** (parity — the twins kept in lockstep via the SHARED helper; vs context-only / FE-only-defer); (D-3) **one slice** (the full SPA incl. the steward console — context's backend was fully ready, unlike risk which split 4b→5). **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the BE caps are the FAITHFUL gate the S-context-1/S-risk-5 learnings flagged** — a single-axis FE `/me/permissions` probe CANNOT replicate the multi-axis release scope; the integration tests prove the caps PREDICT the exact SoD-2 403/200 outcomes for BOTH registers (the steward HOLDS `document.release` but SoD-2 → `can_release:false`; the third-party releaser → `true`) — drop `sod`/`allow_approver_release` and the steward computes `true` and the test fails; (6) **a new orthogonal Home tile read folds into BOTH `PlanCard.allForbidden` AND every all-forbidden test** (the bare-demo `HomePage` test + the PlanCard no-access test both needed `/context/summary` 403 added). **Reviews:** diff-critic CLEAN (verified the helper line-by-line vs the PEP `evaluate` — can't be true-when-403 or false-when-allow; the risk migration loses NO authz) + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN (fixtures pinned via `satisfies`, no jest-dom×tsc trap, the duplicate-name actively avoided, non-optimistic mutations, non-tautological assertions) + a 3-lens adversarial Workflow (FE-gating/deny-wins · a11y/colour-safe-RAG · read-of-record) → 1 confirmed MINOR a11y finding (trap #3), FIXED + test-locked. **⚠ CI flaked ONCE on an UNRELATED `ReviewApprovePage` test** (`/Supplier Selection/` render-timing race in the loaded runner;
