- **S-process-scope-1** (enrich the secondary auth surfaces with `process_ids` + the `document.create` link-on-create write-path) — **the named S-owner-assignment-1 follow-up "enrich every auth surface with `process_ids`", shipped for the surfaces that CONVERGED.** S-owner-assignment-1 migrated `_document_scope` (document detail/list/edit), but the workflow approval-history reads, the search row-filter, and `document.create` all built their own `ResourceContext` WITHOUT `process_ids`, so a bound Process-Owner's PROCESS-scoped grant mis-denied them. **What shipped (BE+FE, NO migration [head stays `0056`], NO new permission key [catalog stays 102, R38 not engaged]; contract = ONE additive `DocumentCreate.process_ids`):** (1) a shared `vault_repo.process_ids_for_doc(s)` loader — `_document_scope_by_id` + the `GET /documents` list batch refactored onto it (parity-preserving, deletes the two duplicated inline ProcessLink queries); (2) **workflow** — `GET /workflow-instances/{id}` + `GET /documents/{id}/approval` carry the subject doc's `process_ids` (both gate `document.read`); (3) **search** — `_readable_hits` + `/search/suggest` batch-load `process_ids` per candidate hit; (4) **`document.create` write-path** — `DocumentCreate.process_ids` (optional, `maxItems:50`) links the new doc AT creation: `create_document(processes=...)` creates the doc + `ProcessLink` rows + `PROCESS_LINKED` audit (with `identifier=doc.identifier` → `to_audit_event` maps `scope_ref=identifier`, byte-compatible with the standalone link endpoint's per-document trail) in ONE txn/commit (atomic — a failed link can't strand a doc its process-scoped creator could no longer read); authorize `document.create` over the declared processes THEN re-`enforce` `document.manage_metadata` PER declared process (mirrors `_enforce_target_process`, so an owner of P1 can't smuggle a link to an unowned P2 — the S-owner-assignment-1 escalation class), empty `process_ids` ⇒ byte-identical to the pre-slice create; plus a processes `MultiSelect` on the New-Document wizard. **Load-bearing decisions:** the enrichment is **strictly monotonic / AZ-INV-8-safe** — the PDP matches a PROCESS grant iff `selector.process_ids ∩ resource.process_ids ≠ ∅`, so adding `process_ids` only newly *matches* a grant already targeting that exact process, never widens SYSTEM/ARTIFACT/FOLDER/DOC_CLASS (re-derived per surface). `_decision_scope` (the workflow approve/review DECIDE gate) was deliberately EXCLUDED — the seeded "Process Owner" role holds no `document.approve`/`review`, so enriching it is a dead no-op (named, not missed). **⚠ THE big lesson — the records read enrichment did NOT converge and was TRIMMED OUT mid-slice:** records read (a record inherits its source-doc + `EvidenceForLink(PROCESS)` scope, matching the packs `record.read` gate) was built + reviewed, but Codex surfaced a NEW evidence-link/correction over-grant edge every round — **CX-1** (evidence-link POST doesn't re-auth the PROCESS target → an owner of P1 makes a record readable to P2's owners), **CX-4** (correction doesn't re-scope its source), **R2-1** (the re-auth must PRESERVE the record scope, replacing only `process_ids`, else ARTIFACT/FOLDER holders over-blocked), **R2-2** (the evidence-link DELETE also needs target re-auth), **R2-3** (`capture_correction` FORCES a source-backed original's OWN source — the body's is ignored — so re-auth the EFFECTIVE source), **R3-1** (a source-less evidence-linked record's correction loses its process binding → invisible to its creator), **R3-2** (a PRE-EXISTING `capa_stage` evidence-link authz gap the partial re-auth highlights). After 3 substantive rounds with no convergence, the owner's call was to **revert the records read enrichment** (restore `api/records.py`, `services/records/repository.py`, `services/packs/repository.py` to `main`) and ship only the converged surfaces. **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **adding `process_ids` to a READ surface is monotonic and safe, but adding it to a surface whose process bindings are created by UN-RE-AUTHORIZED write paths (records evidence-link / correction) opens an over-grant** — the read enrichment is only as sound as the write-path target re-authorization (the `_enforce_target_process` discipline) for EVERY target type, AND the correction-chain scope; that whole sub-project is deferred. (2) the `document.create` chicken-and-egg (a new doc has no ProcessLink) is the reason create needs `process_ids` in the BODY + atomic link-on-create — it can't be a pure resolver enrichment like the reads. (3) the ruff PostToolUse hook strips just-added imports (body-first, recurring). (4) **Codex authz non-convergence again** — the shipped surfaces (workflow/search/create) had ZERO findings across 4 rounds; 100% of findings were on records (reverted) or the deferred FE; triage per round, and when a surface keeps generating edges, TRIM it rather than chase. **Deferred (named, not faked) — ONE focused follow-up, "records process-scope read":** the records read enrichment bundled with its write-path target re-auth (evidence-link POST/DELETE + correction effective-source + EVERY non-process evidence-link target incl. the pre-existing `capa_stage` gap), the correction-chain scope, the pre-existing packs `record.read` exposure, AND **per-process read filtering on `GET /processes` + `GET /clauses`** (both SYSTEM-gated today → the create-in-process wizard works for SYSTEM/Author authors but the picker + clause step are empty for a bound Process-Owner; the `document.create` backend is correct regardless). Codex **CX-3** (require `document.create` per declared process) was **DECLINED** — the end-state (a doc linked to P1+P2) is reachable with the same perms via `create([P1])` + the standalone `link(P2)` (which gates only `manage_metadata`-for-P2), so per-process create would be stricter than the documented decomposed flow. **Test delta: +8 api integration** (`test_process_scope.py`, CI-only on Windows: create-in-owned-process + multi-process dedup + can't-create-unlinked + the P1+P2 escalation-403 + unknown-process-422 + create-holder-without-manage_metadata + the workflow approval/instance 403→200 flip on a linked doc with the unlinked-stays-403 boundary + search-sees-only-linked-effective) **+2 web** (`NewDocumentWizard.test.tsx`: the picker sends `process_ids`; the omitted-when-empty byte-identical body); **web 1084→1086**, no api unit added. ruff + mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); redocly clean; full web `1086/1086`. **diff-critic (×2) + web-test-trap-reviewer + a 3-lens review Workflow (missed-surface / authz-edges / create-parity) all CLEAN on the shipped surfaces**; the records findings were 100% Codex (the documented authz-non-convergence pattern). **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads (12 total — records moot/reverted, CX-3 declined, FE deferred — all replied + resolved) + owner's explicit go. PR [#211](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/211), squash `42f8de6`.

- **S-owner-assignment-1** (real process-owner binding + the repo-wide `_document_scope`→`process_ids` migration) — **closes the owner-assignment gap that every prior PROCESS-scoped slice rode around via SYSTEM overrides.** The whole PROCESS-scoped ABAC engine was already built (`ScopeLevel.PROCESS`, the PDP `_matches_scope` process_ids intersection, `role_assignment.bound_scope` as the concretization seam, the seeded "Process Owner" permission-role), but nothing turned "Diego owns Purchasing" into a concrete `process_id`: every seeded Process-Owner grant carried the literal placeholder `selector.process_id = ":assignment_process"` (migrations 0004/0036/0040/0043/0044/0052) that matches no real process, so PROCESS-finest-scope authority was satisfied only by SYSTEM overrides. **What shipped (BE+FE, migration `0056`, NO new permission key — rides the seeded-but-unenforced `process.assign_owner`; catalog stays 102, R38 not engaged):** (1) the ERD-deferred **`org_role_assignment`** RACI carrier (`org_role_id`→`org_role`, `user_id`→`app_user`, `process_id` NULLABLE→`process`, `UNIQUE(org_role_id,user_id,process_id)`) + its ORM (registered in `db/models/__init__.py`) + two additive `event_type` values `PROCESS_OWNER_ASSIGNED`/`_REVOKED` (autocommit_block ADD VALUE; NO new `audit_object_type` — events key on the existing `process` value); (2) **`services/owner_assignment.py`** — `assign_process_owner`/`revoke_process_owner` in ONE txn: resolve-or-create the single generic "Process Owner" org_role, upsert the org_role_assignment RACI row, and **mint/extend a SINGLE PROCESS-scoped Process-Owner `role_assignment.bound_scope`** carrying a GROWING `process_ids` set (the PDP reads `selector.process_id OR process_ids`, so one row authorizes many owned processes — `role_assignment` has no uniqueness backstop, so one growing row beats N rows), **system-attributed** (the `process.assign_owner` content-tier gate is the sole authority; NOT re-gated through SYSTEM-tier `permission.grant`), serialized on the parent `app_user` row FOR UPDATE, audited both halves, then `invalidate_user_permissions`; (3) `POST`/`DELETE /processes/{id}/owner` + `GET /processes/{id}/owners` (+ openapi); (4) the **repo-wide `_document_scope` migration** — `_document_scope_by_id` now folds the doc's `ProcessLink` ids into `ResourceContext.process_ids` (deleting the single-use `_document_scope_with_processes`, repointing `_distribute`), and the `GET /documents` list read-filter batch-loads process links per row (no N+1), so a bound Process-Owner's `document.*` grant authorizes across EVERY document gate, not just `distribute`; (5) a minimal **`admin/ProcessesAdmin.tsx`** tab (assign/revoke owners; coarse SYSTEM `process.assign_owner` probe gates the write affordances, server 403 is the true boundary). **THE central design device — the `managed_by:"owner_assignment"` bound_scope marker** (the PDP `_scope_from_dict` ignores it — reads level/selector/predicates only): owner-assignment-minted grants confer the scoped PERMISSION set but are EXCLUDED from every ROLE-MEMBERSHIP consumer. **⚠ THE load-bearing lesson — "mint a Process-Owner `role_assignment`" leaks role MEMBERSHIP everywhere, and Codex (3 substantive rounds, 6→6→3 findings) is the only finder of it** (clean diff-critic/migration-reviewer/web-test-trap passed the core code each round): the marker exclusion had to be applied to (a) **workflow candidate resolution** `wf_repo.users_with_roles` — the **P1**: migration 0043's DCR-MAJOR-approval stage NAMES "Process Owner" as a candidate role and `users_with_roles` joins on `Role.name` (scope-blind), so an owner of process A would otherwise become a candidate for every "Process Owner"-gated stage org-wide (a DCR for process B); (b) **ack audience** `resolve_audience` — same flood onto every process owner for a role-targeted distribution; (c) the **generic role surface** `authz.py` — `list_user_roles` HIDES marked rows + `revoke_user_role` 409s them (a bare delete would orphan the org_role_assignment RACI row), and the marker is **un-forgeable** (`assign_user_role` strips a caller-supplied `managed_by`). **⚠ The `_document_scope` widening ALSO introduced a process-link ESCALATION** — `document.manage_metadata` now matches via ANY linked process, so an owner of A on a doc linked to A+B could mutate links to B → the link/unlink endpoints re-`enforce` `document.manage_metadata` against the TARGET process scope (`_enforce_target_process`: SYSTEM/ARTIFACT/FOLDER holders still pass, a PROCESS owner must own the target). **⚠ Other traps:** an idempotent re-assign must SKIP the phantom `PROCESS_OWNER_ASSIGNED`/`ROLE_ASSIGN` audit rows (track whether the binding or the process_ids actually changed); a narrowing revoke emits `ROLE_REVOKE` (not `ROLE_ASSIGN` — revoke always reduces access); `GET /owners` is process-scoped read (a PROCESS owner can read their own process's owners — **the FIRST CI failure was a TEST bug**: it's `process.read`-gated and the tests granted only `assign_owner` → 403, then the next test iterated the 403 error body → `TypeError`); the optional `org_role_id` body field was REMOVED (every binding keys to ONE generic org_role → at most one org_role_assignment per (user,process) → revoke can't over-delete an unrelated RACI binding); `bound_scope` is JSONB → reassign a fresh dict, never in-place (S-ing-4); FK names match the Base naming convention (alembic-check phantom-DROP) + the ORM registered in `__init__.py`; the ruff hook strips just-added imports (body-first). **Deferred (named, not faked) — ONE coherent follow-up, "enrich every auth surface with `process_ids`":** the slice migrated `_document_scope` (document detail/list/edit/approve work), but `document.create` (POST /documents authorizes from folder/doc_class), workflow approval-history reads (`/workflow-instances/{id}`, `/documents/{id}/approval`), the `search` row-filter, and `record.read`/list scopes all build their OWN ResourceContext without process_ids — so the minted Process-Owner grant is **read/edit/approve-effective on EXISTING process-linked documents** but create + those secondary reads need the same enrichment (each a sibling resolver). Plus the FE per-process assign-owner probe (deliberate coarse-SYSTEM gate; additive if process-scoped `assign_owner` delegation lands); the **CAPA Raise process-scope deferral is now UNBLOCKED** (the binding exists) but the Raise process-picker is still unwired. **Test delta: +11 api integration** (CI-only on Windows: the 403→200 doc-read flip on a process-linked doc · the union + idempotent no-op · revoke-narrows-then-drops · admin SYSTEM + PROCESS grants survive · workflow-candidacy exclusion · managed-revoke 409 · target-process link authority · forged-marker strip) **+4 web** (`ProcessesAdmin.test.tsx`: roster + read-only drawer, assign, remove, calm 403); **web 1080→1084.** No api unit added. ruff + mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); migration round-trip up↔down↔`alembic check` CLEAN on PG16; redocly clean. **diff-critic 1 MINOR** (owner-revoke could clobber a separately-granted admin Process-Owner row → the `managed_by` marker; fixed + tested); **migration-reviewer + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN; Codex 3 substantive rounds → round 4 CLEAN 👍** (the design class genuinely doesn't converge — each round surfaced a new role-membership/scope-widening interaction; triage per round: fix the introduced issue, defer bounded-safe). **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads (15 total, all replied + resolved) + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. PR [#209](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/209), squash `48c7e71`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVE GRADING FREEZE — per-reading frozen direction/threshold (closes the S-obj-charts "freeze the grading inputs" deferral) (0055)

- **S-obj-freeze** (freeze the FULL per-reading KPI grading basis) — **closes the named S-obj-charts v1.x deferral: the per-reading RAG verdict was only PARTIALLY frozen, so a commitment revision that flipped `direction` (HIGHER↔LOWER) or moved the `at_risk_threshold` retroactively re-graded historical readings (a past green could read red).** Only `kpi_measurement.target_at_capture` was frozen; `direction`/`at_risk_threshold` were read LIVE from the governing commitment at serialize time. **What shipped (BACKEND-ONLY, additive, migration `0055`):** two new `kpi_measurement` columns — `direction_at_capture` (REUSE the `objective_direction` enum, `create_type=False`) + `at_risk_threshold_at_capture` (Numeric) — both **NULLABLE**; `record_measurement` snapshots them from the SAME governing-else-working resolution as `target_at_capture` (and seals them into the WORM `KPI_READING` record's `form_field_values` too); `api/objectives.py::_measurement` grades off the frozen columns (the two measurement endpoints SHED their now-dead `resolve_commitment` blocks — a net simplification). **The frozen basis stays INTERNAL** — the `Measurement` response is byte-identical (only the `rag` description in `openapi.yaml` updated to the frozen-basis semantics), so **no web/MSW change** (contracts + web CI jobs are no-ops). `compute_scorecard` (the live-objective grade) is intentionally UNCHANGED — a different semantic from a frozen historical reading. **Capture-time backfill (the load-bearing part — 4 Codex rounds hardened it):** each existing reading freezes the commitment that was the CURRENT effective version at its `created_at`, EXACTLY what `record_measurement` froze (it reads `current_effective_version_id`, which only moves at `_cutover`). The version-selection (1) considers ONLY versions that actually went Effective (`version_state='Effective' OR effective_to IS NOT NULL` — never a still-`Approved` scheduled revision), and (2) bounds each version's governing window by the PRIOR version's `effective_to` (the real cutover via the `superseded_by_version_id` chain), NOT its own (possibly scheduled) `effective_from`. A reading with no applicable governing version (pre-first-release) or under a fold-less/non-object snapshot falls back to the working row for BOTH columns (mirroring the runtime `governing = raw if isinstance(raw, dict) else None` guard). The backfill UPDATE runs as the migration OWNER role, unaffected by `kpi_measurement`'s app-role `REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE` (WORM intact — no app path updates the columns post-insert). **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the historical backfill is the hard part, not the column add** — reconstructing "what commitment governed at capture" is genuinely subtle and the migration round-trip / `alembic check` are VALUE-BLIND (empty fresh DB), so the **diff-critic + migration-reviewer were CLEAN on the application code but Codex was the edge-finder on the backfill over 4 rounds**: capture-time-vs-current → scheduled-vs-actual-cutover → not-yet-cutover-Approved-version → nullable-row-aborts-SET-NOT-NULL. Validate the backfill CASE/version-selection with **synthetic VALUES-based SQL** (no FK scaffolding) on a throwaway PG16 — pin the gap cases (a reading between a scheduled `effective_from` and the late `release_due` cutover must freeze the PRIOR basis). (2) **the migration-reviewer (not Codex) caught the FIRST real bug a clean diff-critic missed** — the threshold CASE was gated on a different predicate than the direction CASE (a `COALESCE` vs a `CASE`-with-fold-guard), so a fold-less governing version would NULL the threshold where the live grader uses the working row → gate BOTH columns on the IDENTICAL `jsonb_typeof(... ->'objective_commitment')='object'` predicate. (3) **`direction_at_capture` is NULLABLE, not NOT NULL** — `objective_id` is schema-nullable + the serializer handles an objective-less reading, so a `SET NOT NULL` would abort on an ad-hoc/imported objective-less row (Codex); the serializer narrows the now-Optional direction (None→"unmeasured", unreachable for the objective-scoped endpoints). (4) **the discriminating test must FLIP the verdict** — the existing target-freeze test coincidentally stays amber under both old/new behaviour; the new direction-flip + threshold-move integration tests are designed so frozen≠live (else they don't prove the freeze). (5) the **revision-id `varchar(32)` limit** — `0055_objective_freeze_grading_inputs` (36 chars) overflowed `alembic_version.version_num` at runtime (CI/round-trip would have caught it, but locally first) → renamed to `0055_objective_grading_freeze` (29). (6) the **ruff auto-fix hook strips a just-added import** (the recurring trap — re-add `objective_direction_enum` AFTER the column references it). **Deferred (named, not faked):** exposing the frozen `direction_at_capture`/`at_risk_threshold_at_capture` in the `Measurement` response (audit-transparency tooltip "graded under higher-is-better, amber<95" — owner kept them INTERNAL this slice; a trivial additive add); the other S-obj-charts deferrals (register sparklines, time-proportional x-axis, per-process objective reads) are untouched. **Test delta: +2 api unit** (`test_objective_measurement_rag.py` unit: `test_rag_reads_frozen_direction_not_live` + `test_rag_reads_frozen_threshold_not_live` — same value/target, opposite frozen basis → opposite verdict; full unit **810 passed**) **+2 api integration** (CI-only on Windows: a direction-flip and a threshold-move revision where frozen≠live → the old reading's `rag` is unchanged) + the `test_objective_revision.py` mid-revision capture test EXTENDED to assert direction/threshold snapshot the GOVERNING (not in-edit) values via a direct DB read; **web unchanged** (backend-only). ruff + mypy-strict clean; migration round-trip up↔down↔`alembic check` clean on PG16 + the backfill logic proven across 8 synthetic cases. **diff-critic CLEAN; migration-reviewer** found 1 MAJOR (the threshold/direction asymmetry, fixed + re-confirmed CLEAN); **Codex 4 rounds** (capture-time backfill / seal-record / contract-sync → prior-`effective_to` window → `version_state` filter + nullable → final **clean: "no major issues, Delightful"**); all 7 inline threads resolved. **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. PR [#197](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/197), squash `b83bae4`.

## v1.x LEADERSHIP ROUTING — document-backed Top-Management release authorization (POL/OBJ/MR)

- **S-leadership-dcr-test** (lock in the DCR-implement leadership preflight — closes the named S-leadership-1 deferral) — **closes S-leadership-1's named-not-faked deferral verbatim: "a dedicated DCR-implement-of-a-leadership-artifact integration test."** **Backend TEST-ONLY — no migration (head stays `0055`, next free `0056`), no production code / contract / permission change.** **The guard:** `services/dcr/service.py::implement_dcr` preflights the Top-Management release gate SYNCHRONOUSLY (`services/vault/leadership_authorization.assert_release_authorized`, BEFORE `session.commit()`) for a REVISE/CREATE go-live — because the real cutover runs LATER in the async `release_due` Beat sweep, which **swallows** the gate's 409 (`vault/lifecycle.release_due` catches `(ProblemException, IllegalTransition)` and skips). Without the preflight a leadership-gated DCR implement would commit the DCR as Implemented while the version stayed Approved (a stuck false-success — the S-leadership-1 round-2 Codex P2). That path had ZERO DCR integration coverage (no `grep` hit for leadership / `assert_release_authorized` / `leadership_authorization_required` under `tests/integration`). **What shipped:** ONE integration test `test_revise_implement_blocked_until_leadership_authorized` (appended to `tests/integration/test_dcr_implement.py`) on a NON-singleton **OBJ**-typed REVISE DCR, both arms in one narrative: (1) flag on → implement → **409 `leadership_authorization_required`** AND `GET /dcrs/{id}` still `Approved` (the flip rolled back — no false Implemented); (2) authorize the Approved version (`POST …/request-leadership-authorization` + a Top-Management `verify`) → the **SAME** implement → 200 Implemented → `release_due()` sweep → version Effective → `close` → Closed (proves the preflight blocks, rolls back, AND does not over-block). **Care points / decisions:** the gate keys on `document_type.code ∈ {POL,OBJ,MR}` + the flag + a version `verify` sig, so a PLAIN OBJ-typed vault document (`s5.drive_to_approved(type_id("OBJ"))` + the existing REVISE `_drive_dcr_to_approved`, **NO `quality_objective` row**) exercises it — REVISE never trips the CREATE-only `create_target_managed_subtype`/`create_target_not_new` guards, and the generic sweep cutover has no managed-subtype coupling; **OBJ is `is_singleton=False`** so pushing it Effective is shared-org-safe (POL would be singleton → 409-only, no happy path — the owner's chosen "both arms on OBJ" over "blocked-only on POL"). The org flag is flipped ON in a `try`/reset OFF in `finally`, every assertion is run-scoped to this test's own ids, and `release_due()` is checked with membership (`in`), never an absolute global count (the global-sweep pattern of the existing `test_revise_implement_then_sweep_then_close`). Reuses the leadership helpers (`_set_leadership_flag`/`_assign_top_mgmt`/`_request`/`_my_pending_task`) cross-imported from `test_leadership_authorization` (aliased `_request as _request_leadership`, `_my_pending_task as _my_leadership_task` to dodge the `test_capa._my_pending_task` clash); identity wiring is consistent (same `keycloak_subject` → same `AppUser` across `_auth`/`_ensure_user`/`_assign_top_mgmt`). **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) the **ruff auto-fix hook STRIPPED the just-added imports as unused** (they're unused until a body references them) → append the test body FIRST, THEN re-add the imports (the recurring "ruff strips a just-added import" trap). (2) **CI scopes mypy to `src` only** (`ci.yml` api job: `uv run mypy src`), NOT `tests/` — so integration tests are NOT type-checked (this is why the pre-existing `no-any-return`/`attr-defined` "errors" in `test_vault`/`s5_helpers`/`test_capa`/`test_leadership_authorization` sit on green `main`); `ruff check .` DOES lint the whole repo (incl. tests). So a TEST-ONLY slice's local gate = ruff lint + format-check; mypy is irrelevant; the integration shards in CI are authoritative (the `-m integration` suite can't run on the owner's Windows box). (3) the discriminator: the **SAME** implement call is asserted 409 then 200 around the authorize step (same `_latest_approved_version` resolved both sides), so the verify-sig is genuinely load-bearing — not a coincidental pass. **Test delta: +1 api integration** (`test_dcr_implement.py`, +103 lines); **web unchanged** (backend-only). ruff + format clean; **diff-critic CLEAN** (verified the 409 code is raised in exactly one place — `leadership_authorization.py:187`; no earlier authz/SoD-2/FSM gate pre-empts it; the positive arm depends on the sig; flag-reset/run-scoping/`release_due`-membership all sound); **Codex CLEAN** ("Didn't find any major issues"); all 4 integration shards green. **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 review threads + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. PR [#201](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/201), squash `8d9dd08`.

- **S-leadership-cx1** (close the S-leadership-fe deferral **CX-1** — the server-computed per-document "request leadership authorization" capability) — **a small, FE-enabling follow-up that fixes a real visibility gap; backend probe + 1 contract field + FE gate rewire. NO migration (head stays `0054`), NO new permission key (rides the existing `document.approve`; R38 not engaged, R45-consistent); the welded `document_approval` path + `capabilities.release` byte-identical.** **The bug:** the `LeadershipReleaseGate` Request button gated on `usePermissions().can("document.approve")` with **no scope arg** → probes `/me/permissions` at **SYSTEM scope**; but `document.approve` has **`finest_scope=ARTIFACT`** (docs/07 §3.1 — the catalog even shows `Ken | document.approve | DOC_CLASS=Level-2`), so a content/process/folder/doc-class-scoped approver who legitimately holds it at the doc's scope (and whom the server WOULD authorize on POST) saw the dimmed "an approver must start it" message. A **visibility gap, not a security hole** (the request endpoint still enforces the real scope). **What shipped:** a server-computed, ABAC-aware boolean **`can_request`** on the `GET /documents/{id}/leadership-authorization` status payload the gate **already fetches** for POL/OBJ/MR alike (the FE now reads `data.can_request` and **drops `usePermissions` entirely**). The probe `_can_request_leadership_authorization` mirrors the request endpoint's gate (`_approve = require("document.approve", async_scope_resolver=_document_scope)`) **exactly**: `authorize(gather_grants("document.approve"), "document.approve", _document_scope_by_id(doc.id), ctx).allow` — **no `sig_hook`, no `process_ids`, the SoD overlay is inert** (the scope carries no author/approver, so a plain `authorize` matches the endpoint's effective result), and it does **NOT** fold in `is_leadership`/`required`/`Approved` state (those stay on the same payload; the FE ANDs them — the obsolete-capability-vs-§7.3-runtime-gate split). It uses the **pure PDP** (`gather_grants`+`authorize`), never `enforce` → **no authz-audit row** per detail GET. `release_authorization_status` stays caller-agnostic (the `can_request` merge is computed in the endpoint, which has the caller + `Request`). **Owner scoping call (the one real fork):** carry the boolean on the **status payload** (Option A) vs the document/objective/MR **`capabilities` block** (Option B, the brief's literal). Chose A — the gate already reads that exact payload for all three surfaces, so it's **1 serializer, 0 parent changes, no drift** across three independently-computed `capabilities.release` booleans; B would touch 3 cap serializers + 3 openapi schemas + thread a prop from 3 parents. **OpenAPI:** `can_request` added to `LeadershipAuthorizationStatus` `properties` **and** `required` (it has `additionalProperties:false`). **⚠ Codex P2 (the edge-finder again — a CLEAN diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer BOTH missed it):** the probe built `RequestContext` with **`source_ip=None`**, but the PDP rejects an **`ip_allow`-narrowed** `document.approve` grant when `source_ip` is None (`pdp.py:134`), while the real POST gate goes through the PEP's `evaluate()`, which sets `source_ip=request.client.host` (`pep.py:94`) → under an `ip_allow` grant the status returns `can_request:false` and the FE HIDES a button the server would allow — **the inverse false-PASS (over-strict probe) CX-1 itself exists to prevent.** Fixed (commit `8fedd64`) by threading `source_ip` into the probe exactly as `pep.py::evaluate` builds it, so an `ip_allow` grant evaluates identically in probe and gate. **⚠ Note for a future session:** `ip_allow` is a **v1-deferred** predicate (its `guest_grant` carrier is v1.x; no grant carries it today — docs/06), and the **sibling capability probes** (`release`/`edit`/… in `_document_capabilities`, `_objective_capabilities`, `_mr_capabilities`) **share the same pre-existing `source_ip` gap** → a separate, codebase-wide follow-up (thread `source_ip` through every capability probe, or leave it while `ip_allow` stays deferred); CX-1's probe now mirrors its endpoint exactly. The diff-critic had pre-verified the **SoD overlay is inert** here (it chased `document.approve` ∈ `_SOD_KEYS` → refuted: `_document_scope_by_id` never populates `author_user_id`/`approver_user_ids`, so both paths return identical allow/deny). **Deferred-still-open (named-not-faked):** CX-4 (the status read fails OPEN by design) and CR-2 (mock `:id` echo) from S-leadership-fe remain; the sibling-probe `source_ip` gap above. **Test delta: web 1041 → 1041** (FE test **reworked, not net-new** — `LeadershipReleaseGate.test.tsx` drops the `grantApprove()`/`/me/permissions` mock + `MePermissions` import and drives all 8 cases off the status fixtures' `can_request`; the in-progress/NEEDS_ATTENTION fixtures keep `can_request:true` so those suppression tests prove the STATE gate, not an accidental cap-false; one case uses `{...leadershipRequiredStatus, can_request:false}`); **+1 api integration** (`test_status_can_request_is_per_caller`: the requester [holds `document.approve`] reads `True`, the releaser [holds `document.release`+`read` but NOT `approve`] reads `False` — both can GET the status; run-scoped own-salt, flag-independent so no shared-DB flag manipulation) + a `can_request is False` assertion folded into the OBJ release happy-path. All 5 MSW status fixtures pinned to the real serializer (`satisfies`-enforced). `/check-web` green (eslint + strict `tsc` + build + **1041/1041**); ruff + mypy-strict clean; redocly valid; CI 11/11. **diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN; Codex** found the 1 P2 (fixed) + re-reviewed clean. **Merge gate:** Codex thread resolved + green CI + owner's explicit go. PR [#195](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/195), squash `6a14102`.

- **S-leadership-fe** (the deferred FRONT-END for the document-backed Top-Management RELEASE authorization, POL/OBJ/MR) — **completes the leadership-routing feature end-to-end; mirrors the S-improvement-4 review SPA.** **FE-only — no migration (head stays `0054`), no new endpoint/contract** (the backend #190 already shipped the `LeadershipAuthorization{Status,Cycle,Task,Request}` schemas + the two paths + the `WorkflowInstance.subject_type` enum member + the `OrgConfig` flag). **What shipped:** (1) a **`/tasks` decide arm** for a new `LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION` task subject — `DecisionCard` gains verify/reject + the `verify` signature (structurally identical to `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE`); a new `LeadershipApprovalContext` best-effort-reads `GET /documents/{id}` (calm 403 → falls back to the task's `subject_identifier`/`subject_title`); a `ReviewApprovePage` branch with **`isLeadership` added to the load-bearing `isDocumentSubject` negation** so a leadership task NEVER routes the welded document-approval stepper+redline (proven by a no-`workflow-instance`-read test); `useDecideTask` invalidates the leadership-authorization + doc/obj/MR caches. (2) a shared, **self-suppressing `LeadershipReleaseGate`** (new `features/leadership/` dir + `hooks.ts`) reading `GET /documents/{id}/leadership-authorization` — renders **null** for a non-leadership doc or flag-off (safe to embed everywhere); when `required && !authorized` it suppresses the Release button (because **`capabilities.release` does NOT fold in the gate** — verified in `_document_capabilities`, which computes `release` from `document.release`+SoD-2 only) and shows the state (authorized→release-may-proceed / awaiting / NEEDS_ATTENTION+re-request / a `document.approve`-gated Request button); embedded in ALL THREE release surfaces — **POL** via `ApprovalsTab`, **OBJ** via `ObjectiveDetailPage`, **MR** via `ManagementReviewDetailPage`, each guarding `canRelease` with `!blocksRelease`. The OBJ/MR Lifecycle-card render condition also includes `lead.blocksRelease` so the gate panel can't **collapse-and-vanish** when release is the only blocked affordance. **Owner scoping calls:** affordance on all three surfaces (one shared component) · inline panel above Release · admin org-flag toggle OUT of scope (set via `PATCH /admin/config`) · no dedicated pending-list (the `/tasks` inbox + the per-doc panel cover it). **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the orient fan-out reader GUESSED `action_expected:bool` and `stage_key:"top_management"` — BOTH WRONG**: `Task.action_expected` is a nullable `Text` (`string|null`) and the seeded stage key is `"leadership_authorization"` (migration 0054, `_STAGE["key"]`). Pin MSW fixtures to the REAL serializer (`api/documents.py::_leadership_authorization`), not the orient summary — and the **diff-critic** (not the clean web-test-trap-reviewer) caught the stage-key fixture mismatch. (2) **Codex (the edge-finder) found a real P1 a CLEAN diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer BOTH missed:** the leadership-authorization status is **version-scoped but cached by document id**, so a re-approval (release→revise→re-approve) would reuse the prior version's stale `authorized:true` → the gate would show Release for an unauthorized NEW version until the cutover 409s. Fix: the welded **DOCUMENT approval decision** (POL/OBJ/MR all re-approve through it) invalidates `["leadership-authorization", id]`. (3) **Codex > CodeRabbit** on this PR — Codex filed 5 (1×P1, 3×P2, 1×P3) incl. the P1; CodeRabbit filed 2 actionable + 1 nitpick; their **only overlap** was CR-1≡CX-5 (invalidate the status on the request 409 via **`onSettled`**, not just `onSuccess`). **Review fixes applied pre-merge** (commit `ca2be38`): CX-3 (the P1) · CX-2 (NEEDS_ATTENTION keeps the Request affordance — the backend permits a fresh cycle from a terminal NEEDS_ATTENTION instance) · CR-1/CX-5 (`onSettled` refetch) · CR-nit (assert the obj+MR invalidation keys). **Deferred (named-not-faked):** **CX-1** — the Request button gates on **SYSTEM-scope** `document.approve` because `DocumentSummary` carries no `process_id`, so a content/process-scoped approver doesn't see it (the server still enforces the real scope); the clean fix is a **server-computed per-document capability** (like `capabilities.release`) — a backend+FE follow-up (the v1 SYSTEM-fallback posture matches objectives/CAPA register gating; chip `task_500cf729`). **CX-4** — the status read **fails OPEN** by design (a transient leadership-status read failure → `blocksRelease=false` → Release shows; failing closed would couple EVERY document's Release to that one endpoint's availability, and the backend cutover is the real gate; the protected persona — can release OBJ/MR but lacks `document.read` — is effectively empty). **CR-2** — echo `:id` in the request mock (low value; no test reads the response body). **Test delta: web 1017 → 1041 (+24)** — `LeadershipReleaseGate.test.tsx` (8: self-suppress / required+Request / no-`document.approve`-hides-Request / awaiting / NEEDS_ATTENTION+re-request / authorized / non-Approved-null / 409-calm+refetch), a `ReviewApprovePage` LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION describe (context+verify-card / no-welded-path / sign-gating / decided-alert / axe), a `DecisionCard` variant, the `useDecideTask` LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION + DOCUMENT-CX-3 invalidation tests, and the gate integration on ApprovalsTab/OBJ/MR. `/check-web` green (eslint + strict `tsc` + build + full vitest **1041/1041**). **web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN; diff-critic** caught the stage-key fixture + flagged the OBJ/MR card-collapse coverage (both fixed pre-PR). **Merge gate:** all 7 Codex+CodeRabbit threads resolved (fixed or deferred-with-rationale) + 0 unresolved + green CI + owner's explicit go. PR [#192](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/192), squash `9681b6d`.

- **S-leadership-1** (route the clause-5/6/9 leadership artifacts' release sign-off to a Top-Management pool) — **the document-backed sibling of S-improvement-4, closing the named-enhancement gap the welded single-stage `document_approval` can't express (doc 10 §2.5, decisions-register R45).** **Why:** the Quality Policy (POL §5.2), Quality Objectives (OBJ §6.2) and Management Review (MR §9.3) are all `kind=DOCUMENT` and rode the welded single-stage path — their approver pool is whoever holds `document.approve` (Approver/QMS-Owner); there was NO Top-Management gate on these leadership acts, and the welded `decide()` cannot conditionally route. **What shipped (BACKEND-ONLY, opt-in, additive — the welded `document_approval`/`decide()`/`instantiate_approval` path is byte-identical, pinned by `test_approval.py`):** an org config flag `system_config.leadership_release_requires_top_management_authorization` (default **OFF**) that, when on, blocks **RELEASE** of a leadership-type doc until a "Top Management" member signs `meaning=verify` on the Approved `document_version`. The gate is enforced at the **shared `vault/lifecycle._cutover` chokepoint** (covers the direct `POST /documents/{id}/release`, the `/objectives/{id}/release` + `/management-reviews/{id}/release` wrappers, AND the DCR-implement go-live — one insertion, no side-door) via a shared `services/vault/leadership_authorization.assert_release_authorized`. The sign-off routes through the generic multi-stage engine: `POST /documents/{id}/request-leadership-authorization` (gate `document.approve` at the doc scope; 409 `not_a_leadership_artifact` / `document_not_approved` / `authorization_in_progress` / `already_authorized`) opens a seeded `leadership_release_authorization` instance (a single Top-Management `PARALLEL`/`ANY` stage, `signature={meaning:verify}`) under a NEW `WorkflowSubjectType.LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION`; the decision rides the existing `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` (a new dispatch branch → `decide_leadership_authorization`, which allow-lists `{verify,reject}` AFTER the keyless candidate-pool auth gate and forces `REJECTED`+skips siblings on a decisive decline). The COMPLETING `verify` mints a SINGLE `signature_event(meaning=verify, signed_object_type=document_version, signed_object_id=<version>)` bound to the EXISTING version row (NO own-table stage-event → **no two-INSERT seam**, unlike CAPA/initiative) + a first-class `EventType.LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZED` audit (object_type=`version`); the document FSM is **untouched** (release is the separate act the cutover gates). Plus a `GET /documents/{id}/leadership-authorization` status read (`{is_leadership_artifact, required, version_id, authorized, instance}`). **Authority = Top-Management candidate-pool membership (NO new permission key — R38; the self-scoped-task doctrine); the REQUEST reuses `document.approve`.** **Migration 0054** (head `0053→0054`): the two enum `ADD VALUE`s (`workflow_subject_type`→`LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION`, `event_type`→`LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZED`) in an `autocommit_block` so the new subject-type commits before the seed uses it (the 0053 ordering rule); `signed_object_type=document_version` + the `verify` meaning are **REUSED** (no enum adds there — R2 closed-but-additive); an `ALTER TABLE system_config ADD COLUMN … boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` (mirrored in the ORM); and a seed-only `leadership_release_authorization` workflow_definition + its `leadership_authorization` stage **reusing the 0038 "Top Management" role** (NOT reseeded). Round-trips up↔down↔`alembic check` clean; NOT-EXISTS-guarded downgrade. **OpenAPI:** the two new document endpoints + 4 schemas (`LeadershipAuthorizationRequest`/`Task`/`Cycle`/`Status`), `LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION` added to `WorkflowInstance.subject_type`, the config flag on `OrgConfig`/`OrgConfigUpdate`. **The Codex saga (5 findings / 2 rounds — a CLEAN diff-critic + migration-reviewer + all local gates missed every one; the edge-finder again):** **round 1 (3×P2 + 1×P3):** (a) the single-active guard only blocks NON-terminal instances → a 2nd request after a COMPLETED authorization (pre-release) mints a DUPLICATE `verify` sig → the `scalar_one_or_none()` replay re-derivation 500s → fixed by guarding the request with `has_release_authorization` (409 `already_authorized`; **version-scoped**, so a NEW Approved version still re-requests); (b) the new `WorkflowSubjectType` must be added to the openapi `WorkflowInstance.subject_type` enum (`GET /workflow-instances/{id}` + `GET /tasks/{id}` serialize it → a generated client would reject the response); (c) the decision result used `version_id` but `DecisionResult` is `additionalProperties:false` and defines `document_version_id` → renamed the result key (COMPLETE + replay) + the tests; (d/P3) a decisive reject left `stage_state=PENDING` while forcing `current_state=REJECTED` → set `stage_state=FAILED`. **round 2 (1×P2):** the **DCR-implement go-live** of a leadership artifact runs the cutover only later in the async `release_due` sweep, which CATCHES the gate's `ProblemException` and skips → `implement_dcr` would commit the DCR as Implemented while the version stays Approved (false success, stuck) → extracted the gate to the shared `assert_release_authorized` (the cutover delegates) and **preflight it synchronously in `implement_dcr`** before scheduling `effective_from`/committing. ⚠ **Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the ANY-quorum + outcome-allow-list pair from S-improvement-4 carry verbatim** — allow-list `{verify,reject}` AFTER the keyless candidate-pool gate (else a generic positive mints a spurious verify; a pre-auth 422 leaks the task), and an ANY decline is NOT decisive in the engine → force `REJECTED`+skip siblings in the caller. (2) **the release-gate read of the hot shared `system_config` row lives in the SERIALIZABLE `_cutover`** — acceptable (the integration suite is sequential per pytest-split shard; a genuinely concurrent `/admin/config` write would 40001 a release, which is retryable), but a v1.x option is to read the flag pre-cutover. (3) **POL is `is_singleton=True` (R25)** — the shared integration org tolerates exactly ONE Effective POL, so the **full release→Effective happy-path was put on NON-singleton OBJ**; POL covers only the gate-blocked-409 + non-releasing assertions (it is never pushed Effective). (4) **a new `WorkflowSubjectType` whose `subject_id` is a `documented_information` id needs NO `subject_label`/My-Tasks change** — the existing DocumentedInformation fallthrough/outerjoin already resolves it. **Deferred (named-not-faked):** the **front-end** (request/decide UI + the release-gate affordance) — the next slice; **`quorum: ALL`** (doc 10 §2.5's worked example — shipped as `ANY`, consistent with the CAPA `crit_topmgmt` + initiative precedent); the **import-baseline path** is intentionally ungated (a baseline import is not a release; it never hits `_cutover`); a dedicated **DCR-implement-of-a-leadership-artifact** integration test (the preflight reuses the gate proven by the direct/OBJ/MR tests; a clean DCR-revise-of-a-leadership-doc fixture is high-cost — POL is singleton, OBJ/MR have bespoke revision flows). **Test delta: +12 api integration** (`test_leadership_authorization.py`: OBJ full request→verify→release-Effective with the verify signature + LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZED audit; flag-off ungated; POL recognized + release-blocked-409; ordinary-doc [SOP] untouched with the flag on; request guards [not-leadership / not-approved / twice / already-authorized]; decline-decisive + re-requestable + allow-list-422; non-member 404-collapse; idempotent verify replay; MR release-gated). **web unchanged** (backend-only). Full unit `808 passed`; migration round-trip + `alembic check` clean; redocly valid; ruff + mypy-strict clean (only the pre-existing Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` source nit). **diff-critic + migration-reviewer CLEAN** pre-PR. **Merge gate:** all Codex threads addressed across 2 rounds + green CI (11/11) + owner's explicit go. PR [#190](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/190), squash `9ee99b2`.

## v1.x RENDER HARDENING — pre-render linked-resource detection + gotenberg 8.34 (no migration)

- **S-render-1** (detect externally-linked Office resources before render → R26 source-only, then adopt gotenberg 8.34) — **closes a WORM/mirror integrity hazard the 8.34 bump introduces.** **Why:** gotenberg 8.34 changed LibreOffice conversion so external/local **linked** resources (`http(s)://`, `file://`, UNC `\\host\share`, drive/POSIX-absolute, and external-mode *relative* targets) still convert (HTTP 200) but are **no longer rendered into the PDF**. The worker (`GotenbergRenderSink`) caches any successful convert as the mirror's CONTROLLED COPY, so a doc referencing a linked logo/include/picture would silently cache an **INCOMPLETE** controlled copy — a violation of "the controlled copy is a faithful rendition of the controlled source." So before any convert, the worker runs a structural scan; a linked source is marked **non-renderable (R26, doc 04 §11.4)** → the mirror keeps source bytes + `no_controlled_rendition` instead of a lossy PDF. The gotenberg 8.34 adoption (declined earlier as Dependabot #157, pending exactly this guard) ships in the SAME PR. **100% BACKEND-ONLY** — **no migration** (head stays `0052`), **no new permission key / endpoint / OpenAPI contract** (gate = `/check-api` + `/check-migrations` n/a). **What shipped:** a NEW pure-stdlib module `services/vault/linked_resources.py::scan_linked_resources(mime, source_bytes) -> LinkScan(has_external_links, reason)` (mirrors the `domain/ingestion/minhash.py` house rules: **pure / no-I/O / stdlib-only** [`zipfile`/`re`/`xml.etree`] / **bounded** [8 MB member cap, 4 MiB RTF/OLE prefix, 512-member + 64 MB zip budgets] / **ReDoS-safe** [no nested quantifiers, anchored bounded classes] / **XXE-closed** [refuses any `<!DOCTYPE` before the default non-fetching expat parser — no defusedxml, D4] / **fail-open** [any parse error → `LinkScan(False)`, defer to the normal render path]). Routing: RTF + legacy-OLE by mime; **OOXML/ODF by CONTAINER CONTENT** (a top-level `content.xml` → ODF scan; `[Content_Types].xml`/any `*.rels` → OOXML scan — NOT a fixed mime allowlist, so every `.dotx/.xltx/.potx/.ppsx`/`.ott/.ots/.otp/.odg` variant the render path converts is inspected). **Hyperlinks are EXCLUDED** (OOXML `Type=.../hyperlink`, ODF `text:a`/`draw:a`, RTF `HYPERLINK` command) — 8.34 renders a clickable annotation fine, and flagging them would source-only nearly every real document. **Doctrine direction:** a false-positive is SAFE (→ R26 source-only, source always retained); a false-negative is the hazard (an incomplete cached copy). **Wiring (threading unchanged across all rounds):** scan runs in `GotenbergRenderSink.render` AFTER `_is_non_renderable`, BEFORE `_convert`; `RenderResult.reason` (new field) → `_resolve_rendition`'s 5-tuple → `mirror._metadata` writes `no_controlled_rendition_reason` into `metadata.json` for the auditor. The api process holds the no-op `LoggingRenderSink`, so this is worker/CLI-only (the S-dcr-3b rendering-is-worker-only invariant). **The 6-round Codex saga (the load-bearing story):** an inherently-imperfect heuristic over UNTRUSTED Office formats kept surfacing safe-direction edges — Codex findings ran **7→6→3→6→3→5 across rounds 1–6** (severity decaying P1→P2), and round-6 was 4/5 RE-RAISES of already-decided dispositions. The fixes that landed: hyperlinks excluded (r1); 7 false-negatives closed [INCLUDEPICTURE/INCLUDETEXT match anywhere, LINK only in field-context, case-insensitive, External-mode relative targets, variant mimes] (r2); **parse-and-concatenate split `<w:instrText>` runs** [Word splits `INCLUDE`+`PICTURE` across adjacent runs → a raw-text regex misses it] + ODF embedded-subdocument dir-prefix membership [`./Object 1` stored as `Object 1/content.xml`] + footnote/endnote/comment story parts (r3); **route ODF by top-level `content.xml` first** + scan `.rels` before the budget break + **bounded RTF control words** between `\fldinst` and the command [`\fldinst \lang1033\rtlch INCLUDEPICTURE`] (r4); **independent per-category member budgets** [rels vs field-code parts each get `_MAX_ZIP_MEMBERS` — fixes the symmetric starvation the r4 rels-first sort introduced] (r5); **scan BOTH ODF+OOXML when both zip fingerprints present** [OR-ed, short-circuit — a crafted OOXML with a dummy `content.xml` no longer bypasses its `.rels` scan; supersedes the r4 either/or routing] (r6). ⚠ **Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **Codex caught ~17 real scanner edge-cases across 6 rounds that CLEAN diff-critic passes missed** — on a heuristic over untrusted/adversarial input, the diff-critic is necessary but NOT sufficient; the adversarial PR reviewer is the real edge-finder. (2) **It does not converge** — past ~round 4 Codex re-raises the same documented residuals (incl. the owner's own fail-open tradeoffs framed as findings); the discipline is to TRIAGE (fix genuinely-new high-value, respond/defer the rest) and ASK THE OWNER for the merge decision rather than loop. (3) **the auto-formatter strips a just-added unused import** — `import pytest` added BEFORE its first `@pytest.mark.parametrize` use was removed by the PostToolUse ruff hook; add the usage first or re-add after (the recurring S-statusbadge-2 trap). (4) **rels-first ordering is a half-fix** — preferring the most-reliable signal under a SHARED budget starves the other category; the right shape is INDEPENDENT per-category budgets. **Owner decisions:** (a) **KEEP FAIL-OPEN** for a VALID zip whose part is uninspectable (DOCTYPE-bearing or oversized member) or a truncated RTF/legacy prefix — explicitly chosen over fail-closed (D1 trusted authors; source always retained → worst case is an incomplete COPY for an uncommon shape, never lost content; a fail-closed switch stays an easy follow-up). (b) **fix-high-value / defer-rest** triage for rounds 4–6. **Deferred (named-not-faked) → v1.x hardening:** RTF/legacy >4 MiB streaming/chunked scan with overlap (a marker after a huge embedded-hex picture is missed); a ZIP entry-enumeration cap (stdlib `ZipFile` parses the whole central directory on open regardless, so capping `namelist()` can't reduce the dominant cost without a custom incremental reader — D4); a legacy-OLE **drive-path** (`C:\…`) marker (a raw-byte marker would false-positive on the ubiquitous embedded template/author paths every `.doc` carries → needs structural CFB/OLE2 moniker parsing). **By-design (not a bug):** cached-rendition recheck — a cached `rendition_blob_sha256` was produced by the pre-8.34 gotenberg (complete copy), and the single-host Compose deploy (D4) restarts the image + scanner together (no rollout window), so a cache hit correctly returns a complete copy; only a cache MISS runs 8.34 + the scan. **Test delta: +55 api unit** (new `test_linked_resources.py` = **53**: OOXML/ODF/RTF/legacy-OLE + variant mimes + corrupt/fail-open/bounded + every round's regression; **+2** `test_render.py` short-circuit/clean-convert) **+ 1 integration** (`test_render.py` linked-Office → `no_controlled_rendition`); **web unchanged** (backend-only). Full unit `800 passed / 18 skipped` (Windows; 17 POSIX skips + 1 release-ceremony). **diff-critic CLEAN** on rounds 3 & 4 (round-5/6 self-verified + Codex-reviewed). **Merge gate:** all Codex threads resolved + 0 unresolved + green CI (11/11) + owner's explicit go. PR [#180](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/180), squash `97f4192`. (Rides atop the merged Phase-2 design-critique work + the fully-drained Dependabot queue; gotenberg 8.34 was declined as Dependabot #157 pending this slice.)

## v1.x DESIGN-CRITIQUE remediation (whole-app `/impeccable` P1s, baseline 26/40) — systematising the slice-by-slice SPA

- **S-design-p4** (the design-critique **P2/P3 polish tail** — the named follow-up S-design-p3 left open: the compact inline-state primitive + the Skeleton-list loader for the deferred idiom families, plus the residual Drift "Failing" glyph + the as-of-clock consistency gap) — **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** — no migration (head stays `0055`), no key/endpoint/contract; gate = `/check-web`. **Three new `lib/states.tsx` primitives (siblings of the four page-level ones from S-design-p3):** **`InlineState({kind, children, onRetry?})`** — the compact in-tab / in-drawer / in-card `<Text size="sm">` idiom (`loading`→`role="status"` dimmed live region, `forbidden`/`empty`→dimmed, `error`→red + an OPTIONAL inline "Try again" mirroring `ErrorState.onRetry`); **`SkeletonList({rows, height, gap?, label?, role?})`** — N stacked `<Skeleton>` rows for table loaders, ALWAYS a named `role="status"` region (an `aria-label` on a roleless container is an axe `aria-prohibited-attr` violation — hanging it off `role="status"` FIXES the prior nameless `LibraryPage`/`IngestionRunsPage` loaders); **`MutationErrorState({title, error, fallback?})`** — unwraps `ApiError.message` centrally for the calm red `<Alert>` on a failed write (the write-side sibling of `ErrorState`). **Sweeps (size-faithful — the load-bearing discriminator):** `InlineState` forces `size="sm"`, so it was adopted **ONLY where the original was already `size="sm"`** (in-tab/drawer/card/modal) — **8 sites:** `document/HistoryTab`, `RedlineViewer`, `WhereUsedTab`, `ApprovalsTab`, `VisualDiffViewer` (its inline 403/error guards ONLY — the Pending/Failed long-op render card stays bespoke), `AcknowledgementsTab`, `dcr/DcrImpactTable`, `dcr/ImplementCreateDcrModal`. `SkeletonList` → **3:** `library/LibraryPage`, `ingestion/TriageTable`, `ingestion/IngestionRunsPage`. `MutationErrorState` → **5 audits:** `CorrectFindingModal`, `ProgramForm`, `PlanForm`, `NewAuditModal` (ONLY the `create.isError` block; the sibling `programs.isError` read-Alert left as-is), `LogFindingModal`. **Two deliberate consistency fixes (the only behaviour changes):** `AcknowledgementsTab`'s matrix non-forbidden load error went dimmed→red (`kind="error"`) to match its sibling `dist` error which was already red; its two "Loading…" texts went default-size→`size="sm"` to match their `size="sm"` siblings. **Drift DP-5:** `DriftStatusPage`'s `Failing: {n}` count now carries the canonical danger **✕** glyph (`aria-hidden`, on the AA `--es-danger-text` token per the S-obj-rag dark-glyph rule — a glyph filled with the base hue would be the low-contrast mark) when `n>0`, legible by shape + label not colour alone; neutral at 0. The prominent red Alert above it is unchanged. **As-of clocks:** `<AsOf at={dataUpdatedAt} />` added beneath the page header (mirroring `ObjectivesRegisterPage`) to the **9 register pages** that lacked one — `AuditsListPage`, `ImprovementRegisterPage`, `DcrsRegisterPage`, `ManagementReviewsRegisterPage`, `NcrsPage`, `ComplaintsPage`, `CapaBoardPage`, `SupersededCopiesPage`, `IngestionRunsPage` — the hooks already spread `...query`, so `dataUpdatedAt` was present with **NO hook changes**. **Owner forks (AskUserQuestion up-front):** fold in ALL 9 register pages for as-of (vs a 3-page subset/defer); INCLUDE a shared `MutationErrorState` (vs defer the write-error family). **⚠ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the size-fidelity boundary IS the adopt/skip discriminator** — `InlineState` is `size="sm"`, so adopting it on a page-level default-size `<Text c="dimmed/red">` (the `/tasks`+`/acks` inboxes, `DcrDiffPage`, the `LibraryPage` error line) would SHRINK page-level text — the S-design-p3 "preserve sizes" rule applied as the gate; those stay as-is (deferred-as-idiom-mismatch). (2) **the Drift failing-glyph COLLIDED with the existing tests** — the default `driftStatusFixture` has `failing>0` AND a `DIVERGENT` badge, so adding a 2nd danger `✕` made `getByText(TONE_GLYPH.danger)` multi-match → re-scope the 2 existing badge-glyph assertions via `within(badge)` (the glyph is a `leftSection` span INSIDE the labelled `<Badge>`) and pin the new failing-count tests to a CONTROLLED fixture (both scans `CLEAN` / `BLOB_REHASH:null`) so the only `✕` is the count's. (3) `InlineState.onRetry` is **tested but unwired** in this sweep (a behaviour-preserving consolidation; the inline retry mirrors `ErrorState` and is there for future use) — diff-critic + web-test-trap both flagged it as a benign observation, not a defect. **Execution:** built the 3 primitives + their `states.test.tsx` tests MYSELF (single editor = no cross-partition drift; the primitives own their defaults, so no `EmptyState`-size-style trap can recur) and did the InlineState/SkeletonList/MutationErrorState/Drift sweeps inline; fanned out ONLY the 8 as-of edits to a **4-agent wave** (disjoint files, mechanical — each adds `dataUpdatedAt` + `<AsOf>`, self-checks scoped eslint), then reconciled + ran the full gate centrally. The UNDERSTAND phase was a **6-reader Workflow** mapping the deferred idiom families. **Deferred (named-not-faked):** the page-level default-size inbox text (`TasksInbox`/`AckInbox`) + `DcrDiffPage` + the `LibraryPage` error line (idiom + size mismatch — converting shrinks); **not-found** panels (intentionally gray + back-link, distinct from a retryable read error); the `DocumentDetailPage`/`VisualDiffViewer` bespoke COMPOSITE skeletons (header+grid+block / two-panel — a generic `SkeletonList` can't preserve the layout coherence); the `setError` imperative try/catch error sites (improvement/authoring/`SpawnDcrModal` — a different idiom storing a string, not a react-query `.isError`); `AuditLifecyclePanel`'s deliberately-orange advance error; the Home tile vocabulary (`TileNoAccess`/`TileSkeleton` — already idiomatic). **Test delta: web 1071→1080 (+9):** +7 states-primitive tests in `states.test.tsx` (InlineState per-kind / loading-role / retry-wired / no-retry; SkeletonList rows-in-named-region; MutationErrorState ApiError-unwrap / fallback; + the axe block extended) + 2 Drift failing-glyph tests in `DriftStatusPage.test.tsx` (✕ present `>0` / neutral `=0`); 2 existing Drift badge-glyph assertions re-scoped via `within()`. `/check-web` green (eslint + strict `tsc` + `vite build` + **1080/1080** via `--pool=forks --singleFork`); CI **11/11**. **diff-critic CLEAN** (all 31 conversions traced faithful; the 2 named fixes are the only behaviour changes; AsOf placement after every early-return; Drift glyph decorative + AA-token) **and web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN** (every new assertion MUTATION-verified real, no false-PASS, no broken queries); **Codex CLEAN** ("Didn't find any major issues. Delightful!"). **Merge gate:** green CI + diff-critic/web-test-trap/Codex all clean + owner's explicit go. - **S-design-p3** (the FINAL design-critique **Phase-3** remainder — closes the three named Phase-3 items the tracker still had open: **(A)** the shared loading/error/empty primitives + the real `useAckCount` silent-zero bug, **(B)** the PDCA-grouped nav rail + an in-product glyph legend, **(C)** the residual non-badge `▲`) — **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** — no migration (head stays `0055`), no key/endpoint/contract; gate = `/check-web`. **(A) shipped:** new `lib/states.tsx` — `LoadingState` (centered `role="status"` + an accessible name; the old bare `<Loader/>` announced nothing), `ErrorState` (red Alert **+ a "Try again" button** wired to the query's `refetch` — the affordance every hand-rolled error panel LACKED), `NoAccessState` (gray Alert, "No access" title OWNED by the primitive), `EmptyState` (dimmed body-size text + optional action). **Swept across 39 feature files / 85 sites**, each preserving its surrounding Container/Card/Title chrome + verbatim copy. (2) `useDebouncedSearch` **clobbered an EXTERNAL `?q` change** (back/forward, a same-route link) — because **react-router's `setSearchParams` is NOT referentially stable** (it changes on every location change), a write effect keyed on it re-fired on the external change with the stale local value. ⚠ Two insufficient fixes were caught by the new regression test before the right one: a naive `setQ(urlQ)` sync (a same-commit clobber survives), then a `debounced === q` guard (the unstable-setter re-fire survives) → the landing fix **refs both `urlQ` + `setUrlQ` and keys the write effect on `debounced` ONLY**. ## v1.x DCR UI track — clause §10→§7.5 change control — surfaces the built-but-UI-less DCR domain in the SPA (read spine first)

- **S-dcr-target-typeahead (A3)** server-driven debounced DCR raise target picker — **CLOSES the last-named DCR ui-2a residual** (the target-picker large-list typeahead that S-dcr-ui-2a/S-doc-filters both explicitly deferred: the raise REVISE/RETIRE target `Select` in `DcrRaiseFields` fetched `useDocuments({current_state:"Effective"},{limit:200})` + filtered CLIENT-SIDE by label, so a target beyond the 200-row cap was unreachable for any org with >200 Effective controlled docs). **BACKEND + FE, migration-free, no permission key** (head stays `0055`, next `0056`; rides `document.read`); gates `/check-api` + `/check-contracts` + `/check-web`. **Owner design fork (asked in-plan, A vs B vs a discovered C):** **A — add a top-level `q` to `GET /documents` (substring ILIKE)** — chosen over **B** (the FTS `GET /search`: heavier `snippet`/`rank`/`clause_refs` shape + `websearch_to_tsquery` semantics, awkward for picking an exact doc by an identifier fragment) and **C** (reuse the existing `GET /search/suggest` typeahead — already Effective-only + documents-only + `document.read`-filtered + `{id,identifier,title}`-shaped, BUT its `_SUGGEST_SQL` is a **prefix** match `'<term>%'`, so reusing it would REGRESS finding `SOP-PUR-014` by typing `PUR`, and broadening it to substring would alter the shared ⌘K `CommandPalette`). ⚠ **#138 was NOT a typeahead precedent** (it added the boolean `has_effective_version`/`managed_subtype` *filters*; `ImplementCreateDcrModal` is still client-`searchable`) → there was **no existing server-typeahead picker to mirror**; the only debounced-server-query precedent is `CommandPalette` + `useSuggest`. **Backend:** `list_documents` gains an optional **top-level `q`** (a sibling of `limit`/`offset`, **NOT** part of the `filter[…][…]` eq/has/gte/lte grammar → `_FILTER_ALLOW` untouched, no `unknown_filter` risk) → a case-insensitive **substring** `or_(identifier.ilike, title.ilike)` with pattern `%term%`, wildcards neutralised by a new **`_ilike_escape`** (backslash-first, mirrors `services/search/indexer.py`) + `escape="\\"`, **appended to the `filters` list so it ANDs** with the bracketed grammar + the `org_id`/`kind=DOCUMENT` scope. A blank/whitespace `q` adds **no condition** → byte-identical for the Library + every other `useDocuments` caller. ⚠ **the `document.read` per-row authz filter is unchanged and REMAINS the security boundary** — `q` only narrows the candidate window (UX narrowing, never a visibility change); the backend `_resolve_target` stays the submit-time correctness guard (a REVISE/RETIRE target must be a controlled Document, not a Record). **FE (`DcrRaiseFields`, the single shared component → one change covers Raise + BOTH SpawnDcrModal seams [CAPA + MR-output]):** a 200ms `useDebouncedValue(search)` drives `useDocuments({current_state:"Effective", q: debounced.trim()||undefined},{limit:20})`; **react-query keys by `q`, so a slow earlier response can't clobber a newer one — the hand-rolled stale-guard the `CommandPalette` needs is a non-issue by construction**; Mantine's client filter is disabled (`filter={({options})=>options}`, server already narrowed) and the redundant `kind==="DOCUMENT"` client filter is dropped (server excludes Records); a `Loader` `rightSection` while fetching + an `isError`-aware `nothingFoundMessage` (calm degrade, never crash). The **picked option is unioned into the data** so its label survives a later narrower search (the Codex stale-row edge), **gated on `selected.value === value.target_document_id`** so a stale pick goes inert the instant the parent nulls the target on a CREATE switch (no orphan can leak — derived, no effect). The `CREATE⟺no-target` biconditional (`isDcrFieldsValid`) + the RETIRE-clears-date logic are untouched. ⚠ **The reset story took a mutation-testing pass:** an initial `useEffect` to clear the search on the CREATE switch was a **genuine NO-OP** — Mantine **remounts** the inner `Select` on the CREATE→REVISE round-trip (and fires `onSearchChange("")` on the fresh mount), so the search already resets; it couldn't be discriminatingly tested → **removed it**, and the only real lingering-state path (a stale *committed* pick after a CREATE clear) is closed by the `selected.value === target` union gate instead. ⚠ **Web test traps carried:** (1) the **debounce timing trap** — `SOP-PUR-014` is present in BOTH the `q=""` and `q="PUR"` pages, so `findByRole(PUR)` is a FALSE gate (it matches the pre-narrow list); the real narrowing SIGNAL is `QMS`-gone **AND** `PUR`-present asserted in ONE `waitFor` (retries through the `q=""` both-present state + the in-flight loader blank); (2) the **ruff PostToolUse hook strips a just-added unused import** (the `_ilike_escape` test import) — append the body FIRST, re-add the import AFTER (the recurring trap); (3) MSW fixtures `satisfies DocumentSummary`/`DocumentsPage` pinned to the real `_document` serializer + the real `{limit,offset,returned,has_more}` page envelope (the old fixture's `total` was fictional); (4) both the union test AND the orphan-guard test are **mutation-verified** (each fails when its mechanism is removed). **Reviews:** diff-critic = CLEAN; **web-test-trap-reviewer 2 rounds — both findings the no-op reset effect + the uncovered `selected.value===target` union guard were resolved with mutation-verified discriminating tests** (the round-2 catch: deleting the guard clause kept the suite green → added a "stale pick not re-offered after a CREATE clear" test that fails without it); **Codex CLEAN ("Didn't find any major issues. Swish!")** on the final commit. **Deferred (named, not faked):** true paging / infinite-scroll in the picker (a debounced typeahead + a 20-row page is sufficient — a target is found by typing, not scrolling; the `document.read` row-filter + the `_resolve_target` guard keep it safe regardless); **diacritics-insensitive search** (ILIKE is ASCII-case-only — `unaccent`/a trigram index is a v1.x refinement, the same note S-doc-filters carried); the **CREATE-implement picker** (`ImplementCreateDcrModal`) left on its #138 server-narrowed client-`searchable` form (its never-released-Approved candidate set is small + already server-narrowed — the owner scoped this slice to the raise picker only). **Test deltas: +2 api unit** (`test_documents_filters.py` — `_ilike_escape` leaves plain text untouched + neutralises `% _ \`, order-correct) **+2 api integration** (`test_documents_list.py` — run-scoped via `owner_user_id`+salted titles: substring narrowing over identifier AND title / case-insensitive / identifier-vs-title isolation / non-match→empty; `%`-escaping doesn't broaden + `q` ANDs with `filter[current_state][eq]`; **CI-authoritative on this Windows box**); **web 1045→1050 (+5:** DcrRaiseFields 2→6 [debounced narrowing, re-show-clean-after-CREATE, union persistence, orphan-guard], useDocuments 6→7 [top-level `q` emission / omitted-when-blank]). **Verified:** `/check-web` (eslint + strict tsc + build + 1050 vitest, full run via `--pool=forks --singleFork`) · `/check-api` fast (ruff + format + mypy-strict; only the known Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline) · `/check-contracts` (redocly valid; `q` documented as a top-level optional string) — all green; **CI all 11 checks green incl. all 4 integration shards.** PR [#203](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/203), squash `ed4af1d`. **The DCR-UI track now has NO open named residuals.**

- **S-doc-filters** server-side CREATE-picker candidate filters on `GET /documents` — **closes the CREATE-picker half of the long-named picker-pagination v1.x deferral** (the ui-2a/ui-4 first-page-only gap). A cross-cutting `/documents`-API + library-hook slice serving the DCR CREATE-implement picker. **BACKEND + FE, migration-free, no key/enum** (head stays `0051`, catalog 100); gates `/check-api` + `/check-contracts` + `/check-web`. Two opt-in, boolean, `eq`-only filters added to the bracketed grammar in `api/documents.py`: **`filter[has_effective_version][eq]`** (→ `current_effective_version_id IS NULL`/`IS NOT NULL`) and **`filter[managed_subtype][eq]`** (→ `~(EXISTS quality_objective OR EXISTS management_review)` — a shared-PK `NOT EXISTS`; **F2: chosen over a doc-type-code exclude so it's immune to type-code renames** — OBJ/MR carry no discriminator column on `documented_information`). New `_parse_filter_bool` (422 `validation_error` on non-`true`/`false`); `_FILTER_ALLOW` + two `_filter_condition` branches + `or_`/`QualityObjective`/`ManagementReview` imports; **`list_documents`/the limit clamp/`_LIST_SCAN_CAP`/per-row authz untouched**. The CREATE picker (`ImplementCreateDcrModal`) now passes `{has_effective_version:false, managed_subtype:false}`; its client-side `.filter` + `useDocumentTypes`/`managedTypeIds` are DELETED; `DocumentFilters` += two optional booleans; `buildDocumentsQuery` emits each **only when `!== undefined`**. **Owner F-decisions:** **F1 = CREATE picker ONLY** (the ui-2a target picker [`DcrRaiseFields`, Effective docs] is OUT — narrowing can't help a picker that *wants* Effective docs; its fix is server-side typeahead, deferred); **F3 = bracketed grammar, default-off** (omitted-when-unset → the other `GET /documents` consumers — the Library page + the ui-2a DCR target picker — are byte-unaffected; ⚠ global search is **NOT** a `/documents` consumer, it hits OpenSearch `/search`). ⚠ **KEY framing: PURE UX, not a correctness fix** — `services/dcr/service.py::_resolve_implement_version` already rejects an invalid CREATE target (`create_target_not_new`/`create_target_managed_subtype`) regardless of the picker (the S-dcr-ui-4 server guard); this slice only stops invalid candidates from *appearing*. ⚠ **Traps a future session must carry:** (1) the **FE false-emit trap** — a boolean default-off query filter MUST emit on `!== undefined`, never `if (filters.x)` (else `false` is silently dropped — the CREATE picker sends `false`); (2) the **managed-subtype exclusion has no discriminator column** (OBJ/MR are shared-PK subtype rows) → `NOT EXISTS` against the subtype tables, not a doc-type-code exclude; (3) **diff-critic compiling the REAL route query** proved the `EXISTS` correlates correctly when spread via `*filters` — a standalone `_filter_condition` compile shows a *misleading uncorrelated cartesian* (a SQLAlchemy auto-correlation artifact resolved at embedding), so verify correlation on the assembled `select`, not the bare condition; (4) **backend live smoke on this Windows box** (PG not host-published, worker runs baked images) — ran the new query SHAPE inside the running worker via a `docker exec -i easysynq-worker-1 sh -c 'cd /app && uv run python -'` heredoc against live PG (**no image rebuild when you INLINE the query** instead of importing the new code): the partition `narrowed+excluded==approved` held and `managed_subtype=true` (8) matched the OBJ(5)+MR(3) subtype-join ground truth exactly. **Deferred (named, not faked):** the ui-2a target-picker large-list typeahead (needs server-side text search — a new length-capped ILIKE facet or OpenSearch `/search` reuse); true paging/infinite-scroll in the pickers (narrowing keeps the CREATE set under the 100-clamp; the `_resolve_implement_version` guard keeps it safe regardless). **+14 api unit (`tests/unit/test_documents_filters.py`) + 2 api integration (`test_documents_list.py` — the four-shape narrowing matrix [Effective-initial / Approved-new / Approved-revision-of-Effective / OBJ] + a non-boolean→422); web 866→869** (the false-emit triple + the modal request-URL + server-trust tests replacing two obsolete client-filter tests). diff-critic + web-test-trap CLEAN; CI 9/9; Codex CLEAN round 1. subagent-driven TDD (3 parallel tasks + per-task quality review, all clean). PR [#138](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/138), squash `8eaaf98`. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-14-s-doc-filters-create-picker*`.

+ FE picker filters (`current_effective_version_id === null` + exclude OBJ/MR document-types via `useDocumentTypes`, FRM and other plain controlled docs stay valid) so invalid candidates never appear. the client-side filters could hide a valid page-2 candidate) — the same v1.x limitation as the S-dcr-ui-2a target picker; **the server-side guard makes it safe** (validity is *enforced* regardless of the picker; full-navigate deep-link redirects to Home; the page token is blocked by the privacy guardrail) — so the FE rendering is covered by the unit tests + the web-test-trap-reviewer's real-serializer fixture cross-check. **Reviews:** diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer **CLEAN**;
