- **S-dcr-impact-annotation + the `CapaApprovalContext` a11y follow-up** — two small follow-ups closing two named residuals of the (now-complete) DCR-UI track; both **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** (no migration, no permission key, no new endpoint, no contract change; gate = `/check-web` only — head stays `0051`).
  - **#132 — inline annotation of the 7 DCR impact dimensions.** The SPA could *view* a DCR's impact dimensions (the ui-1 read-only `DcrImpactTable`) but not *annotate* them; this wires the requester annotation through the already-built **`PUT /dcrs/{id}/impact`** (S-dcr-3b/-5 — the service `annotate_impact` is a **partial merge**: it sets `requester_annotation` only on the dimensions present in the body dict, leaves `auto_populated` untouched, emits `DCR_UPDATED`, has **no FSM-state gate** — it only requires the impact rows to exist; unknown dimension → 422 `unknown_dimension`, an un-assessed dimension → 409 `impact_not_assessed`, both unreachable from the UI which only edits existing rows). **Owner F-decisions (2026-06-14, after verifying the backend):** F1 — the Annotation column is editable when **`impact.length > 0 && <capability> && state ∉ {Closed,Cancelled,Rejected}`** (matches the backend's permissiveness — a requester/approver can refine annotations right up through approval, where they inform the decision; only the three terminals hide it, where an edit is pointless); F2 — **inline-editable cells + one batch Save** (the Annotation cells become `Textarea`s; a single "Save annotations" button PUTs only the changed dimensions), not a modal. **The slice:** `lib/api.ts` `api.send`/`apiSend` method union widened `+"PUT"` (additive — existing callers byte-unaffected); `useAnnotateImpact(id)` (`PUT … {annotations}`, **`onSuccess` writes the PUT response into the `["dcr-impact",id]` cache via `setQueryData(resp.data)`** + invalidates `["dcr",id]` — non-optimistic, the server returns the refreshed rows); `DcrImpactTable` gains an editable path; `DcrDrawer` passes `editable={(impact?.length ?? 0) > 0 && dcr.capabilities?.assess === true && !["Closed","Cancelled","Rejected"].includes(dcr.state)}`. ⚠ **The editor draft-state design took FIVE Codex P2/P1 rounds — the landed answer is "KEY the editor, never reconcile server↔draft with a render-sync effect":** **(1)** the original spec gated on the SYSTEM-scoped `can("changeRequest.assess")` → Codex steered it to **`dcr.capabilities?.assess`** (PROCESS-scoped — the ui-2b `_dcr_capabilities` precedent; a PROCESS/DOC_CLASS grant-holder is no longer hidden); **(2)** a naïve re-seed on every `impact`-prop change **lost the user's unsaved edits on a background refetch** → preserve unsaved edits across an identical refetch (+ a fixture trap: order the MSW impact handler before the detail one); **(3)** but then a genuine server change (another user annotated) wouldn't surface on a **pristine** draft → adopt fresh server values when the draft is pristine; **(4)+(5)** the converging fix that subsumed (2)/(3) and killed a **cross-DCR leak** (a dirty draft for DCR-A surviving a switch to DCR-B → Save would PUT to the wrong DCR) and a **post-save stale window**: the read-only `<DcrImpactTable>` delegates the editable path to a child **`EditableImpactTable` keyed on `` `${dcrId}::${annotationSignature(impact)}` ``** (signature = `id=requester_annotation` joined over the rows). The key **remounts** (re-seeds a plain `useState` draft) on ANY genuine server change — a different DCR, a content refetch that changed a value, or **our own post-save `setQueryData` cache write** — but NOT on an identical background refetch (same signature → same key → edits preserved). So the editor holds a plain local draft with **zero server↔draft reconciliation**; Save computes `draft[dim] !== seed[dim]` and sends only the changed subset, disabled when nothing changed; a calm inline error on failure. Paired with the cache-write `onSuccess` there is **no stale-refetch window** (the saved values are in cache before any refetch, and they change the signature → the editor remounts to them). **Reviews:** diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN; **5 Codex P2/P1 rounds all fixed + threads resolved** (gate-scope, MSW order, dirty-loss, pristine-clobber, cross-DCR leak, post-save stale). **Live smoke (Chrome MCP):** edited one Annotation cell → Save → confirmed the PUT carried exactly the one changed dimension and the value persisted on re-open. **Test delta: web 842→852 (+10).** PR [#132](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/132), squash `e6b8256`. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-14-s-dcr-impact-annotation*`.
  - **#131 — `CapaApprovalContext` heading-order a11y fix** (a parked residual flagged during ui-2b). The `/tasks` CAPA approval context skipped the page h2 straight to h4 (missing h3) — the **same** heading-order skip already fixed in `DcrApprovalContext` during ui-2b. Bumped `CapaApprovalContext`'s levels h4/h5 → h3/h4 + added a page-context CAPA **jest-axe smoke** (failing-first on the old levels) so it can't regress. FE-only; touches `features/review/CapaApprovalContext.tsx` + `ReviewApprovePage.test.tsx`. **Test delta: web 841→842 (+1).** PR [#131](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/131), squash `e377492`.
  - **After these two, the DCR-UI track has exactly ONE residual remaining: C — CREATE-implement / the CREATE resulting-doc deep-link** (a CREATE DCR's `resulting_version_id` lives on a NEW document whose id `_dcr` does not expose, and there is no top-level `GET /versions/{id}` → the SPA can't resolve it; the read-spine "Resulting version" link shows a bare id and the ui-2b cockpit defers CREATE-implement. - **S-dcr-ui-3** DCR page-image visual diff + redline — **CLOSES the DCR-UI track** (the last named deferral): a reviewer/auditor can now *see* what a REVISE change altered. A dedicated **`/dcrs/:id/diff`** full route shows the worker-async page-image visual diff **and** the text/metadata redline of a DCR's resulting version against the version it supersedes. **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** — no migration, no permission key, no new endpoint, no contract change; **gate = `/check-web` only** (head stays `0051`). Reuses the S-web-4b document-diff machinery **verbatim** (`VisualDiffViewer`/`RedlineViewer`/`useVisualDiff`/`useVersionDiff`). **Owner brainstorm F-decisions** (a 5-reader source-verification fan-out over the render path + the diff backend + the DCR serializer FIRST — it resolved two agent contradictions by direct code reads): **F1 — FRONT-END-ONLY/reuse** (the `VisualDiff` cache is keyed by `(from_version_id, to_version_id)` ONLY [not document-bound — `visual_diff.py:36`]; the three endpoints + the redline endpoint all already exist gated `document.read_draft`; for a REVISE DCR the resulting version AND its predecessor are both versions of `target_document_id`, so the same-document endpoint validation passes untouched — no backend touch). **F2 — already solved, no special handling** (the central finding: `services/diff/visual.py::_ensure_rendition_pdf` renders a not-yet-Effective version **transiently** — `copy_status=version.version_state`, no verify QR — and **deliberately does NOT write the shared `rendition_blob_sha256`** [the mirror's controlled-copy cache, `:112-117`], so previewing an Approved/pre-cutover resulting version is safe). **F3 — a dedicated full-page route** (not a drawer section: the page-image viewer is cramped in a 360–640px portal; full routes drive cleanly in Chrome-MCP whereas the drawer is flaky; a deep-linkable diff URL is auditor-friendly). **F4 — REVISE + Implemented/Closed** (`resulting_version_id` is set only at implement, only for REVISE/CREATE; CREATE has no client `version_id→document_id` resolution, RETIRE has no resulting version). **F5 — both visual + redline** via a `?mode=text|visual` toggle (parity with the doc-detail page). **F6 — impact-annotation kept out of scope** (an unrelated lifecycle phase — annotation at assess-time, the diff at Implemented/Closed). **The slice (`features/dcr/`):** `resolvePredecessor.ts` (a pure helper — succession-link post-cutover [`superseded_by_version_id`], else the governing **Effective** version pre-cutover, else a degenerate seq-fallback); `DcrDiffPage.tsx` (the route — header + back-link to `/dcrs?dcr=:id`, the mode toggle, the pinned-pair viewers, calm states: not-eligible/403-no-access/no-predecessor/load-error); the `DcrDrawer` "View visual diff →" link in the Resulting-version field (REVISE + `resulting_version_id` + `target_document_id`); the `App.tsx` `dcrs/:id/diff` route; `useDocumentVersions` widened with an optional `{retry?:boolean}` (the S-web-8 `useTask` conditional-spread precedent — existing callers byte-untouched — so the diff page skips retries on a deterministic `document.read_draft` 403). ⚠ **Folded-in fix (pre-existing, surfaced by the live smoke; the reused `useVisualDiff` hook — reachable from the doc-detail Compare tab too, NOT introduced by this slice's feature):** the worker-async poll could **stall on first mount** (it seeded the cache from the POST's `onSuccess setQueryData`, then gated the poll's `enabled` on a NON-reactive `qc.getQueryData(key)?.status==="Pending"` — when the POST seeded fresh data at the instant `enabled` flipped true, React Query v5's `shouldFetchOptionally→isStaleByTime` [`staleTime:0`] read it as "fresh" and SKIPPED the initial GET; no `refetchInterval` fallback → it hung on "Rendering…" with zero GET traffic until a manual "Re-request render"). Fix: **the poll owns its own fetch** — drop the seed, enable off the reactive `request.isSuccess` so the first GET runs against an empty cache (`data===undefined` always fetches). Then a **Codex P2** caught that `request.isSuccess` isn't pair-scoped → on a pair change while mounted (navigating between `/dcrs/:id/diff` pages, or the doc-detail picker) the new pair's poll could GET an unrequested row before its own POST → 404; fix: **pair-scope the gate** (`request.isSuccess && request.variables === url`, the POST's url passed as the mutation variable) — proven by a **genuine failing-first test** (confirmed it fails on the pre-fix code; models the backend's 404-until-POST). ⚠ **Traps carried:** the authed page-PNG is `apiGetBlob`→objectURL (the only API-proxied binary in the SPA); every MSW fixture `satisfies <Type>` (incl. the inline no-predecessor `DocumentVersion`, a web-test-trap-reviewer nit); `import {expect,it} from "vitest"`; a per-page jest-axe smoke; the deep-link/navigate `waitFor` discipline; `ApiError.message` = `problem.detail ?? title`. **Codex P2 #2 (resolvePredecessor):** the raw seq-fallback would pick an abandoned higher-seq Draft left by a changes-requested loop instead of the governing Effective version — fixed by preferring `version_state==="Effective"` pre-cutover (INV-1 guarantees one); +1 test. **Reviews:** diff-critic = CLEAN ("safe to PR"; verified the succession direction vs `lifecycle.py:505`, the hook widening's backward-compat, the casts); web-test-trap-reviewer = CLEAN on both the slice and the useVisualDiff fix (the GET overrides are required + faithful — they return the same status, not a silent Ready upgrade); **both Codex P2s fixed + threads resolved**; a final `@codex review` triggered on the merge commit. **Pre-merge live smoke (Chrome MCP):** built a real Implemented REVISE DCR on SOP-PUR-002 (text/plain) via the services (author≠approver≠implementer SoD; approvers picked from each task's `candidate_pool`); verified the drawer link → the diff route → the Text redline (real metadata + text diff against the resolved predecessor→resulting pair) → the Visual page-image diff (authed-PNG `blob:` + layer toggle + the changed-page rail) → the back-link; the useVisualDiff fix verified on a cold pair (POST 202 → GET 202 = the poll now fires; it didn't before) — and the "poll stops after one tick" turned out to be the automated tab being **hidden** (`visibilityState:hidden` + React Query `refetchIntervalInBackground:false`), environmental, not a bug. **Deferred (named, not faked):** **CREATE-implement visual diff** (no client `version_id→document_id` — needs a `resulting_document_id` enrichment or a version-lookup endpoint); ## v1.x CONTINUAL IMPROVEMENT family — clause 10.3 (0052–0053, R46/R2) — opens the last named-but-unbuilt doc-14 §9 entity; a NON-★ own-table mutable-state workflow object (the DCR/R22 doctrine), NOT a shared-PK kind=DOCUMENT subtype; S-improvement-2 wires the OFI-finding + MR-output spawn endpoints (zero-migration); S-improvement-4 (0053) adds the signed, engine-routed Top-Management authorization — **family COMPLETE end-to-end**

- **S-improvement-4** the **engine-routed, signed Top-Management authorization** (clause 10.3, R46/R2) — **CLOSES the Improvement family** (the last, opt-in slice): the initiative's management-authorization now routes through the multi-stage workflow engine to a signed leadership sign-off — the **CAPA action-plan-approval template (`decide_capa_action_plan`) ported to an own-table subject.** **BACKEND (migration 0053) + thin FE.** A Completed initiative's manager opts in via **`POST /improvement-initiatives/{id}/request-authorization`**, opening an engine workflow routed to the seeded **"Top Management"** role; when a member signs (**`meaning=verify`**) via `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` (a new `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE` dispatch leg), the sign-off **closes** the initiative, binding the `signature_event` to the new `Closed` `improvement_initiative_stage_event` via the **pre-generated-UUID seam** (two mutually-referencing INSERTs, never an UPDATE — the table is REVOKE-immutable). **`GET /{id}/authorization`** surfaces the cycle (the `GET /documents/{id}/approval` analogue). **Migration `0053`** = three additive enum `ADD VALUE`s in an `autocommit_block` — `workflow_subject_type.IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE` (the engine subject — ⚠ **the FIRST migration to USE a just-added enum value in its OWN same-migration seed**, so the autocommit-commit-then-seed ordering is load-bearing), `signed_object_type.improvement_initiative_stage_event`, `event_type.INITIATIVE_AUTHORIZED` — + a seeded `improvement_initiative_authorization` workflow_definition (single Top-Management **ANY** stage, `signature={meaning:verify}`; reuses the 0038 "Top Management" role + the 0052 `signed_event_id` hook; NOT-EXISTS-guarded downgrade). **NO new permission key** — the SIGN is candidate-pool (Top-Management) membership (the self-scoped-task doctrine); the request gates the existing `improvement.manage` @ PROCESS, the read gates `improvement.read`. **Contract:** the two endpoints + `WorkflowInstance.subject_type`/`Decision.outcome`/`DecisionResult.outcome` `+= IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE`/`verify` + `DecisionResult.initiative_stage` + `ImprovementInitiativeStageEvent.signed_event_id` + the two new auth-cycle schemas. **Owner decisions (asked in-plan):** `meaning=verify` (leadership verifies the realized benefit; reuses the closed R2 set — **no new meaning**); **additive/opt-in** (the existing unsigned `Completed→Closed` `/transition` close is UNTOUCHED — honors R46's "10.3 mandates no per-initiative sign-off"); a **single Top-Management ANY stage** (proportionate; fails closed to `NEEDS_ATTENTION` when no member is assigned); **backend + thin FE.** **Thin FE:** a `/tasks` `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE` decision arm (`DecisionCard` verify/reject maps + `InitiativeApprovalContext` + the `isDocumentSubject` negation extended `&& !isImprovement`), a cockpit **"Request management authorization"** affordance (suppressed while a cycle is pending, "no Top-Management approver" on `NEEDS_ATTENTION`) + `RequestAuthorizationModal`, and an `InitiativeStageTimeline` "verified by leadership" marker. ⚠ **Codex found 9 real findings across 2 rounds that a CLEAN diff-critic + migration-reviewer + web-test-trap-reviewer ALL missed (the edge-finder lesson repeats HARD on a signed/engine-routed slice):** **round 1 (5×P2 + 1×P3):** (1) the generic engine ANY quorum treats EVERY positive `TaskOutcomeKind` (approve/complete/acknowledge/verify) as completing → a Top-Management caller could POST `{outcome:"approve"}` and mint a **`verify` signature** + close the initiative without a real verify decision → **a `{verify,reject}` allow-list** (the PERIODIC_REVIEW complete-only precedent); (2) the unsigned-close FE race (Close rendered during the auth-cycle load window) → gate close/request on the cycle query having **resolved** (`!isLoading && !isError`); (3) the required request body 422'd a body-less POST → `Model | None = None`; (4) `verify`/`initiative_stage` missing from the Decision contract; (5/P3) the IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE decision branch didn't invalidate `["my-tasks"]`; (6) **a single decline left the cycle pending** (ANY quorum fails only on all-reject) → **a decline is now DECISIVE** — force the instance `REJECTED` + skip sibling PENDING tasks (the **`decide_dcr_approval`** precedent), re-requestable. **round 2 (3×P2):** (7) the **unsigned `/transition` Closed must be 409'd while a non-terminal authorization instance exists** (the FE suppressed it, but a direct call would close unsigned + orphan the pending sign-off) → a backend guard in `transition_initiative`; (8) `WorkflowInstance.subject_type` enum in openapi missing `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE`; (9) the verify/reject allow-list must run **AFTER** `_assert_initiative_authorizer` (else a non-pool caller gets a leaky 422 instead of the 404-collapse). ⚠ **The diff-critic DID catch its own P1 pre-PR:** the original reject test assumed a single-member pool (the shared CI DB always has ≥2 Top-Management members from `test_capa` + this file → one decline = PENDING, not REJECTED, under ANY) — made deterministic by the decisive-decline change (#6). ⚠ **the PostToolUse ruff hook strips a just-added unused import** bit THREE times (re-add AFTER the usage edit — the recurring S-statusbadge-2 trap). **Deferred (named, not faked):** document-backed leadership routing (MR/OBJ/POL sign-off — the named-enhancement deferral persists); a distinct unsigned "Verified" FSM node (folded into the authorized close); `improvement_initiative_action` milestone rows; objective-miss / 9.1.3 auto-seed; an effectiveness re-loop ("CAPA's 10.2 job"); OrgRole-based candidate-pool resolution (stays on the `Role.name` seam, R39); **no cancel/withdraw of a pending authorization** (re-requestable only after it terminalizes — verify→Closed or reject→REJECTED). **Test deltas: +7 api integration** (`test_improvement_authorization.py` — request→sign→close+`verify`-signature, request-requires-Completed, request-twice-409, decline-is-decisive+re-requestable+422-on-bad-outcome, non-member-404-collapse, idempotent-replay, unsigned-close-409-while-pending; **CI-authoritative on this Windows box**) **+ web 1009→1017 (+8:** ReviewApprovePage IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE arm ×4 + a11y smoke; InitiativeAdvancePanel request/suppress/needs-attention ×3). Verified: `/check-api` (ruff+mypy-strict+format) · **`/check-migrations` full round-trip up↔down↔`alembic check` on a throwaway PG16 — CLEAN** (the autocommit-then-seed ordering proven) · `/check-contracts` (redocly) · `/check-web` (eslint+strict-tsc+build+vitest) — all green; CI all 11 checks green on `ef4344b`. **Merge gate:** Codex 2 rounds (9 findings) all fixed + threads replied + resolved + green CI + owner's explicit go; merged `--admin` (behind only the docs-only #187, CI green — the documented fast-lane). - **S-improvement-2** the Improvement Initiative **SPAWN endpoints** (clause 9.2/9.3 → 10.3) — wires the two ways to **raise** an initiative from an origin: **POST `/findings/{finding_id}/raise-initiative`** (OBSERVATION/OFI finding → `source=OFI`, `source_link_id=finding.id`; **422 `finding_not_improvable`** on an NC, **409 `finding_superseded`** on a corrected finding; inherits the audit's auditee process per R28 — `_auto_capa_for_finding`'s `plan.auditee_process_id`, not the soft `process_ref`) + **POST `/management-reviews/{review_id}/outputs/{output_id}/raise-initiative`** (ACTION/IMPROVEMENT output → `source=review`, `source_link_id=output.id`; **422 `output_not_improvable`** on a DECISION, **409 `review_not_tracking`** unless `close_state==ActionsTracked`; emits `MGMT_REVIEW_INITIATIVE_SPAWNED` on the MR doc). **ZERO-migration** — every seam shipped in `0052`: the `source_link_id`/`spawn_idempotency_key` columns + the `uq_improvement_initiative_spawn` partial-UNIQUE, the `MGMT_REVIEW_INITIATIVE_SPAWNED` event type + `improvement_initiative` audit object type, the `create_initiative(_commit=False)` compose seam, the `improvement.read`/`improvement.manage` keys (head stays `0052`, next `0053`). Both are **1:N + optional `Idempotency-Key`** (201 new / 200 replay via the `(org, source_link_id, key)` partial-UNIQUE), compose `create_initiative(_commit=False)` in ONE txn, and mint **no signature** (R43); the idempotent replay runs **before** the mutable close-state gate so a retry after the review closes still replays (the `spawn_dcr_for_output` precedent), with the `IntegrityError` rollback+re-query backstop (the `allocate_seq` IMP-seq increment rolls back with the txn → no counter leak). **Owner decisions (asked in-plan):** MR-output eligibility = **{ACTION, IMPROVEMENT}** (the reserved `IMPROVEMENT` output type is exactly this — broader than the CAPA/DCR siblings' ACTION-only); the MR back-link **`review_output.spawned_initiative_id` stays reserved-null** (1:N one-way via `initiative.source_link_id`; un-reserving the reciprocal latch is a future owner-flipped `0053` per the 0051 `spawned_capa_id` recipe — so the S-improvement-3 MR drawer finds initiatives by `source='review' AND source_link_id=output.id`, like DCRs). **Placement (parent-domain modules):** `services/mgmt_review/actions.py::spawn_initiative_for_output` (beside `spawn_capa`/`spawn_dcr`) + `services/audits/service.py::raise_initiative_from_finding` (beside `_auto_capa_for_finding`); both routes reuse `_initiative`/`_scope_for` imported from `api/improvement` (the `api/mgmt_review`→`api/dcr` cross-router precedent; `api/improvement` imports only services → no cycle). ⚠ **diff-critic CLEAN but Codex found 3 real P2s (all valid; the lesson repeats HARD — Codex, not the diff-critic, is the edge-finder):** (1) **replay scope authz** — the idempotent replay returned an initiative by `(org, source_link, key)` without re-authorizing its STORED scope → a process-B caller could read a process-A initiative via a known key; **fix:** both endpoints re-enforce `improvement.manage` against the returned `initiative.process_id` on a replay (gate-2; the finding endpoint keeps its `require()` gate-1 + adds an imperative gate-2). (2) **superseded findings** — a corrected finding (the audit close gate already excludes it) could still seed an initiative (an OBS later corrected to NC); **fix:** load the `Record` and reject `superseded_by_correction` → **409 `finding_superseded`**, checked AFTER the replay lookup so a prior valid raise still replays. (3) **tracking-window race** — the unlocked `close_state` read; **documented benign**, matching the `spawn_capa`/`spawn_dcr` siblings (the close gate reads only the spawned MR_ACTION task state, never spawned objects, so a just-after-close spawn is coherent) — a uniform lock across all three is a separate cross-cutting call (deferred). **Contract:** +2 paths in `openapi.yaml` (inline `additionalProperties:false` bodies, `Idempotency-Key` header, 201/200; the finding 409 added in the fix round) + a new **`docs/15 §8.12b` Improvement Initiatives** section (the family had no docs/15 entry). **Deferred (named, not faked):** **S-improvement-3** (the SPA register/InitiativeDrawer/`improvement_stage` StatusBadge/raise affordances/PDCA-ACT tile); **S-improvement-4** (opt-in Verified benefit stage / mgmt-authorization routing); the reciprocal `spawned_initiative_id` latch (a `0053` owner call); a uniform spawn-lock across capa/dcr/initiative. **Test delta: +15 integration (`test_improvement_spawn.py` — both origins × {happy, 422 ineligible, 404 unknown, idempotent replay incl. replay-after-close, authz deny}, the superseded→409, the cross-process-replay→403, `source`/`source_link_id`/process-inheritance, the MR-side audit event, no-signature, `spawned_initiative_id`-stays-null); api unit + web unchanged (backend-only).** Verified locally (Windows): ruff + ruff format --check + mypy `src` clean; redocly lint valid; import smoke + unit collection clean — integration is CI-authoritative (ProactorEventLoop/psycopg), all 4 shards green across both commits. - **S-improvement-1** the Improvement Initiatives **BACKEND CORE** (clause 10.3 continual improvement) — **OPENS the Improvement Initiatives family** (mig `0052`, **R46**), the last named-but-unbuilt entity in doc 14 §9. **The doctrine:** per R46 an initiative is an **own-table mutable-state workflow object** (the DCR/R22 posture), NOT a kind=RECORD artifact and NOT a `documented_information` subtype — because clause 10.3 is **NON-★** (`is_mandatory_star=False`, no checklist node to flip), so the R44/R45 shared-PK kind=DOCUMENT rationale that OBJ/MR ride is *absent* and copying it here would be a category error. Mutable `stage` is the headline; the append-only `improvement_initiative_stage_event` (REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE; no `updated_at`) is the immutable history; events key on a fresh `audit_object_type='improvement_initiative'` (the ncr/dcr own-table precedent), `scope_ref=<identifier>`. **FSM** (`domain/improvement/fsm.py`, the dcr/capa pure-FSM precedent): unsigned `Open→InProgress→Completed→Closed` (+`Cancelled` reachable ONLY from `{Open,InProgress}`); `Closed`/`Cancelled` terminal + set `closed_at`; the `Closed` transition folds a free-text `outcome` into the sealed `stage_event.payload` (the lightweight 10.3 evidence — NOT a signed gate, NOT recomputed; no new `SignatureMeaning`, R2 closed). `transition_initiative` loads FOR UPDATE with `.execution_options(populate_existing=True)` (the S-drift-1 stale-identity-map trap) + a 409 `improvement_transition_invalid`, writing stage-event + stage flip + `INITIATIVE_TRANSITIONED` in ONE txn. get + stage-events gate `improvement.read`; create enforces `improvement.manage` on the body's optional `process_id`; PATCH enforces manage on BOTH the current AND (on reassignment) the target process; + the unknown-UUID 500 above. **Migration `0052`:** two fresh native-PG enums from the ORM `*_VALUES` tuples (the 0010/0040 no-drift rule) — `improvement_stage` (Open/InProgress/Completed/Closed/Cancelled, title-case like `dcr_state`) + `improvement_source` (`OFI` uppercase to match `FindingType.OFI`; the append-only `improvement_initiative_stage_event` (REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE from `easysynq_app`; `signed_event_id` is the **D3 Part-11 hook — a real FK present but NULL/unsigned in v1.x**, the `dcr_stage_event` precedent); `audit_object_type` += `improvement_initiative` + 4 event-type ADD VALUEs (`INITIATIVE_RAISED`/`_UPDATED`/`_TRANSITIONED` emitted now + `MGMT_REVIEW_INITIATIVE_SPAWNED` pre-provisioned for slice 2) in an autocommit_block; the two additive (R38) CONTENT-domain keys `improvement.read` + `improvement.manage` (**catalog 100→102**, `sig_hook=False`) + role grants. `openapi.yaml` +6 endpoints in-PR; the `create_initiative(_commit=False)` seam lets slice-2 spawn endpoints compose creation inside their own txn (the dcr/capa precedent). **Deferred (named, not faked):** **S-improvement-2** spawn wiring (POST `/findings/{id}/raise-initiative` — 422 `finding_not_improvable` unless `finding_type∈{OBSERVATION,OFI}`, Idempotency-Key — + POST `/management-reviews/{id}/outputs/{oid}/raise-initiative`; no `signature_event` per R43; leaves `review_output.spawned_initiative_id` reserved-null unless the owner flips the latch, a 0053 call per the 0051 `spawned_capa_id` recipe); **S-improvement-3** web (the Improvement › Continual Improvement register + InitiativeDrawer/stage-timeline + an `improvement_stage` StatusBadge + raise affordances on OFI/Observation findings & MR IMPROVEMENT/ACTION outputs + the PDCA-ACT quadrant tile); **S-improvement-4** (opt-in only) the optional unsigned **Verified benefit-review** stage (reuse `meaning='verify'` + the pre-generated-UUID seam if ever signed — never an UPDATE, the table is REVOKE-immutable) and/or an engine-routed management-authorization approval (a new `WorkflowSubjectType`); and the not-yet-slotted `improvement_initiative_action` **milestone rows** + the **objective-miss / 9.1.3 auto-seed**. **Test delta: +9 api unit (`test_improvement_fsm.py`) + 8 integration (`test_improvement.py` — lifecycle, FSM 409s, the cancel-window, the PROCESS-scoped row-filter authz regression, the REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE append-only proof [SQLSTATE 42501], R43 no-`signature_event`); `test_authz.py` + `test_quality_objectives.py` catalog-count assertions bumped 100→102; web unchanged (backend-only).** Verified locally (Windows): ruff + ruff format --check + mypy-strict clean; `test_improvement_fsm.py` 9/9; redocly lint valid; throwaway-PG16 alembic up↔down↔check clean — integration + full-unit are CI-only on this box. Register **R46**. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-15-s-improvement-1-continual-improvement*`. PR [#150](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/150), squash `fe2f1d3`. **Retroactively finish-sliced 2026-06-15 (D-1 docs cleanup) — PR #150 shipped the code but not this changelog entry.**

## v1.x MANAGEMENT REVIEW family — clause 9.3 (0050–0051) — flips the 9.3 ★ COVERED → the ISO 9001:2015 ★ spine is feature-complete; S-mr-2 makes it usable in the SPA; S-mr-3 wires its ACTION outputs to the CAPA/DCR action systems; S-mr-pack adds the filed-minutes PDF export

- **S-mr-pack** the Management Review minutes pack (PDF) (clause 9.3 → doc 13 §7.3) — **closes the named S-mr-1 deferral "the rendered Management-Review-Pack PDF (v1.1)" (R45).** A *released* MR now exposes a downloadable, table-styled PDF of its **filed minutes** at **`GET /management-reviews/{review_id}/pack`** (gate `mgmtReview.read`, **released-only** → 409 `pack_unavailable`; 404 cross-org) + a "Download minutes pack (PDF)" button on the MR detail page (Effective-only). **ONE new endpoint + the OpenAPI entry + FE; NO migration, NO permission key, NO enum** (head stays `0051`, catalog 100); gates `/check-api` + `/check-contracts` + `/check-web`. **Owner-approved shape (the central fork — 3 coherent end-to-end options surfaced):** the **lightweight "printable view"** — a *synchronous, in-request* **reportlab Platypus** render streamed straight back as `application/pdf` (NOT the heavyweight evidence-pack: no Celery, no status row, no reaper, no cache, no blob, no new EVIDENCE record, no WORM re-seal — the released MR version is *already* the canonical WORM record; the pack is a derived rendering of it, like a controlled-copy). ⚠ **Why sync is legal** (the "API can't render" rule is about `GotenbergRenderSink` HTML→PDF via the external service): a reportlab table-PDF over a few-KB JSON dict is pure-Python — and the MR's minutes blob is `application/json` (`no_controlled_rendition`, R26) so Gotenberg *can't* render it, which is exactly *why* a self-render is needed. **Sub-decisions (all owner-confirmed):** source = the **released version's FROZEN snapshot** (`metadata_snapshot["mgmt_review_minutes"]`), not the live `review_input`/`review_output` rows; delivery = a direct `Response(application/pdf)` stream (no blob/cache); include an **e-signature sign-off block**; **plain footer** (canonical version id + the JCS minutes source digest, no verify QR); **table-styled** (Platypus `Table`/`TableStyle` + `Paragraph` cells, not line-rendered). **Architecture (3 focused units):** the PURE render leaf `domain/mgmt_review/pack_render.py` (`render_minutes_pdf(...) -> bytes` — no DB/IO/`ProblemException`; deterministic via an **invariant canvasmaker** [`Canvas(invariant=1)` fixes the PDF `/ID`+metadata, no `Date.now()`] so a given released MR renders byte-identical) → the gather service `services/mgmt_review/pack.py` (`minutes_from_snapshot` [409 on a missing key], `_resolve_names` [org-scoped], `_signer_label`, `build_minutes_pdf`) → `repository.list_signoffs_for_version` (the version's `approval`+`release` signatures, OUTER JOIN to `app_user`, **`voided_by IS NULL`** so a rescinded sig never appears in a compliance PDF) → the thin endpoint. **FE:** the authed-binary `getBlob`→objectURL→`<a download>` pattern (the visual-diff PNG precedent — the only API-proxied binary in the SPA); the button gates on `current_state==="Effective"`. ⚠ **Load-bearing traps — the pack must render ONLY frozen/immutable facts (else byte-instability / a 500 / PII):** (1) **render the FROZEN snapshot title, NOT live `doc.title`** — `PATCH /documents/{id}` can rename a released MR, changing the "filed" pack's bytes; (2) **DON'T render `close_state`** — it mutates ActionsTracked→Closed *after* filing, so before/after-close would differ; (3) **NO email PII** — `_resolve_names`/`_signer_label` fall back display_name → **id** (NEVER email) because the pack is only `mgmtReview.read`-gated and the directory exposes only `{id, display_name}` to ordinary members; (4) **signer identity** — a human with a null `display_name` falls back to the id, NOT "system"; only a true null `signer_user_id` (a Beat system release) is "system" (select `signer_user_id` to distinguish); (5) **`Table(splitInRow=1, repeatRows=1)`** — a max-length (4000-char) decision in one cell would otherwise exceed the page frame → `LayoutError` → a 500; (6) ⚠ **the CI web Blob.stream() trap (a genuine CI-vs-local divergence):** the FE download test's MSW handler returning a `Blob` body throws `object.stream is not a function` during MSW's interceptor lookup on CI's node (which lacks `Blob.stream`) → the download path never runs → the click-spy fails; **return a `Uint8Array` body** (streamable; the consumer's `resp.blob()` still works). ⚠ **THE review lesson repeats HARD — diff-critic was CLEAN but Codex found 7 real P2s across 2 rounds, all valid, all fixed:** R1 [signer-as-system, the 4000-char LayoutError, mutable close_state, org-scoped names] + R2 [frozen title, email PII, the frozen `compiled_at` row]; the merge was held an extra round because R2 included a real PII leak. **Live smoke (Chrome MCP, full route — no `/dcrs` drawer wall):** the button shows on the released MR-GEN-003 + is hidden on an InReview MR; click → `GET …/pack` → 200, no console errors; the rendered PDF **eyeballed** (metadata table incl. the frozen `Inputs compiled` row, attendees, 9.3.2 RAG-summary inputs, 9.3.3 outputs with resolved owner names, the sign-off block [approval + release; null signer → "system"], the verifiable footer). ⚠ Native-Windows: integration + the full unit suite are CI-only (ProactorEventLoop / native crash) — verified locally via ruff + mypy + targeted unit tests, integration by reasoning + CI. **Deferred (named, not faked):** external share-links for the pack (the S-pack-2 token machinery); the heavyweight **embedded-source-artifacts** bundle (the maximal evidence-pack shape — the owner chose printable-minutes); + the standing MR deferrals (MR-minutes revision, `improvement_initiative` **(model now built — S-improvement-1 / R46; the MR-output spawn seam is slice 2)**, Top-Management approval routing, broader-than-ACTION output spawning). **+13 api unit (6 render + 7 service — incl. `_signer_label` + a 4000-char-row split test) + 5 integration (CI-only: 200/409/404/403 + a frozen-snapshot-AND-close_state-invariance proof) / +5 web (861→866, incl. an Effective-state jest-axe smoke).** diff-critic CLEAN; CI 9/9 (one web flake from the Blob.stream trap, fixed); Codex 2 rounds, all 7 P2s fixed + threads resolved; subagent-driven TDD (6 tasks, per-task spec+quality review; the Task-5 integration test on opus for CI-fidelity). PR [#136](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/136), squash `1d8eb05`. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-14-s-mr-pack-minutes-pdf*`.

- **S-mr-3** MR outputs → action systems (clause 9.3 → §10/§7.5) — **un-reserves the two deferred S-mr-1 seams + lands the S-mr-2 Codex-#1 chip**: a *released* Management Review's **ACTION output** now drives the action systems — spawn a **CAPA** (full backend + FE) or a **DCR** (backend-only). ⚠ **Two ground-truth corrections to the brief's framing (the "verify everything against code" instruction earned its keep):** (1) `review_output.spawned_initiative_id` and the DCR link are **DIFFERENT seams** — `spawned_initiative_id` points at an `improvement_initiative` table that **does not exist anywhere in the codebase** (docs/14 §9 "deferred/unbuilt in v1"), so it **stays reserved-null** this slice; the DCR link is the `DcrSourceLinkType.mgmt_review` enum member (one-way, on the DCR's `source_link`, no reciprocal column). (2) **The DCR domain has ZERO SPA surface** (no `features/dcr/`; grep `/dcrs`/`change_type`/`source_link` across `apps/web/src` is empty — even the existing CAPA→DCR loop is backend/CLI/test-only), so a Raise-DCR *button* would spawn a DCR into a black hole → DCR is scoped **backend-only** (a tested endpoint + the contract; the FE waits for a future DCR-UI track). **Migration `0051` (breaks the migration-free streak, head 0050→0051):** the FK on the EXISTING `review_output.spawned_capa_id` column → `capa.id` (`ondelete=RESTRICT` — the `spawned_task_id` precedent on the same table; acyclic so no `use_alter`; **name-mirrored in the ORM `review_output.py` or `alembic check` phantom-DROPs it**) + additive `ALTER TYPE dcr_reason_class ADD VALUE 'mgmt_review'` + the `MGMT_REVIEW_CAPA_SPAWNED`/`MGMT_REVIEW_DCR_SPAWNED` event types (`IF NOT EXISTS` in an `autocommit_block` — the 0048 pattern; a from-scratch `upgrade head` already has them via the `*_VALUES` tuples → they no-op there). Round-trip up↔down↔`alembic check` verified clean on a throwaway PG16. **The CAPA spawn (`services/mgmt_review/actions.py::spawn_capa_for_output`):** ⚠ **uses `build_capa(source=CapaSource.review_output, _commit=False)` NOT `raise_capa`** — `raise_capa` still 422s `review_output` (the generic `POST /capas` stays closed to it); `build_capa` accepts it, mirroring `_auto_capa_for_finding`'s atomic flow (build uncommitted → set `output.spawned_capa_id` → `MGMT_REVIEW_CAPA_SPAWNED` audit → ONE commit; **no signature**, R43). It is **forced on-demand** (a CAPA REQUIRES a severity the ACTION output doesn't carry → an auto-at-release spawn would have to invent one), exposed as `POST /management-reviews/{id}/outputs/{oid}/raise-capa` (gate `capa.create` at SYSTEM — the MR has no process), and a **one-shot latch**: the output row is locked `with_for_update().execution_options(populate_existing=True)` BEFORE the `spawned_capa_id is None` check and held across `build_capa`+commit, so two racers serialize → the loser 409s `capa_already_spawned`. **The DCR spawn (`spawn_dcr_for_output`):** **1:N + idempotent**, mirroring `raise_dcr_from_capa` — `raise_dcr(source_link_type=mgmt_review, source_link_id=output.id, reason_class=mgmt_review, spawn_idempotency_key=<Idempotency-Key>, _commit=False)`; idempotency pre-check → try raise+`MGMT_REVIEW_DCR_SPAWNED` audit+commit → except `IntegrityError` rollback+re-query (the audit lives inside the try so a rollback discards it; an early replay returns before the audit → no dup; `refresh` only on success); `POST .../raise-dcr` gates `changeRequest.create` at the target-doc scope (`_dcr_doc_scope`; CREATE→SYSTEM), returns 201 new / 200 replay. **F3 — the close-gate DECOUPLE is the ABSENCE of a change:** a spawned CAPA must NEVER block MR close, so `close_review`/`output_blocks_close` are byte-untouched (they key solely off the spawned MR_ACTION task state via the fail-closed OUTERJOIN), pinned by `test_spawned_capa_does_not_block_close` (CAPA left open + task DONE → close 200). **diff-critic confirmed the RESTRICT FK can't block a legal erasure** — disposal/WORM-destroy keeps the `capa`/`record` row as a tombstone (no `session.delete(Capa)` anywhere) and `delete_output` is `_require_draft`-gated, so it can never row-delete an output carrying a `spawned_capa_id` (spawning requires the post-release `ActionsTracked` state). **Codex #1 (the S-mr-2 chip `task_ae567104`):** `_mr_capabilities` computes `{release}` at detail-read time via the SoD-2 overlay — reuse the existing `_release_scope` (already `enrich_release_sod_scope`-enriched) + `gather_grants`+`authorize(sig_hook=True, sod=sod)`, mirroring `_objective_capabilities`'s release branch — and `_mgmt_review` gains an optional `capabilities` kwarg included **detail-only** (only `get_review_endpoint` passes it; list/create/etc. don't); the FE Release button flips from `can("document.release")` to `mr.capabilities?.release === true && state==="Approved"` → no show-then-403, and the FE Raise-CAPA gate `can("capa.create")` matches the backend SYSTEM `capa.create` (no FE/BE gate desync). **FE:** `RaiseMrCapaModal` (severity-only — the backend derives the title + sets `source=review_output`), the `ReviewOutputsSection` Raise/View-CAPA affordances on ACTION rows (Raise when `tracking && capa.create`; a `/capa?capa=<id>` View deep-link — the audit→CAPA precedent — when `spawned_capa_id` is set; the modal conditionally-mounted so close resets it), and `ManagementReviewDetailPage` passing `tracking={close_state==="ActionsTracked"}`. ⚠ Adding the non-optional `spawned_capa_id` to the `ReviewOutput` TS type breaks every fixture lacking it → patched in the same task to keep `tsc` green (`capabilities?` is optional → `MgmtReviewDetail` fixtures are safe). **diff-critic = CLEAN** (1 MINOR: the two new OpenAPI summaries said "Gated mgmtReview.record_outputs" but the handlers gate `capa.create`/`changeRequest.create` — doc-only drift, fixed). **CI green (all 9 checks); Codex post-PR raised 3×P2 the diff-critic missed — all valid, all fixed:** (1) the FE View-CAPA deep-link was gated on `tracking` so a Closed review lost it (gate only Raise on tracking; show View whenever `spawned_capa_id` is set); (2) `spawn_dcr_for_output` ran the close-state gate BEFORE the idempotency replay → a same-key retry after close 409'd instead of replaying (moved `_find_spawned_dcr_for_output` ahead of the tracking gate — the `raise_dcr_from_capa` precedent); (3) the contract `DcrReasonClass` enum omitted `mgmt_review` though raise-dcr returns it. +2 tests (FE closed-review-View + the after-close idempotency-replay integration test). PR [#122](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/122), squash `1a2a7ba`. **Gates:** `/check-web` green (lint+tsc+build + the full **761-test** vitest suite), `/check-migrations` + `/check-contracts` green; backend ruff+mypy clean + targeted unit tests pass — ⚠ the FULL unit suite + `-m integration` are CI-only on this native-Windows box (ProactorEventLoop / native crash), so the 6 new integration tests run in CI. Deferred (named, not faked): **MR-minutes revision** (the S-obj-4 analog — DEFERRED: a 9.3.3 record is point-in-time, you convene a NEW review rather than revise a filed one), `improvement_initiative` + `spawned_initiative_id` (no target table **at S-mr-3 time — the model now exists per S-improvement-1 / R46; the MR-output→initiative spawn seam is slice 2**), the **MR→DCR front-end** (awaits a dedicated DCR-UI track), broader-than-ACTION output spawning, the MR-Pack PDF (v1.1), Top-Management approval routing. +~13 api tests (7 unit + 6 integration) / +7 web (754→761); subagent-driven TDD (11 implementer tasks, per-task spec+quality review, opus on the service core, diff-critic pre-PR). Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-13-s-mr-3-mr-outputs-to-action-systems*`.

- **S-mr-2** the Management Review UI (clause 9.3) — **CLOSES the Management Review family** (the ISO 9001:2015 ★ spine is now usable end-to-end in the SPA). The owner chose the maximal path on every brainstorm fork, so this is the FE module + **three migration-free backend touches** (head stays `0050`, **catalog stays 100, no new permission key, no new enum**; gate = `/check-web` + `/check-api` + `/check-contracts`). **Backend touch 1 — `GET /management-reviews/next-due`** (the only way to surface the cadence: VERIFIED that no GET exposes `system_config.mgmt_review_cadence_months` — not even `/admin/config`, which is `config.update`-gated AND omits the field — so the Home widget is NOT pure-front-end-possible): a shared `read_cadence(session, org_id) -> CadenceStatus|None` + `mr_review_state` + an MR-specific `MR_REVIEW_LEAD_DAYS=30` in `cadence.py`, with `sweep_mgmt_reviews` **refactored to call `read_cadence`** so the widget + the daily sweep can't desync; the endpoint is gated `mgmtReview.read`, **declared BEFORE `/{review_id}`** (the S-pack-2 str-convertor shadow — pinned by a `route.matches` unit test), uses `today_org()` not UTC, and **never 500s** (a `cad is None` neutral fallback). **Backend touch 2 — MR_INPUT auto-resolve at submit** (the cadence-minted `MR_INPUT` "prepare" task is non-decidable — `decide_mr_task` has no leg for it — so it would linger PENDING forever): `_resolve_prepare_tasks` in `submit_review_for_review`, on the seam **between `audit_transition` and the single `session.commit`** (rides the same atomic txn), finds the **`MGMT_REVIEW` container** instance via `find_nonterminal_instance(..., terminal_states=())` (NOT the DOCUMENT approval instance) and flips its PENDING `MR_INPUT` tasks to DONE — a plain mutation, **no `TaskOutcome`/no signature (R43)**; a manually-`POST`ed review has no container → graceful no-op (the existing submit tests are the backstop). **Backend touch 3 — a shared `compute_scorecard`** (`services/objectives/queries.py`) de-duplicates the RAG tally that `api/objectives.py::scorecard_endpoint` and the MR compiler reproduced; ⚠ **the fn is authz-AGNOSTIC — the #1 risk held explicitly**: the gates STAY at the call sites (the endpoint's `require('objective.read')` PEP; the MR compiler's owner-DIRECT-PDP `_owner_holds`, which fail-closes to a gap row, never a 403) — pulling authz into the shared fn would emit a spurious audit row, gate the wrong principal, and turn the F3 gap row into a 403; both response shapes byte-preserved (the endpoint serializes from the returned `rows`, the two preservation tests stay green). **FE — a new `features/management-review/` module** (greenfield; mirrors `features/objectives/`): the `/management-reviews` register (gated nav entry in the CHECK cluster + flat routes), the detail/lifecycle cockpit (header → the **9.3.2 inputs as calm RAG tables** — a generic `source_ref` renderer + the OBJECTIVES_STATUS RAG band, **N6 no-charts / N9 server-RAG-verbatim**, doc-13 §5.2's gauge/donut vocabulary restated → the 9.3.3 outputs grouped DECISION/ACTION/IMPROVEMENT, an ACTION showing its owner/due + a best-effort spawned-task state → a Lifecycle `Card` reusing the shared `ApprovalStepper` with Compile-inputs/Submit/Release/Close gated on `current_state` + `usePermissions().can(...)` since the MR serializer carries **no `capabilities` block**, + the as-built close-gate codes `review_close_blocked`/`review_not_open_to_close` mapped to calm copy), the Draft-only outputs editor (`AddOutputModal` — an ACTION requires an owner, client-enforced), and the create modal. **FE — the `/tasks` MGMT_REVIEW arm** in the shared `ReviewApprovePage`: `MR_INPUT` → **nav-only** (no decide affordance — non-decidability is a FE contract since `decide_mr_task` doesn't gate on `task.type`), `MR_ACTION` → a complete-only **`MrActionCard`** (one-click `outcome:complete`, per-mount Idempotency-Key, **no signature/no DecisionCard** — mirrors `AttestationCard`); the document-branch disablers gained `!isMgmtReview` (extracted as a single named `isDocumentSubject` so a future arm can't forget a negation); `useDecideMrTask` invalidates the review **detail** + list + `my-tasks`. **FE — the Home CHECK next-review widget** (`NextReviewLine` off `useMgmtReviewNextDue`): `owner_configured:false` → "cadence not configured", else due/overdue with RAG; **a forbidden/errored/unarmed read contributes NO RAG** (the S-home-1 worst-of invariant — it can never drag the tile red), and the hook is read twice (CheckCard + NextReviewLine) but react-query dedups the single `["management-review-next-due"]` key (no double fetch). ⚠ **Review catches worth carrying** (per-task spec+quality review + the jest-axe gate): (1) a **jest-axe smoke check on the detail page caught a real heading-order a11y bug** (h2 page-title → h4 sections; fixed the input/output section headings to h3); (2) the best-effort `useTask` reading a spawned action task the caller may not own needs **`retry:false`** (a 404 is the EXPECTED non-owner outcome, not a transient to re-hammer 3× — the documented trap; `useTask` was widened with a conditional-spread `retry` per S-web-8, existing callers unaffected); (3) `useDecideMrTask` must invalidate the review **detail** key (close-readiness is read there), not just the list; (4) the plan's `TaskStateBadge`/`ApprovalStepper` import paths were `../document/` not `../review/` — caught by the implementers against source. **Reconciliation (verified at wrap, no register change):** R45 (decisions-register) + `docs/15-api-design.md` already use the as-built `/management-reviews` + `review_close_blocked` names — only the **archived S-mr-1 design spec** drafted `/mgmt-reviews` + `mgmt_review_close_blocked`, so the fix is a one-line as-built banner on that spec. Deferrals carried (named-not-faked): MR commitment **revision** (first-release-only, the S-obj-3 posture → a possible S-mr-3 with the CAPA `review_output` un-reserve + the DCR `mgmt_review` link); the four sourceless 9.3.2 inputs + risk + improvement (gap rows); the rendered MR-Pack PDF (v1.1); a dedicated Top-Management approval routing; org-tunable cadence + `MR_REVIEW_LEAD_DAYS`; a backend `decide_mr_task` type-gate (defense-in-depth; the FE contract suffices for v1); minor DRY nits accepted (the four near-identical lifecycle-action blocks, a duplicated `nameOf`, `mr_review_state` mirroring `review_state`'s 3-line body — the latter not deduped because `review_state` is a shared documents-module fn whose tests are integration-only/CI-gated on this Windows box). **+~4 api tests** (the `route.matches` ordering unit + the `mr_review_state` bucket-math unit + the `next-due` shape + the MR_INPUT auto-resolve integration tests; integration is CI-gated — native pytest hits the Windows ProactorEventLoop wall) / **+51 web (703→754)**; subagent-driven TDD (13 implementer + 2-stage spec/quality review per task; the two load-bearing catches above came from the per-task quality reviews + the jest-axe gate). Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-12-s-mr-2-management-review-ui*`.

- **S-mr-1** the Management Review backend (clause 9.3) — **OPENS the Management Review family** (mig `0050`, **R45**) and is the last ★-node slice: **one released Management Review flips the 9.3 ★ checklist node COVERED, so the ISO 9001:2015 ★ spine is now feature-complete** (proven in integration). **The DOCUMENT-head thesis:** a Management Review is a **kind=DOCUMENT shared-PK subtype** of `documented_information` (document_type `MR`, the S-obj-1/R44 precedent), auto-mapped to clause 9.3 at create — a **deliberate, register-sanctioned deviation from doc-14 §9's RECORD prescription** (only a released *document* earns the `current_effective_version_id` the compliance checklist reads at `services/reports/checklist.py`, so DOCUMENT is the only shape that flips the ★). **The freeze** (the S-obj-3/S-rec-3 recipe verbatim): at submit, the convened review's minutes — the auto-compiled 9.3.2 inputs *as-of* + the 9.3.3 decisions/outputs — `rfc8785`-canonicalize the JSON-safe dict (hashed **bare, no preamble**) → `finalize_worm` an `application/json` source blob (lands `no_controlled_rendition`, R26) → the SAME dict into `metadata_snapshot.mgmt_review_minutes` via a one-kwarg `_snapshot` fold; the document then rides the **unchanged** submit→approve→release machinery, and **release** files the minutes as the 9.3.3 retained record. The operational lifecycle (doc-10 §7 Scheduled→…→Closed) maps onto the **authoring FSM + a mutable `close_state` tail** (`ActionsTracked → Closed`) on the satellite, outside the version. **Sign-off** rides the standard signed `document.approve`/`document.release` (**no new `SignatureMeaning`**, R2; SoD-2 submitter≠approver≠releaser binds because the submitter authored the frozen version); `attendees` jsonb is the informational roster (a dedicated Top-Management approval routing is deferred). **Outputs** are append-only `review_output` rows; an `ACTION` output (owner + due) spawns one `MR_ACTION` task at release on a `MGMT_REVIEW` workflow_instance — ⚠ **diff-critic MAJOR (fixed): a per-action `stage_key` `"action:<output_id>"`** so the engine's distinct-approver guard never spans two actions of one owner. The new `MGMT_REVIEW` `/tasks/{id}/decision` dispatch leg (`decide_mr_task`, the `decide_periodic_review` mirror; 404-collapse non-membership) flips the task DONE; the **review-close gate mirrors `_audit_close_gate`** (pure `output_blocks_close`, fail-closed: an ACTION whose task is None/not-DONE blocks; a DECISION never blocks; the loader OUTERJOINs the spawned task) → 409 `review_close_blocked` until every action is DONE. **Input compilation** (`compile-inputs`, Draft-only) runs the **six live org-wide reads** (objectives scorecard, audits, CAPAs/NCRs/complaints, KPI readings, compliance-checklist+overdue, drift) gated on the review **owner's** grants (the deterministic-pack `gather_grants`+`authorize` direct PDP path), **fail-closed per source → an `available=false` gap row, never a 403**; the four sourceless 9.3.2 inputs + risk/opportunity (e) + improvement (f) are honest gap rows. **Cadence** is a coded default (`system_config.mgmt_review_cadence_months`=12) driving a daily Beat sweep (`sweep_mgmt_reviews`, mirroring `sweep_reviews` — advisory-lock single-flight, org-scoped `open_review_exists` idempotency, NULL-owner + mis-seed honest degrades) that mints the next Scheduled Draft MR + an `MR_INPUT` task. The family **rides the already-seeded `mgmtReview.read`/`create`/`record_outputs` keys** (seeded + granted to QMS Owner in `0004_seed_authz.py`) — **no new permission key, catalog stays 100, no R38 change**; `record_outputs` is `sig_hook=False` (R43 — recording outputs mints no signature). **Migration `0050`:** the `management_review` subtype + append-only-by-posture `review_input`/`review_output` child tables (the `spawned_capa_id`/`spawned_initiative_id` columns ship **reserved-null** — the CAPA un-reserve + the DCR `mgmt_review` link are slice-2) + the `review_input_type` (12) / `review_output_type` / `management_review_close_state` enums + the four additive `MGMT_REVIEW_INPUTS_COMPILED`/`_OUTPUT_RECORDED`/`_ACTION_SPAWNED`/`_CLOSED` event types (`object_type='document'` + `scope_ref=<identifier>`, R39 reuse — no new `audit_object_type`) + the `MR` document_type seed + the `management_review` workflow_definition seed + the `system_config` cadence/owner columns. The `/management-reviews` router (create/list/detail/compile-inputs/outputs-CRUD/submit-review/approval/release/close/meta-PATCH) is contracted in `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml`. Imported legacy minutes remain kind=RECORD type `MGMT_REVIEW` (evidence; do not flip the ★) and coexist. Deferrals (named, not faked): the four sourceless 9.3.2 inputs + risk (e) + `improvement_initiative` (f) as gap rows; the CAPA `review_output` un-reserve + the DCR `mgmt_review` link → slice-2; the rendered Management-Review-Pack PDF → v1.1; a dedicated Top-Management approval routing; MR commitment **revision** (first-release-only in v1, the S-obj-3 posture); the trailing **S-mr-2** UI + the Home "next review in N days" widget. +41 api tests. Register **R45**. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-12-s-mr-1-management-review*`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVE REVISION — revise an Effective commitment through the full cycle — closes the S-obj-3 residuals

- **S-obj-4** Objective commitment revision (clause 6.2) — **MIGRATION-FREE** (head stays `0049` — `alembic check` round-trip pinned as a no-op; catalog stays 100, no new audit type [V-5: working-copy edits are unaudited by system-wide precedent — the documents metadata-PATCH emits nothing; the version chain is the audit trail], no new signature meaning) — **closes every S-obj-3 deferral**: commitment-revision-edit, **F-2's read-back switch**, the FE submit-gate widening, AND the generic byte-path guard. An Effective objective now revises end-to-end: `POST /objectives/{id}/start-revision` (**`objective.manage`**, a thin wrapper over the SAME vault `start_revision` — T7 FSM + Redis edit lock + WorkingDraft + REVISION_STARTED; namespaced because the QMS Owner holds no `document.edit` — the F-1 asymmetry repeats) → `PATCH /objectives/{id}` (**O-1**: the satellite IS "the editable working copy frozen at check-in" — its own docstring; Draft|UnderRevision only, `model_fields_set` explicit-null semantics [null CLEARS the 3 nullables, 422s the 4 required], policy_id mirrors create's Effective-POL check) → the **revision-aware submit** (T9; ⚠ **the S-obj-3 freeze guard INVERTS on a revision** — the latest version is v1's *Effective* one whose snapshot HAS a commitment, so `is None` would SKIP the freeze and T9 would IllegalTransition; the new rule is the pure `commitment_needs_freeze`: freeze iff latest is None OR latest isn't a Draft OR the working commitment ≠ the latest frozen one — an unchanged re-submit still dedups; optional `change_reason` body lands on the frozen version, significance always MAJOR; the start-revision WD is deleted IN-txn + its lock released POST-commit, the generic-checkin pattern) → re-approve → re-release (the UNCHANGED `_cutover` supersedes v1 — INV-1; **micro-call B**: a unit-changing re-release resets `current_value` to NULL — rag honestly `unmeasured` until a new-unit reading; a same-unit revision PRESERVES it, test-pinned). **The read-back switch (O-3, F-2 closed): every grading read resolves the GOVERNING frozen commitment** — `list_objectives`/`get_objective` outerjoin `metadata_snapshot['objective_commitment']` via `current_effective_version_id` (a per-row PK probe, the drift_report precedent — the feared N+1 never existed; register/scorecard stay ONE query), the `_objective` serializer resolves through the pure `parse_commitment`/`resolve_commitment` (⚠ snapshot values are build_commitment STRINGS — re-parse to Decimal/enum/date before `rules.py` or it TypeErrors; pre-first-release output is provably bit-identical), and **`record_measurement` validates unit + freezes `target_at_capture` against the governing commitment (O-2)** — a mid-revision edit can never leak an unapproved target into WORM evidence; ⚠ its governing read is `populate_existing` but **NO doc-row lock** (it holds the qo FOR UPDATE — a doc lock would invert `_load_objective_doc`'s doc→satellite order); ⚠ **the `current_value` rollup now unit-filters** (review catch: an old-unit backfilled reading would otherwise re-roll garbage against the new-unit target, resurrecting exactly what micro-call B reset). Detail gains **`pending_commitment`** (the diverging working commitment, null otherwise — detail-only beside capabilities/effective_from) + capabilities `edit`/`start_revision` (micro-call C: identical to `submit` — all `objective.manage`, state-blind, split so the contract self-describes). **The byte-path guard (O-5): `reject_objective_byte_path` 422s (`objective_managed_via_objectives`) at FOUR writers** — `checkout`+`checkin` service-level (FIRST statement, before lock/WD — deterministic), generic `start-revision`+`submit-review` ENDPOINT-level (⚠ the guard cannot live in the shared vault functions — the objective endpoints call them); reads stay open (the approver card needs `/versions`); ⚠ the dangerous bypass was generic **submit** (it skips the content-aware freeze → could advance a stale/commitment-less version toward an Effective-OBJ-with-no-commitment). **FE**: Start-revision (Effective+caps), the **calm revision panel** REPLACING the stepper while UnderRevision (O-6a — the latest-instance read still returns v1's completed cycle, which would render "Not yet released" against a doc that IS released), `EditCommitmentModal` (seeds **`pending_commitment ?? main fields`** — the main fields are GOVERNING, seeding from them would silently revert a prior edit; full-body PATCH, explicit-null clears; warn-not-block BandPreview), `ProposedRevisionCard` (was→now of changed fields only), register **state chips on non-Effective rows** (O-6c — fixes the pre-existing Draft-invisibility; `ObjectiveState` is now a `DocumentCurrentState` alias so the shared StateBadge just works), and the `/tasks` approver card's **was→now delta** (O-6b) + the previously comment-only newest-first `.find` pin is now a **two-commitment-version regression test**. ⚠ Review catches worth carrying: (1) the approver's "was" must be **the newest commitment-bearing version that is `version_state=Effective`, NEVER `[1]` blindly** — a changes_requested→PATCH→re-submit cycle leaves a commitment-BEARING orphan Draft at [1], and on a first-release cycle there is no governing version at all (a phantom "revision" framing) — version-state-filtered + orphan-regression-pinned; (2) the edit modal must **never let an errored/loading policy read DECIDE `policy_id`** — preserve the seeded link (the S-home-1 lesson applied to WRITES, not just copy; the create modal was safe only because no link existed to lose); (3) MSW capabilities fixtures can never split submit/edit/start_revision (one server-side answer). Deferrals carried (named-not-faked): abandon-revision (T8 — MVP-deferred for ALL documents; an UnderRevision objective only moves forward), approval-cycle history (latest-instance only — v1's cycle leaves the stepper at re-submit; the audit trail holds it), the post-commit lock-release crash window (≤8h TTL, parity with generic checkin), mgmt-review routing, Process-Owner `objective.manage`, KPI charts (N6), org-tunable RAG (v1.x), title edits (document metadata, not commitment). +18 api tests (5 unit [incl. the freeze-matrix + strict-parse pins], 14-test `test_objective_revision.py` integration file − the deleted open-seam pin), +24 web (679→703); subagent-driven TDD (14 implementer/review dispatches; the two non-trivial review catches above were found by per-task quality reviews). **The Quality Objectives family is now revision-complete.** Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-12-s-obj-4-commitment-revision*`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVE LIFECYCLE — release a Quality Objective to Effective — flips the 6.2 ★ COVERED

- **S-obj-3** Objective lifecycle & release (clause 6.2) — **MIGRATION-FREE backend-led slice** (head stays `0049`, catalog stays 100, R2 closed — no new key/meaning/table) that **closes the S-obj-1/2/S-home-1 deferral**: objectives stop being permanently-Draft, and one released OBJ flips the **6.2 ★ checklist node COVERED** (proven live: PARTIAL→COVERED, `effective_count` 0→1). **The freeze** (the S-rec-3 `form_template` recipe): `domain/objectives/commitment.py::build_commitment` makes the canonical commitment dict (target/unit/direction/due/threshold/baseline/policy_id — **decimals as STRINGS**, never float; `current_value` stays OUTSIDE the version) → `rfc8785` → `put_staging_bytes`/`finalize_worm` (`application/json` → `no_controlled_rendition` R26, no garbage CONTROLLED COPY) → a Draft `document_version` whose `metadata_snapshot.objective_commitment` is the **SAME dict** (bytes≡snapshot); the shared `_snapshot` extended by **ONE optional kwarg**, never branched (ordinary docs byte-identical, unit-pinned). ⚠ Unlike `checkin_form_schema`, `checkin_objective_commitment` **FLUSHES, never commits** — it is a sub-step of `submit_objective_for_review` (409-unless-Draft → freeze-**iff-no-version** [a request_changes→re-submit advances the SAME Draft version — T3 reverts version_state, so T2's from-state check holds] → T2 → `instantiate_approval` → audit, ONE txn); and it **flushes BEFORE `_emit`** (the `default=uuid.uuid4` id is a FLUSH-time default — the legacy `checkin`/`checkin_form_schema` emit pre-flush and their CHECKIN audit rows carried no real version id — FIXED in-PR: flush-before-emit in both + an object_id regression pin; historic NULL rows stay, the chain is append-only). **The lifecycle rides the proven machinery unchanged**: the approval is the DOCUMENT `/tasks` decide leg (`instantiate_approval` hardcodes subject_type=DOCUMENT; `document.approve` + SoD author≠approver — the submitter IS the frozen version's `author_user_id`), release is the shared SERIALIZABLE `_cutover` via `POST /objectives/{id}/release` (imperative `enforce("document.release", sig_hook=True)` over the `enrich_release_sod_scope`-enriched scope — SoD-2 author-can't-release proven by integration test; ⚠ `release()` commits in its OWN session → **`session.expire_all()` before the re-read** or the serializer reads the pre-release identity map). Submit gates on **`objective.manage`** (ownership puts it up for review; the cryptographic sign-offs stay document.*) — keeps the slice migration-free (no role-grant seed). Reads: `GET /objectives/{id}/approval` (**`objective.read`**-gated — the QMS Owner may hold no `document.read`; local `_approval_instance`/`_task` serializers field-equivalent to workflow.py's), detail-only `capabilities {submit,release}` + `effective_from` (⚠ a DETAIL response **always carries `effective_from`, null until Effective** — the `_document` precedent; list/scorecard rows omit both — and the additions were **load-bearing in the contract**: `Objective` has `additionalProperties:false`, so an undocumented key would 422 schema validation), `GET /objectives/policy` (the Effective POL `{id,identifier,title}|null` — **declared BEFORE `/{objective_id}`**, the scorecard/S-pack-2 route-order lesson, in FastAPI AND MSW). ⚠ The S-drift-1 trap bit TWICE: the submit handler's `for_update` load needs `populate_existing` on **BOTH** the doc AND the `quality_objective` satellite (the authz resolver identity-mapped both; a stale satellite would freeze yesterday's commitment once a commitment-edit path exists). **FE**: the detail page's Lifecycle card (Submit gated `caps.submit`+Draft · the REUSED `ApprovalStepper` — `ObjectiveState` is structurally `DocumentCurrentState` so no cast · Release gated `caps.release`+Approved · AuthorActions-style error Alert); the `/tasks` DOCUMENT leg renders **`ObjectiveCommitmentContext`** (the frozen commitment card) instead of the redline — detection keys on **`metadata_snapshot.objective_commitment` presence, never the document type** (forms=`field_schema`, plain docs=neither; versions are newest-first by `version_seq DESC` so `.find(Boolean)` picks the InReview commitment in the revision era); the create modal's **policy checkbox** (`useEffectivePolicy`; sends `policy_id` only when checked). ⚠ **diff-critic MINOR (fixed, the S-home-1 green-on-error class):** the modal's policy fallback claimed the positive "No effective Quality Policy yet — you can link one later" on a LOADING/ERRORED read, and "later" was a false promise (the commitment freezes `policy_id` at submit; no edit path) → branch on `isError` → neutral "Couldn't load the Quality Policy — you can still create the objective" + the no-policy copy now says "the link is optional". Live smoke (worker heredoc, service-layer): create→submit→approve→release = Effective + the exact frozen snapshot + 6.2 COVERED + `approval`+`release` signatures on the version. Deferrals (named-not-faked): **commitment-revision-edit** (first-release only in v1 — no commitment-edit endpoint, so UnderRevision re-freeze is pointless; when it lands, ALSO switch Effective-objective reads to the frozen snapshot [F-2's deferred half] and widen the FE Submit gate); ⚠ **the generic `checkout`/`checkin` byte-path is an unguarded seam on an OBJ** (no v1 UI offers it, but a generic checkin on a Draft OBJ would suppress the freeze, and on an Effective OBJ a v2 byte-checkin would show a stale v1 commitment to the approver — guard it when the revision slice lands); management-review approval routing (the OBJ rides the generic `document_approval` pool); Process-Owner `objective.manage`. +14 api tests (4 unit + 10 integration), +18 web tests (659→677); subagent-driven TDD (10 dispatches, per-dispatch spec+quality review; diff-critic = 1 MINOR, fixed). **The Quality Objectives family is now lifecycle-complete.** Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-11-s-obj-3-objective-lifecycle*`.

## v1.x PDCA DASHBOARD — the QMS Health home wheel (front-end-only) — CLOSES the v1 web track

- **S-home-1** the PDCA Home dashboard (QMS Health, doc 11 §5.1) — **the v1 web-track FINALE; FRONT-END ONLY** (no migration/key/endpoint/contract; head stays `0049`, catalog stays 100). Replaces the `HomePage.tsx` placeholder with the calm four-quadrant **PLAN/DO/CHECK/ACT wheel** (the doc-11 "nav of four labeled regions" — a 2×2 of `QuadrantCard`s, **NOT a donut**) composing **already-shipped reads** client-side, each tile degrading independently. Surfaces: a header **`HealthSummary`** band (★ mandatory coverage `{covered} / {total} mandatory items current` from `useComplianceChecklist().rollup`, a `coverageRag` badge, the **N9 microcopy** "status against configured thresholds — not a compliance verdict" — there is NO "Certified-ready" verdict; the whole band drills to `/compliance`); **PLAN** (objectives on-target `{on_target} / {total}` + `by_rag` from `useObjectiveScorecard` [server RAG **read verbatim, never recomputed** — N9] + `rollup.overdue_review`; → `/objectives`); **DO** (mirror & blob integrity from `useDriftStatus` [`driftRag` over `scans.{MIRROR,BLOB_REHASH}.status` + `blob_coverage.failing`] + superseded-copies count + `useAckCount`; → `/drift`); **CHECK** (open audits `state!=="Closed"` from `useAudits` + `{covered} / {total}` coverage; → `/audits`); **ACT** (open CAPAs `close_state∉{Closed,Rejected}` + NCRs `disposition===null` + complaints `spawned_capa_id===null`; → `/capa`); and a **`MyTasksRail`** (the self-scoped `useMyTasks` = `GET /tasks?assignee=me&state=PENDING`, count + top-3 by `due_at`, showing **type + action + due, NOT the doc name** — the LIST omits `subject_*`, the `useAckCount` precedent; → `/tasks`). Pure `rag.ts` rules (`planObjectivesRag`/`coverageRag`/`overdueRag`/`countRag`/`driftRag`/`worstRag` + the count filters), unit-tested; **tile RAG = `worstRag` of only the VISIBLE RAG-bearing signals** (a forbidden/errored read contributes no RAG, so it can never drag a tile red; the informational counts — audits/superseded/acks — never colour a tile). Per-signal & per-tile **calm-403 degrade** (each read's `forbidden` flag, `retry:false`): a forbidden signal omits its line, an all-forbidden tile shows `TileNoAccess`, the wheel never crashes. Under the **bare `demo` login only DO + My-Tasks light up** (`drift.read` + self-scoped tasks); the rest need SYSTEM overrides on the live `app_user` row (org **AHT**). ⚠ **diff-critic MINOR (fixed):** DoCard's empty-state fallback is reachable ONLY on a drift **non-403 error** with zero acks (a drift success always pushes the integrity line; forbidden+0-acks hits `TileNoAccess`) — so it must render a **neutral "Couldn't load this section.", NOT a green "You're all caught up."** (which painted a green health state over an errored integrity read); fixed to match the three sibling cards + a regression test. Deferrals (named-not-faked): the precise **open-NC findings count** (no org-wide findings endpoint — per-audit only; the findings payload can't see the linked CAPA's close-state — owner-chosen defer); **"next management review in N days"** (no `ManagementReview` entity), **"high risks open"** (no surfaced `risk_opportunity` register), **"documents pending approval" org-wide** (no endpoint — personal approvals live in the rail); the **6.2 ★ checklist node stays not-COVERED** (objective lifecycle/release is unwired, so CHECK coverage honestly reads e.g. 18/20 — not papered over); **KPI charts/sparklines** (N6); **org-configurable RAG thresholds** (v1.x — coded defaults ship now); the **density control + Process-Map header chrome** (no density system in v1). ⚠ Web traps re-confirmed: the `findByRole` on a card resolves on the immediately-rendered frame while the data line is still a skeleton → the **first content assertion must `waitFor`**; the `MyTasksRail` heading + "See all my tasks" both match `/my tasks/i` → assert with `getAllByText`; the decorative `→`/`See all` arrows are `aria-hidden` so they stay out of a link's accessible name. +32 web tests (627→659); subagent-driven TDD (per-phase spec + quality review; final **diff-critic = 1 MINOR, fixed**). **The v1 web track is now feature-complete.** Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-11-s-home-1-pdca-dashboard*`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVES family — Quality Objectives backend (clause 6.2) (0049) → the UI tail (front-end-only) → S-obj-charts adds the KPI trend chart (closes the S-obj-2 "trend charts" deferral)

- **S-obj-charts** KPI trend charts (clause 6.2) — replaces the `MeasurementsSection.tsx:53` "Trend charts arrive in a later release" placeholder on `/objectives/:id` with a **hand-rolled SVG `ObjectiveTrendChart`** (value-over-period line + a stepped dashed **target reference line** [`target_at_capture` per reading, so it steps when a commitment is revised] + **per-reading RAG-coloured points** + legend + `↑/↓` direction caption), above the existing append-only table. **CLOSES the S-obj-2-named "KPI trend charts/sparklines (v1.x)" deferral.** Mostly FE; ONE small backend touch. **Migration-free (head stays `0051`), no new key/endpoint/enum, catalog 100**; gates `/check-api` + `/check-contracts` + `/check-web`. **Backend (Fork A):** `api/objectives.py::_measurement` gains a per-reading **`rag`** computed server-side via the existing pure `rag_status` rule — **value vs the FROZEN `target_at_capture`** (so a later target edit can't rewrite a past verdict), with `direction`/`at_risk_threshold` from the **GOVERNING** commitment (`resolve_commitment(gov, …)` resolved once at BOTH call sites: the GET-list and the POST-record endpoints) → + the contract `Measurement.rag` (enum `[green,amber,red,unmeasured]`) + the FE `Measurement` type. The unknown-id branch still returns `200 {"data":[]}` (no new 404). **The chart reads `m.rag` verbatim — never re-derives RAG (N9).** No new imports (all symbols already imported in `objectives.py`). **Owner F-decisions:** **hand-rolled SVG** (zero new deps, D4-clean — confirmed no existing chart lib in `apps/web`; the ⌘K-palette/redline house pattern); **detail-page only** (register sparklines = Fork B, deferred — needs the per-objective series in the list response); **server-side RAG points** (additive serializer field, the rule stays server-side per N9). **The SVG:** reverses the newest-first series to oldest-left; `Number()`-parses the decimal strings; y-domain `[min,max]` over values∪targets padded ~8%, **never forced to 0**, degenerate-domain guarded; categorical x (thinned period labels); value polyline only at n≥2; a full-width horizontal target line at n=1; per-point circles filled via a LOCAL `RAG_FILL` of `var(--mantine-color-*-6)` (the `BandPreview` `ZONE_COLOR` idiom — CSS vars, NOT the `labels.ts` `RAG_COLOR` name tokens); native `<title>` tooltips; `role="img"` + a meaningful `aria-label`. ⚠ **THE load-bearing correction (Codex ③, against my own spec):** the "frozen verdict" is **PARTIAL** — **only `target_at_capture` is frozen**; `direction`/`at_risk_threshold` come from the governing commitment, so a commitment revision that changes **DIRECTION or threshold re-grades historical readings** (a HIGHER→LOWER flip rewrites green/red, not just the amber band — my spec's "green/red stays exact" was WRONG). **Owner decision: keep migration-free; treat per-reading RAG as DESCRIPTIVE (N9), not an immutable stored verdict** — documented honestly in the spec caveat + the `_measurement` comment; truly freezing the verdict needs `direction_at_capture`+`threshold_at_capture` columns (a migration that also **can't retroactively** freeze pre-existing readings) → **named v1.x deferral**. ⚠ **Other traps a future session must carry:** **(1)** a chart that **filters its input** (same-unit — a unit-changing revision leaves old-unit rows incomparable on one axis; the chart filters to the governing unit, **mirroring the backend same-unit rollup**, with the off-unit rows staying in the table) must still **EXPLAIN an empty result, never `return null` silently** (Codex ④ — when ALL readings are off-unit, render "in a previous unit — no comparable trend"); **(2)** **NEVER round a displayed reading value** (`toFixed` made `94.999`→"95"/looking on-target while graded amber, and `0.005`→"0") — render the **raw decimal string** in tooltips + the aria-label summary; reserve rounding for **computed axis ticks** with **adaptive precision from the domain span** (Codex ⑤); **(3)** a one-coordinate `<polyline>` renders nothing — a single-reading target needs a full-width 2-point segment (Codex ②). **Reviews:** diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer **CLEAN**; subagent-driven TDD (3 implementers [backend + chart parallel, integration after] + 3 per-task quality reviews, all clean); **Codex 5 real findings over 2 rounds (3×P2 round 1: same-unit filter / single-reading target / the ③ caveat-correction; P3+P2 round 2: ④ off-unit-explanation [introduced by my round-1 filter] / ⑤ raw-decimal labels), all fixed + threads resolved, round 3 clean** ("Didn't find any major issues") — the Codex-finds-what-the-CLEAN-diff-critic-misses lesson REPEATS (incl. correcting a spec claim). **Live smoke (full PASS, OBJ-GEN-005):** the chart rendered an amber/amber/red/green spread with a stepping target line (98→99), the **frozen-verdict semantics showed live** (96-vs-frozen-98 = amber, not 96-vs-governing-99), and recording a measurement via the UI **live-updated** the chart 4→5 points; (2) A **persistently-mounted modal keeps its post-error/typed-field state across reopens** → conditionally render the modal in its PARENT (`{open && <Modal .../>}`) so close unmounts+resets it (the S-web-7d lesson) + a reopen-resets regression test. (3) the register's RAG-filter state was **dead** until wired into a real control (don't `void` a setter — implement the in-spec filter).
