## v1.x DRIFT family — D5 re-review (0045) → D2+D3 mirror tamper/staleness scan (0046) → D1+D4+admin surface (0047)

- **S-drift-3** D1 blob verify + D4 superseded-copies + the admin drift-status surface (`0047`) — **COMPLETES the drift family's detection legs (D1–D5 all shipped)**. Mig `0047`: `drift_scan_kind +=
BLOB_REHASH` (the S-drift-2 seam), `event_type += BLOB_INTEGRITY_FAILED`, and the **R41**
`drift.read` SYSTEM key (catalog 98→99; seeded + granted to System Administrator via the resilient
org lookup — this install renamed the short_code). Owner forks: a NEW `drift.read` key over riding
`storage.read` (the D4 report isn't storage; riding widens storage-config readers); ONE
`BLOB_INTEGRITY_FAILED` event (classification HASH_MISMATCH/OBJECT_MISSING/READ_ERROR in the
payload — no severity split exists, unlike MIRROR_STALE/TAMPER); daily rolling cadence where
**rotation IS the periodic full set** (FAILED-pinned first → verified_at NULLS FIRST → oldest,
default 500/day, CLI `--full` on demand). **The alarm latch is the slice's load-bearing call** —
and the diff-critic MAJOR reshaped it: `blob.verified_at` stays the pure "last verified OK" cursor
(stamped on a pass only), while a finding sets **`blob.verify_failed_at`** (mig 0047), the explicit
pin that sorts FIRST in every rolling sample — a finding re-alarms every run until restored (no
auto-correction exists for blobs; restore-from-backup per the new
`runbooks/blob-integrity-verify.md`). ⚠ The original stamp-on-OK-only-without-a-pin design had a
hole: a once-stamped-then-corrupted blob sorts BEHIND every never-verified row, so a NULL-cursor
influx > sample size (a bulk import) crowds a DETECTED corruption out of the daily sample and the
latest-per-kind status read goes CLEAN over it. The status surface exposes the pin directly
(`blob_coverage.failing`). Two sibling diff-critic folds: an `OBJECT_MISSING` finding whose ROW is
gone at persist time was a legal R27 disposal racing the scan → pruned (info-log), never a
permanent false alarm; the stamp UPDATEs are chunked (10k) under psycopg's 65,535-bind-param cap
and the CLI surfaces a persist failure (warning + exit 1). Per-object errors are findings;
connection-class errors ABORT as FAILED salvaging findings (no noise-event storms when MinIO is
down). D4 is a LIVE
read — `EXPORTED`/`PRINTED` events × now-Superseded/Obsolete versions is sound by construction
(`render_dynamic_copy` only ever serves the then-Effective version); no decrement leg (the `/verify`
token is the per-copy resolution). New surface: `GET /admin/drift/status` +
`GET /admin/drift/superseded-copies` (both `drift.read`; S-web-8 consumes them). Integration
technique: synthetic tamper via planted blob ROWS (a wrong-sha row over real bytes / a row with no
object) — never fight WORM. Spec:
`docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-10-s-drift-3-blob-verify-drift-surface-design.md`.

- **S-drift-2** D2+D3 mirror tamper/staleness scan (`0046`) — **the drift family's THESIS slice**: D2 was *asserted* ("authority flows vault → mirror"), now it is a *verified, audited, self-correcting invariant*. **Migration `0046`:** two operational tables (`mirror_build` = the **vault-side expected-state baseline** [one row per build, keyed by the `.builds/<hex>` dir; `manifest` jsonb with doc-owned entries carrying `document_id`/`version_id`; `manifest_sha256` over the on-disk `_meta/manifest.json`; `swapped_at` the pointer-integrity anchor], `drift_scan` = the per-scan summary [`kind` `MIRROR`; `status` `CLEAN`/`DIVERGENT`/`FAILED`; `counts` jsonb]) + two additive event types `MIRROR_STALE`/`MIRROR_TAMPER` (the 0011 ADD-VALUE pattern). ⚠ **The mirror is never trusted as truth** — the expected state is the PG `mirror_build` manifest, and the on-disk manifest is byte-verified against the stored digest, never read as authority (its non-deterministic `generated_at` makes recompute impossible by design). **The scanner** (`services/vault/mirror_scan.py`, pure-core `compare_tree`/`classify_mismatch`/quarantine + DB orchestration `resolve_pointer`/`scan_mirror`/`persist_scan_results`/`scan_and_sync`): walks the served build tree (`os.walk(followlinks=False)`, NEVER `rglob`) against the baseline → classifies (`STALE_REVISION` = a digest of an OTHER version of the **same** document [`_known_digests` EXCLUDES the expected version — same-version bytes in the wrong role, e.g. raw source over the banded rendition, are TAMPER] → `MIRROR_STALE`; `UNEXPECTED_CONTENT`/`EXTRA`/`MISSING`/`SYMLINK_DIVERGENT`/`POINTER_DIVERGENT` → `MIRROR_TAMPER`) → **QUARANTINES divergent bytes BEFORE any rebuild** (R11: the rebuild prunes the old tree, so scan-first is what preserves forensic evidence; in-tree files copied + re-hashed [`quarantined_sha256` chain of custody], foreign/rogue whole trees moved, into `<mirror>/.quarantine/<ts>__<scan-id>/` at `0o700`) → audits each anomaly (`actor_type=system`; doc-attributable → `object_type=document` + `scope_ref=identifier`, else `config` keyed on the resilient single-org lookup) → writes the `drift_scan` summary → **rebuilds (vault wins)**. ⚠ **Pointer integrity (the CRITICAL fold):** the `current` symlink is **verified against the registry, never trusted** — `resolve_pointer` matches `current`'s target against the newest *swapped* `mirror_build` row; only the relative `.builds/<name>` shape `atomic_swap` writes is parsed (`_parse_current_target` — an absolute/out-of-tree/nested/basename-colliding target classifies **foreign → MIRROR_TAMPER**, raw string as evidence, NEVER resolved against the filesystem); a missing `current` → `missing`, a real-dir `current` → `rogue_dir` (moved aside to unblock the swap), an older swapped build → `rollback`, the swap-then-crash window → `selfheal` (persist stamps `swapped_at`); only an **empty registry** is the benign no-baseline (fresh install / pre-0046 upgrade — zero false alarms). ⚠ A **destroyed or symlink-swapped served `.builds/<name>` tree** is `MIRROR_TAMPER` (`POINTER_DIVERGENT`) + `is_current` stays False so the hourly path rebuilds — NOT a silent CLEAN (a bare `is_dir()` guard that follows symlinks was the C1 quality-review catch). **Composition (owner fork §0.1):** one scan-first pipeline — **every** `sync_mirror` scans the outgoing tree first (R11's per-sync leg; the `mirror_build` insert + the current-target-protected keep-last-20 prune + the post-swap `swapped_at` stamp all moved inside the session scope), and a **NEW hourly Beat `easysynq.mirror.scan`** (`MIRROR_SCAN_INTERVAL_SECONDS`, default 3600 = the accepted drift window) runs the same pipeline, rebuilding only on DIVERGENT/behind-vault/no-baseline and NEVER on `FAILED` (a scan failure is not evidence the mirror is wrong; the sync path still rebuilds — the correction must never be blocked). Both serialize under `LOCK_MIRROR_SYNC`. ⚠ **Lock/persist hardening:** `scan_mirror` is DB-READ-ONLY and **never raises** (an infra failure → an honest `FAILED` report that SALVAGES already-classified findings so persist still audits them); `persist_scan_results` returns success and a persist failure WITH findings **defers the rebuild** (it would erase the on-disk evidence the next scan needs); after a FAILED scan or failed persist the pipeline **re-verifies advisory-lock ownership** (`holds_advisory_lock`, `objsubid=1`) before rebuilding — a mid-scan connection loss silently frees the session-level lock and a lockless rebuild could race a concurrent sync's prune. CLI `easysynq mirror scan` (scan-only) / `sync` / `rebuild` (the force-clear scoped `WHERE version_state == Effective`, committed BEFORE the pipeline). **No new permission key, no endpoint, no contract change** (the admin drift-status read surface is S-drift-3). **Tests:** 19 unit (the classification matrix · the pointer matrix · `_parse_current_target` · quarantine copy/move/rehash · counts math · the FAILED family · gate-order persist-before-rebuild) + 12 integration (Linux CI: tamper→quarantine→audit→correct, stale [source + older-rendition], behind-vault-not-tamper, foreign/rollback/destroyed-tree pointer cases, foreign-tree quarantine-by-move, the protected keep-N prune, the FAILED row, the real task-path lock skip-tick). **4-lens pass folded** (1 CRITICAL pointer-integrity + 8 MAJOR before code) + per-task spec+quality subagent review (C1 destroyed-tree, the out-of-tree basename-collision bypass, salvage-into-FAILED among the catches). **Deferred residuals:** the admin drift-status surface + the trailing UI (S-drift-3 / S-web-8); D1 blob re-hash + D4 superseded-copies report (S-drift-3, which reuses `drift_scan` with `kind=BLOB_REHASH` additively); the by-move × persist-failure window (best-effort, documented); the `built_at`-tiebreak determinism note (practically distinct microsecond timestamps under `LOCK_MIRROR_SYNC`); **the advisory-lock connection-pinning P1 (Codex round 5) — assessed NOT reachable** (per-task `create_async_engine` = isolated pools + the global `pg_try_advisory_lock` at task entry serialize workers; two backends can't both be the lock holder), owner-accepted deferral with a re-evaluation trigger (if these tasks ever share a process-wide engine/pool) recorded in the spec §11a. ⚠ **Codex did 6 review rounds on #108** (5 P1/P2 clusters all in the adversarial-filesystem surface — symlink/special/raw-collision at `current`/`.builds`/`.quarantine`, STALE-class precision, salvage ordering, lock recheck); all fixed except the round-5 pin (pushed back + documented). Owner steer (2026-06-10): disregard further nitpicks/unreachable items, document them, squash-merge on green.

- **S-drift-1** D5 scheduled re-review currency sweep (`0045`) — **opened the v1.x drift family**. **Migration `0045`:** three nullable columns on `documented_information` (`review_period_months` INTEGER — **NOT interval**: psycopg3 cannot load month-bearing PG intervals into `timedelta`, so the column is plain int months; `next_review_due` DATE STORED, reset from the review date on confirm and recomputed on release/PATCH; `last_reviewed_at` timestamptz) + a **partial index `ix_documented_information_next_review_due` on (next_review_due) WHERE NOT NULL** (the Beat sweep's scan path) + additive event types `REVIEW_CONFIRMED`/`REVIEW_OVERDUE` + the seeded single-stage `periodic_review` workflow definition. ⚠ **Org-lookup trap:** the seed uses a `scalar_one_or_none` on `short_code='DEFAULT'` with a `SELECT the only org` fallback — `0038`/`0043`'s verbatim `scalar_one` on `'DEFAULT'` would ABORT an OPERATIONAL install's upgrade because setup G-E renames the short_code (this install = `AHT`); those earlier migrations only "ran clean" because they pre-dated setup. The engine gained an additive `context_users` assignee-spec key in `_resolve_pool` (role path byte-identical) + `instantiate` widened to `actor: AppUser | None` (system sweeps). **Write paths:** create default = 24 months; T2 **AUTO-DEFAULT at submit** (not a 422 — a legacy doc must not strand at submit while the SPA lacks the field, pre-S-web-8); `next_review_due` recomputed on release (`_cutover`, both T6 + scheduled), on confirm, and on PATCH. **ONE rule:** anchor = the LATER of (`last_reviewed_at`, `effective_from`), org-tz dated, + months (`add_months` day-clamped). `PATCH /documents/{id}` accepts `review_period_months` (ge=1 le=120; `null` = opt-out; `model_fields_set` distinguishes omitted vs explicit-null); loads the doc lock-aware. `review_period_months` joins the version `metadata_snapshot` + the `SNAPSHOT_FIELDS` metadata-diff. **Daily Beat sweep `easysynq.documents.review_sweep`** (Beat key `documents-review-sweep`): advisory-lock single-flight (`LOCK_REVIEW_SWEEP`) — `acks_late` re-delivery makes concurrent runs real, and no schema constraint stops two open instances per subject; 30-day lead window; instantiates the seeded `periodic_review` definition per due Effective doc (idempotent open-instance check; subject `PERIODIC_REVIEW`; owner-assigned via `context_users`); task `due_at` = org-tz midnight of `next_review_due`; escalation = once-per-CYCLE `REVIEW_OVERDUE` audit (dedup anchored on `after.instance_id`). ⚠ **Task state is NEVER flipped on escalation**: `engine.decide()` accepts ONLY `PENDING` (engine.py:390) — an `ESCALATED` task would be undecidable. **Decision dispatch** `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` `PERIODIC_REVIEW` → `decide_periodic_review`: 404-COLLAPSE non-membership (never 403) + **live-owner re-check** (`doc.owner_user_id` NOW, with the doc row `FOR UPDATE` — the `context_users` analogue of the siblings' live role re-check); outcomes `complete` ("no change needed" → `signature_event(meaning=review_confirmed)` bound to the Effective version id + its `source_blob_sha256` digest + `REVIEW_CONFIRMED` audit `[scope_ref=identifier]` + `last_reviewed_at=now` + clock reset) | `changes_requested` (→ instance `REJECTED`, NO clock reset — the sweep re-nags while the doc stays Effective and due); a doc obsoleted mid-review → 409 with full txn rollback (task stays `PENDING`). **Read surface:** 4 fields on the `_document` serializer (`review_period_months`, `next_review_due`, `last_reviewed_at`, `review_state` derived `current|due_soon|overdue` — never stored) on detail + list; the compliance checklist's previously-deferred doc 13 "overdue review" leg (`overdue_review` bool per ★ row + rollup count). Contract: `Document`/`MetadataUpdate`/`ChecklistRow`/`ChecklistRollup` additions + `Decision`/`DecisionResult` gain outcome `complete` + 3 nullable result keys. **Unblocks:** `next_review_due` / the "Days to review" tile (deferred since S-web-1), the checklist overdue UI leg (S-web-6 §3.1), currency reporting toward metric M3 (<5% overdue). **Tests:** 24 targeted unit + 17 new/extended integration (Linux CI); 9 implementation commits. **Deferred residuals:** the grace→Finding optional policy (doc 04 §9.1 row 3); org-config default period/lead window (constants 24mo/30d in v1); the dedicated currency/overdue report endpoint (v1.x reporting family); ALL UI (trailing S-web-8 after the family); D1–D4 (S-drift-2 ✅ mirror tamper/staleness scan; S-drift-3 blob integrity verify + the D4 superseded-copies report).

Owner decisions **R40**: DCR is an own-table mutable-state workflow object [R22, NOT a record] · the InApproval changes-requested loop targets **Open** [doc 15 §8.7, superseding doc 05 §5.5's Routed] · keys = the seeded `changeRequest.*` family [R5] · scope-forks: **full** diff [meta+text+visual] + a **doc↔doc link table** for where-used · scheduled re-review D5 + drift D1–D4 stay in the v1.x drift family.

- **S-dcr-1** the DCR core + intake (`0040`) — `dcr` own-table (mutable `state` FSM Open→…→Closed/Cancelled/Rejected; `DCR-{YYYY}-{SEQ}` 4-digit id; `target_document_id` NULL⟺CREATE via the `ck_dcr_create_iff_no_target` CHECK; `source_link_id` polymorphic no-FK; `resulting_version_id` nullable seam) + append-only `dcr_stage_event` (`REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE`; `signed_event_id` FK present, populated S-dcr-4) + 4 enums + pure `domain/dcr/fsm.py` (InApproval changes-requested loop → Open; cancel from {Open,Assessed,Routed} only) + `audit_object_type=dcr` + `DCR_RAISED`/`DCR_UPDATED`/`DCR_TRANSITIONED`. - **S-dcr-2** where-used / impact + assess (`0041`) — the NEW `document_link` doc↔doc graph (`parent_of`/`child_of`/`references`/`supersedes`; editable metadata `GRANT SELECT,INSERT,DELETE`, the `clause_mapping` precedent; CRUD `POST/GET/DELETE /documents/{id}/links` on `document.manage_metadata`) + `impact_assessment` (one row per the 7 doc-05-§5.3 dimensions, `UNIQUE(dcr_id,dimension)`) + `GET /documents/{id}/where-used` (`document.read` — the §7.2 categories over `process_link`/`document_link`/`clause_mapping`/records/`dcr.source_link`) + the pure §7.3 `obsoletion_blocked` predicate SURFACED as a `where-used.obsoletion_safety` advisory (governs-active-process / referenced-by-Effective / sole-★-coverage) — **enforcement deferred to S-dcr-5** per the R40 addendum (the shipped `document.obsolete` untouched) + `POST /dcrs/{id}/assess` (Open→Assessed; mirrors `cancel_dcr` + UPSERTs the impact rows from where-used in one txn; a CREATE DCR → all-N/A) + `GET/PUT /dcrs/{id}/impact`. NO new keys, NO Celery task. The S-dcr-1 `_dcr_doc_scope` (R28 process_ids) gates assess.
- **S-dcr-3a** redline/diff core (**ZERO-migration**, head stays `0041`) — `GET /documents/{id}/versions/{vid}/diff?from={vid2}` (gate **`document.read_draft`** — the diff exposes non-released version content, so `document.read` alone would leak Draft text to an Employee/Guest). The two doc-05-§8.1 core dimensions: **metadata diff** (pure `domain/diff/metadata.py` over the frozen `metadata_snapshot` SNAPSHOT_FIELDS) + **text redline** (pure `domain/diff/text.py` `difflib` line-LCS over on-demand Tika text via a `TextExtractor` seam; fail-closed → `text_diff: unavailable`) + the **provenance header** (`signature_event[]` projected to `{signer_user_id}` only). `document.diff` NOT seeded — the diff rides `document.read_draft` (R5). Owner chose **full diff incl. visual** → delivered as 3a + 3b.
- **S-dcr-3b** the visual page-image diff (`0042`) — **worker-async** (owner chose full coverage over in-request-PDF-only, since the **API can't render**: `LoggingRenderSink` no-op; rendering is worker-only). Deps **pypdfium2** (Apache/BSD prebuilt wheels — NOT PyMuPDF/fitz, passes `test_no_pymupdf_or_fitz_in_lockfile`; no system dep / air-gap impact) + Pillow `ImageChops`. NEW `visual_diff` cache table (`UNIQUE(from,to)` idempotency latch + cache key; `VisualDiffStatus` Pending/Ready/Failed/Unavailable; GRANT SELECT,INSERT,UPDATE — regenerable cache, not append-only) + `easysynq.visual_diff` Celery task (FOR-UPDATE + early-return-on-terminal idempotent; `acks_late` redelivery + re-POST self-heal — **no Beat reaper**) + pure `domain/diff/visual.py` (pypdfium2 rasterize @ scale 2.0 / cap 100 pages + Pillow per-page `ImageChops` overlay) + `services/diff/visual.py`. The task obtains each version's PDF (cache-hit on the mirror `rendition_blob_sha256`; else render via the worker's `GotenbergRenderSink` **TRANSIENTLY — NEVER writes `rendition_blob_sha256`**, else a Draft's diff-rendition [copy_status=state, no verify QR] would POISON the mirror's controlled-copy cache when it goes Effective — the diff-critic-preempted catch), rasterizes both, diffs page-by-page, caches each page's from/to/diff PNG as a content-addressed non-WORM `Blob` (no purge wiring — verified no path deletes a `document_version`'s blobs). Contract = **POST-compute (202) + pure-GET-poll (404-before-request) + `GET .../visual-diff/page/{n}?layer=from|to|diff` PNG stream** (the design-critic-mandated shape; the packs/imports async precedent), all gated `document.read_draft`. Watermark band-noise (footer band differs by rev → a changed footer region) accepted + documented for v1 (raw-render = v1.x). NO new permission key / event type. **The doc 05 §8 full diff (metadata + text + visual) is COMPLETE.**

- **S-dcr-4** routing + approval (`0043`) — DCR approval via the declarative engine (subject_type=DCR, the S-capa-2 pattern). Migration 0043 = ONE `signed_object_type ADD VALUE 'dcr'` (workflow_subject_type.DCR already existed from 0008) + the seeded `dcr_approval` `workflow_definition` (**ROUTER on `change_significance`**: MAJOR → `major_proc` [Process Owner, ANY] → `major_qms` [QMS Owner, ANY] SEQUENTIAL; MINOR → `minor_qms` [QMS Owner, ANY]; reuses the existing roles, no new role) + the `changeRequest.route` grant-backfill (Process Owner + QMS Owner, PROCESS-scoped). `route_dcr` (gate `changeRequest.route`): Assessed→Routed→InApproval atomically — instantiates the workflow w/ `context={change_significance}`; NEEDS_ATTENTION (empty pool) → fail-fast 409 `dcr_no_approvers` (rolls back, DCR stays Assessed). `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` extended with a **DCR dispatch** (DOCUMENT/CAPA byte-identical) → `decide_dcr_approval`: **per-approver signatures** (doc 05 §5.4 — EACH approve writes `signature_event(meaning=approval, signed_object_type='dcr', signed_object_id=<DCR id>)`; a MAJOR DCR → TWO; the `dcr_stage_event(InApproval→Approved).signed_event_id` links the sealing one); on the COMPLETING approve it flips →Approved + sets `decision/decided_by/decided_at`. **reject (→Rejected) / changes_requested (→Open, R40 loop) is DECISIVE** — one approver force-terminates the instance (`current_state=REJECTED` + skip sibling PENDING tasks under the instance lock), since the engine's ANY quorum won't fail on a single negative with other live candidates; a re-route opens a FRESH instance. Authz = `_assert_dcr_approver` (candidate-pool + live-role 404-collapse + cross-stage distinct-approver 409; NO key — `changeRequest.approve` stays ungranted, the CAPA precedent). NO new permission key / event type / Celery task.

- **S-dcr-5** implement/close + the shared-path obsoletion gate + the CAPA→DCR loop (`0044`) — **CLOSES the DCR family.** **DCR-as-orchestrator** (owner, reconciling doc 05/15's "DCR drives the release" over doc 10's "spawn-a-revision"): `POST /dcrs/{id}/implement` (gate `changeRequest.implement`, already-seeded) drives the vault action **atomically by construction** — REVISE releases the target's Approved revision / CREATE releases the authored `resulting_version_id` / RETIRE obsoletes — by setting the version's `effective_from` (`proposed_effective_from` or now) + the cross-FK link + flip→Implemented in ONE commit, then the EXISTING `release_due` Beat sweep performs the SERIALIZABLE single-Effective cutover (DCR-driven release = system-attributed; **no `_cutover` change, no new reaper**); RETIRE folds the flip into `lifecycle.obsolete`'s own commit. **No DCR side-door past document control**: the implement endpoint ALSO `enforce`s `document.release` (REVISE/CREATE, full SoD-2 overlay — the PDP keys SoD on `document.release`, so a hand-rolled check would skip the approver-side leg) / `document.obsolete` (RETIRE) IN ADDITION to `changeRequest.implement` — so a revision's author cannot self-implement (403 `sod_violation`). Shared `enrich_release_sod_scope` (extracted from `documents.py::_release_scope`) is reused by both the direct release endpoint + the implement path. `POST /dcrs/{id}/close` (gate `changeRequest.close`): Implemented→Closed requires the change actually-effective (§5.5; 409 `dcr_effectivity_pending`). **The §7.3 obsoletion gate moves to the SHARED `lifecycle.obsolete()`** — BOTH the direct `POST /documents/{id}/obsolete` AND the DCR RETIRE-implement now 409 `obsoletion_blocked` on a coverage gap unless `force_retire` + `override_justification` (recorded on the signature intent + audit), **superseding the S-dcr-2 addendum** (no bypass; T11-only). The §7.3 reads + `evaluate_obsoletion` centralized in NEW `services/vault/obsoletion.py` (the where-used advisory consumes the same fn — gate + advisory can't diverge; dcr→vault, no cycle; `sole_star_coverage` moved out of `dcr_repo`). **CAPA→DCR loop = dedicated `POST /capas/{id}/raise-dcr`** (gate `changeRequest.create`; `raise_dcr_from_capa` → `raise_dcr(_commit=False, source_link_type=capa)`): **1:N** (a CAPA may spawn child DCRs — NO latch), an `Idempotency-Key` (NEW `dcr.spawn_idempotency_key` partial-UNIQUE) makes a retry return the same DCR (201 new / 200 replay); a terminal CAPA → 409 `capa_terminal`. **The deferred cross-FK** `document_version.dcr_id` ↔ `dcr.resulting_version_id` lands (`use_alter` 2-table cycle, both named FKs via `op.create_foreign_key`, the `capa.origin_finding_id`↔`audit_finding` precedent). Mig `0044` = the cross-FK pair + `spawn_idempotency_key` + its partial-UNIQUE (excluded in `env.py`) + the `changeRequest.implement` grant-backfill (Process Owner + QMS Owner). NO new permission key (R5) / event type (reuse `DCR_TRANSITIONED`) / enum value (`Implemented`/`Closed` exist since 0040) / Celery task.

**The DCR family (doc 05, the Revision & Change Depth family) is now COMPLETE ✅.** Deferred to the v1.x drift family: scheduled re-review (D5) + drift detection (D1–D4).

## v1 WEB UI track (apps/web — React 18 + Mantine 7 SPA) — STARTED

The SPA was MVP-deferred to just the setup wizard + admin stubs while the API matured. This track ports the owner-approved mockup (`mockup/easysynq-mockup.html`, 8 screens; `styles.css` = 722 design tokens) into the live app as a **vertical operational journey** (UJ-3 review→approve) in 3 slices. Stack: React 18 + Mantine 7 + TanStack Query 5 + react-router 7 + Tailwind 3; tests are **stack-free** via vitest + @testing-library/react + **MSW** + **jest-axe** (the web CI job now also runs `npm test`). WCAG 2.2 AA is a release gate (jest-axe + eslint-jsx-a11y). Spec + plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-06-*`.

- **S-web-1** app shell + design-system foundation (**front-end only — NO migration**) — the single-source **token port** (`mockup/styles.css` `--es-*` → `src/theme/tokens.css`, consumed by BOTH the Mantine theme [system fonts, indigo primary] AND Tailwind; the mockup's `[data-theme="dark"]` re-keyed to `:root[data-mantine-color-scheme="dark"]`); the **app shell** on Mantine `AppShell` (TopBar [disabled ⌘K slot, task/ack bells, user-menu logout] · LeftRail [PLAN/DO/CHECK/ACT clause spine from `GET /clauses` + Home/Library] · Breadcrumb · a deep-linkable `?detail=` resizable focus-trapped **DetailDrawer** · skip-link [zIndex above the header — WCAG 2.2 Focus-Not-Obscured] + ARIA landmarks); an **AuthProvider** context + a token-aware **`useApi()`** client + React Query hooks (`useDocuments`, `useClauses`); **routing** = `AppShell` at `/` (Home index + `/library` live; `/documents/:id` + `/tasks/:id` reserved; `/setup` + `/admin` unchanged); a **thin Library list** from `GET /documents` (Identifier · Title · State badge · Clause chips — friendly type/owner deferred [the list endpoint returns only IDs] + no next-review column [`next_review_due` doesn't exist until the drift family]); a calm **Home placeholder** (full PDCA dashboard = a later slice). 12 vitest tests incl. axe; lint/typecheck/build/test all green. Method: brainstorm (visual companion) → owner forks (vertical journey · 3-slice plan) → spec+plan → subagent-driven TDD with per-logic-task spec+quality review (caught & fixed pre-merge: a `render.tsx` task-ordering bug, the Task-5/6 `StateBadge`↔`DocumentDrawer` import cycle, an `api.ts` import-placement nit, the LibraryPage deep-link empty-shell flash, and a skip-link z-index a11y bug) → whole-branch review **READY TO MERGE**.

`require("document.read")` resolves at SYSTEM scope → would exclude ordinary readers), the directory returns **`{id, display_name}` ONLY** (minimal disclosure, ACTIVE non-guest); `GET /documents` gains a **`{data, page}` pagination envelope** with `offset` (**authz-correct**: scan a bounded candidate window → per-row `document.read` filter → in-memory slice + derived `has_more`, NOT a pre-authz SQL OFFSET; `_LIST_SCAN_CAP=2000`, scale-to-SQL deferred per R34), a `(effective_from, gte/lte)` **date filter** (join the current effective version), and an **`effective_from`** field on the row (batch `_effective_from_map`, the Effective column + header date). `/me/permissions` deliberately deferred to the write slice (S-web-4). **Front-end** (`apps/web`): a 2-col Library — an in-page PDCA-banded **ClauseTree** filter (top+child clauses, exact-number match, no counts) + a 5-facet **FacetBar** (Type/Status/Owner/Clause/Effective-date) with **URL-driven** removable chips + a real **Pagination** (page-size + prev/next on `has_more`) + a results table (resolved Type/Owner via the cached `useDocumentTypes`/`useUserDirectory` maps, 7-state `StateBadge` [now icon+label, moved to `features/document/`], Effective date) + density toggle + skeleton/empty/permission-empty states; a deep-linkable (`?detail=`) **tabbed `DocumentDrawer`** with a shared **`ArtifactHeader`** (DP-5, reused by S-web-3) always-on above lazy-loaded Overview (control-metadata + authenticated controlled-copy download) / History (version timeline; **403→quiet no-access** for a reader lacking `document.read_draft`) / Where-used (§7.2 categories) tabs. - **S-web-4b** the worker-async **visual page-image diff viewer** — the doc 11 §4.7 Side-by-side / page-image mode S-web-4 deferred (**front-end only; NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key, NO `openapi.yaml` change** — the worker-async backend trio was already built + contracted in **S-dcr-3b**). NOT onion-skin/canvas); **D-B** the **Text | Visual `SegmentedControl` lives in `VersionCompare`**, swapping the **byte-identical** S-web-4 `RedlineViewer` (Text) and a new `VisualDiffViewer` (Visual) as siblings — URL-driven `?mode=visual`, reusing the same `?from=&to=` pair; **D-C** the **full** viewer (the §4.7/§6.2 bar), not a minimal single-layer image. **The worker-async contract** (`useVisualDiff`, the S-dcr-3b "POST-compute / pure-GET-poll / stream a page sub-resource" shape): a **POST trigger** (idempotent — UPSERTs the cache row + enqueues only while Pending) seeds the poll cache so the **GET poll** never races the 404-before-request, and `refetchInterval` runs **only while `status==="Pending"`** and halts at any terminal status (the `SetupWizard` precedent); a terminal POST never fires a redundant GET. **`VisualDiffViewer`** (`features/document/`): the single image pane (a new **`apiGetBlob`/`useApi().getBlob`** authed-binary helper — the **only** API-proxied binary in the SPA, every other download is a presigned URL — fetches each page+layer PNG → `objectURL`, **revoked** on every page/layer change + unmount, no leak) + a **changed-page rail** (the §4.7 minimap AND the §6.2 screen-reader change index, driven by `pages[].changed` with a **non-color** glyph + textual "changed") + the Before/After/Diff toggle + **`n`/`p`** next/previous-changed-page nav + a phased **§4.9 long-op** poll (skeletons matching final layout, an `aria-live` region, a manual "Re-request render" for the dev renderer-off "Pending forever" case — never a frozen UI). **Calm terminal states** (not errors): `Unavailable` (a non-renderable R26 version) → a source-download fallback; a page-endpoint **404** ("No image for this page/layer" — an added page's Before / a removed page's After) → a per-side note; `Failed` → a calm terminal with the same source-download fallback (**NOT re-drivable** — `get_or_create_visual_diff` re-enqueues only a `Pending` row, so the viewer offers **no dead Retry** on a terminal Failed; the re-request affordance lives on `Pending` only, for the dev renderer-off case); **403 → quiet** (DP-6). **The hook is keyed by the pair** — `status` is read from the pair-keyed poll cache (seeded by the POST), so changing versions never flashes the prior pair's pages or fires page requests for a not-yet-requested diff; the viewer resets the selected page on a pair change. **0-based** `pages[].page`, labelled 1-based in the UI. **Honest v1 caveat surfaced in-copy:** the watermarked rendition's footer band differs by revision → a near-universal "changed" footer region (raw render = v1.x). **Tests:** **+26 web** across `useVisualDiff` (POST-then-poll→Ready, terminal-without-redundant-GET, Failed/Unavailable/403, `retry()` re-POST), `VisualDiffViewer` (authed page fetch + alt + objectURL, the layer toggle re-fetching `?layer=`, the 404 no-image + non-404 error branches, `n`/`p`, the objectURL **revoke-on-change**, Pending/Failed/Unavailable/403), and `VersionCompare` (the Text|Visual switch + `?mode=` deep-link, RedlineViewer unchanged) — **jest-axe `toHaveNoViolations` release gate** on `VisualDiffViewer` (each state) + `VersionCompare` (both modes); the full web suite stays green (`RedlineViewer.test.tsx` byte-identical). Method: spec+plan (`docs/superpowers/.../2026-06-08-*s-web-4b*`) → TDD → **diff-critic = CLEAN** (2 minor coverage gaps folded: the objectURL revoke + the non-404 image-error branch). Live: the 3 visual-diff routes confirmed **mounted on the running api** (401 vs a 404 control); the full visual click-through needs a 2-version Effective doc (the dev vault has none) + a real render (renderer/worker up). **Next:** S-web-5 (Review & Approve — closes UJ-3).

- **S-web-5** Review & Approve — **CLOSES UJ-3** (author → review → approve → release) (**full-stack but thin: ONE migration-free read endpoint, NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key**; every write [`submit-review`, `POST /tasks/{id}/decision`, `release`] + most reads [`GET /tasks`, `/tasks/{id}`, `/workflow-instances/{id}`, the per-doc `capabilities`, the redline] were already contracted + implemented). New repo helper `latest_instance_for_subject` = **latest, ANY state** (NOT `find_nonterminal_instance`): `lifecycle.release` never closes the instance (it lingers `APPROVED` for an Effective doc — which the stepper *wants* to show) and a `NEEDS_ATTENTION` empty-pool instance must still surface. Gate + serializer reuse `get_instance_endpoint` verbatim (the closed catalog has **no `task.*`/`workflow.*` key** — `document.read` on the subject is the real-world gate). 5 integration tests (instance+tasks / null-never-submitted / 404-unknown / 403-no-read / latest-returns-the-decided-APPROVED-instance; the empty-pool NEEDS_ATTENTION case isn't isolable in the shared-DB integration suite — other tests' org-wide Approver grants populate the pool — so it rides code review). **Front-end** (new `features/review/` + doc-side additions in `features/document/`, dep direction `review → document → lib`, acyclic): a `/tasks` **TasksInbox** (self-scoped `GET /tasks`; task/stage/state/due + link — the per-row Document column deferred, it'd N+1 instance→doc; shown on the review page instead), a per-task **ReviewApprovePage** (task → instance → subject doc → the **reused `VersionCompare`/redline** + the **`DecisionCard`** for a PENDING task; a DONE task shows a read-only "Decided"), the **`DecisionCard`** (Approve / Request-changes / Reject radiogroup; comment **conditional-required** for changes/reject [`aria-describedby` rule]; a DP-10 **signature slot** [a "meaning = approval" confirm checkbox + the honest "v1 — single-factor logged confirmation"]; 403 `sod_violation`/409-already-decided/`step_up_required` all rendered **calmly**; a per-mount `crypto.randomUUID()` **Idempotency-Key** so a retry replays not 409s), an **`ApprovalStepper`** (`features/document/`; the doc-11 §4.4 vertical stepper, **derives nodes from the instance + tasks + the doc's own state** — submit / quality-approval [current/done/rejected per task+instance] / release-to-effective [from the doc `Effective`/`effective_from`, authoritative] — **non-color** glyph+label DP-7, `aria-current="step"`; renders the *actual* single stage, NOT the mockup's aspirational multi-stage spine), the **`ApprovalsTab`** card on `DocumentDetailPage` (stepper + a `capabilities.release`+`Approved`-gated **Release** button + a candidate-only "Review & approve →" deep-link), a **`TaskStateBadge`** (DP-7), and the hooks (`useDocumentApproval`, `useTasks`/`useTask`/`useWorkflowInstance`/`useDecideTask`, `useReleaseDocument`, `useMe`). `lib/api.ts` gains an optional `headers` arg on `send` (the Idempotency-Key path, backward-compatible); `App.tsx` swaps the `tasks/:id` `Reserved` stub for the real `/tasks` + `/tasks/:id` routes; `LeftRail` adds the "Review & Approve" nav. **Tests:** 5 api integration (CI/Linux gate — see the Windows note below) + **+28 web** (vitest+MSW+jest-axe across the hooks, stepper node-derivation per state, DecisionCard conditional-comment/SoD-403/a11y, inbox, review page, the doc-page card; the full suite = **132 web tests** green). Method: 7-agent exploration → owner forks (4 decisions) → spec+plan (`docs/superpowers/.../2026-06-08-*s-web-5*`) → TDD → **diff-critic = 1 CRITICAL, fixed + regression-tested**: `ApprovalsTab` gated the approve CTA on `user.profile.sub` (the OIDC **Keycloak subject**) vs `candidate_pool`/`assignee_user_id`, which are **`app_user.id` UUIDs** — a *different* identifier in production, so the "Review & approve" link would never render for the real approver; **the fixtures had collapsed `sub == /me.id == candidate_pool[0]` (a textbook false-PASS).** Fix = a new `useMe()` (`GET /me` → `app_user.id`), gate on `me.id`, + a regression test with `sub ≠ me.id`. **⚠ The full create→approve→release loop needs 3 DISTINCT users** (SoD-1/2 non-overridable): the `priya`/`ken`/`mara` `just seed-personas` fixture. **Live smoke (DONE — full 3-persona loop in the browser):** priya authored SOP-PUR-002 (Rev A, clause 8.4) → submit-review; **ken** saw it in the new `/tasks` inbox → Review & Approve page → Approve (+ the DP-10 signature confirm) → Approved; **mara** opened the doc page → the Approvals stepper (Submitted ✓ / Approved by Ken ✓ / Released ◉) → **Release** → **Effective**. The `/me.id` fix was genuinely exercised (ken's app_user id was in the candidate pool; his Keycloak `sub` was not). Two **fixture** gaps surfaced + fixed for the demo: the seeded author lacked **`clauseMap.read`** (added to `seed_personas._AUTHOR_KEYS`, the UI clause picker needs it) and the seeded Keycloak users lacked an email/name profile (set via `kcadm` to clear the VERIFY_PROFILE required action — a one-time dev step, not code). Browser-automation note for next time: in-memory tokens mean **full navigations re-auth to `/`** (move via client-side nav). **Browser presigned upload/download fix (post-smoke, now verified live — real browser PUT → 200):** two parts were needed — (1) `S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT=http://localhost:9000` so the presign targets a browser-reachable host (the #90 setting; it was empty), AND (2) the SPA CSP **`connect-src`** must include that object-store origin — `connect-src 'self'` alone blocked the direct browser→MinIO call (a gap #90 missed). Fixed generally: the Caddyfile CSP is now `connect-src 'self' {$S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT}` (templated; the `proxy` service gets `S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT` from `.env`), so browser presigned upload/download works in dev (localhost:9000) and prod alike (set the public object-store host; empty when it's same-origin behind Caddy). `S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT` now **defaults to `http://localhost:9000` in `.env.example`** (and `install.sh` `cp`s that, so a fresh clone gets in-app upload/download working out of the box); the live value lives in the gitignored `.env`. Both browser paths verified live: presigned PUT → 200 + check-in 201; controlled-copy download → a 15.9 KB watermarked PDF (application/pdf) → 200 through the CSP.

- **S-web-6** Global **Search + Compliance Checklist** — surfaces the **S10 search/reporting backend** (PR #38) in the SPA (**front-end only; NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key, NO `openapi.yaml` change** — `GET /search`, `/search/suggest`, `/reports/compliance-checklist` were all already shipped + contracted). Owner forks (3, via `AskUserQuestion`): **palette + results page**; **dedicated gated `/compliance` route**; **`/suggest` quick-jump + a "Search →" footer**. **Search surface** (`features/search/`): a hand-rolled **⌘K command palette** (a Mantine `Modal` — **NO `@mantine/spotlight` dep**; `AppShell` owns the open-state + binds **two** `useHotkeys` — `mod+K` with **empty `tagsToIgnore`** so ⌘K fires even inside an input, and `/` with the default ignore-list so it never hijacks typing; the TopBar's formerly-`disabled` "Search (⌘K)" box is now the live trigger [`aria-label="Open search"`, readOnly, click/Enter/Space]); inside, a `combobox`+`aria-activedescendant` listbox over **debounced** (`useDebouncedValue`, 150 ms) `/suggest` rows (↑/↓/Enter keyboard nav) + a fixed **"Search '<q>' →"** footer action; **Enter = top-hit** when suggestions are loaded (Spotlight/VS-Code style; the default-`active=0` first suggestion), else the full search. The **`/search?q=` results page** (`SearchResultsPage`, URL-driven via `useSearchParams`) = `useSearch` ranked rows (`SearchResultRow`: identifier · title→`/documents/:id` · reused `StateBadge` · clause chips→`/library?clause=N` · the **XSS-safe `Snippet`** — splits PostgreSQL `ts_headline`'s literal `<b>…</b>` into `<Mark>`, renders every other segment as a React **text node**, **NO `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`** [a `<script>` in a title renders as literal text]) + the **`hidden_by_scope` footer** ("N hidden by your access scope") + an **honesty hint** ("title/identifier/clause refs — Effective documents only") + **calm** empty/no-results/**error** states (search **filters, never 403s**). **Compliance surface** (`features/compliance/`): a dedicated **`/compliance`** route + a **`LeftRail` entry gated on `usePermissions().can("report.compliance_checklist.read")`** (hidden unless held — the SYSTEM key sits with QMS Owner + Internal Auditor, **not** the demo admin; `useComplianceChecklist` surfaces a **`forbidden`** flag from `ApiError.status===403`+`retry:false` → a **calm no-access panel**, not a crash); the page = a **RAG rollup** (a **non-color** glyph+label+count legend — `✓ Covered / ◔ Partial / ✕ Gap`, *not* badges, to avoid a duplicate-`aria-label` clash with the table) + the **20★ clause `Table`** (`CoverageBadge` COVERED/PARTIAL/GAP, **DP-7** glyph+label) with each clause row → `/library?clause=N` (the doc-13 §3.1 drill-through; reuses the existing Library clause filter). **Tests:** **+30 web** (vitest + MSW + jest-axe) across the hooks (`useSearch`/`useSuggest` enabled-guards · `useComplianceChecklist` success+403), the **XSS-safe `Snippet`** (incl. a `<script>`-as-text guard), the `CommandPalette` (suggest→doc nav · footer→`/search` · Enter · **axe**), the `SearchResultsPage` (URL-driven · `hidden_by_scope` · no-results · **error** · axe), `CoverageBadge`, the `CompliancePage` (rollup · drill-through href · **403-calm** · axe rows+403), the **gated nav** (shown/hidden by `/me/permissions`), the shell wiring (⌘K + click open the palette), and the `/search`+`/compliance` routes — the full suite = **162 web tests** green (lint + tsc-strict + build all clean; tsc caught a `noUncheckedIndexedAccess` nit the per-task vitest runs missed). Method: scout → owner forks (3) → spec+plan (`docs/superpowers/.../2026-06-08-*s-web-6*`) → **subagent-driven TDD** (fresh implementer per task + per-task spec+quality review) — confirmed fixes folded: a **calm search-error state** (the results page silently showed nothing on a fetch error), the rollup **duplicate-`aria-label`** → the plain glyph+label legend, and the strict-index typecheck fix. **Honest deferrals** (the backend can't serve them): server-side **facets** + **saved searches** + **content-plane/body-text** search + the §2.3 owner/process/date facets + auditor **exports** (§7) + the Home **center-hub ★ tile** (the PDCA dashboard stays deferred until its acknowledgement/objective engines exist — the Compliance Checklist is the one *honest* health signal available now, and the future dashboard's center-hub). **Demo precondition:** the Checklist needs a **QMS-Owner / Internal-Auditor login** (or a SYSTEM override of `report.compliance_checklist.read` for the demo admin — the authoring-keys precedent); **search** works for any logged-in user. only an explicit per-row/bulk Confirm sets `after.kind ∈ {DOCUMENT,RECORD}`). **Merge/split server-authoritative** (submit→invalidate, never optimistic reshape; the cockpit builds `dupeMap`/`familyMap`/`splitTargetMap` from the `/dupe-clusters`+`/version-families` lists since the row list carries no membership). Every write carries ONE `crypto.randomUUID()` `Idempotency-Key` per op. - **S-web-7b** CAPA **lifecycle writes** — second installment of the **S-web-7 NC & CAPA front-door epic**; **CLOSES the ACT-phase write loop** (raise → containment → root-cause → action-plan[approved] → implement → verify[SIGNED] → close, with the Verify→RootCause effectiveness loop + the M4 evidence close gate). **Not pure front-end** (the epic labelled it so, but the action-plan approval loop can't work without it): a **thin read-enrichment mirroring 7a — NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key** (every read reuses `capa.read`/self-scope). 2 CI integration tests. **Front-end (`features/capa/` + `features/review/`):** a contextual **`AdvancePanel`** (switches on `close_state` → the ONE legal next-stage form, `usePermissions`-gated at the CAPA's **PROCESS** scope [SYSTEM fallback], a calm read-only line when the key is absent, an "awaiting approval"/"no approver assigned" panel at RootCause from the approval read); **`StageForms`** (the 5 structured stage forms whose `content_block` keys round-trip through the 7a `ContentBlock` renderer + a server-authoritative **`CloseAction`** [always-enabled; the 409 `capa_close_incomplete`/`capa_not_verified` is the gate, surfaced calmly; a `not_effective` Verify → "Return to root cause"]); a signed **VerifyForm** (the S-web-5 v1 logged-confirmation checkbox; `409 sod_self_verify` → a calm SoD-4 message); an **`EvidenceLinker`** (link an EXISTING record → `POST /records/{id}/evidence-links target_type=capa_stage`; no upload — epic §7) rendered **only on the current cycle's** Implement/Verify stages (a looped CAPA's prior-cycle linkers would duplicate the "Record (Verify)" accessible name — the S-web-6 trap); the **`CloseGateStepper`** `deriveGate` made **evidence-aware + 2-arg** `(stages, cycleMarker)`, matching the backend `close_capa` EXACTLY (root_cause cycle-AGNOSTIC; implemented-action + effectiveness CURRENT-cycle + ≥1 evidence; a `not_effective` Verify never satisfies effectiveness — the 7a `closeState==="Closed"` proxy is gone); a board-level **`RaiseCapaModal`** (gated `capa.create`; `review_output` source omitted — the API 422s it); and the **subject-aware `/tasks` `ReviewApprovePage`** (branches on `task.subject_type`: CAPA → a new **`CapaApprovalContext`** [identity + the proposed plan, gated `capa.read` only] + a **generalized `DecisionCard`** [`documentId`→`{subjectType, subjectId}`; the decision POST already dispatches CAPA→`decide_capa_action_plan` server-side]; the DOCUMENT path stays **byte-identical**, decision-pane still `decidable && docId`-gated). Mutations **invalidate + refetch**, never optimistic reshape. - **S-web-7c** Complaint & NCR **intake** — third installment of the **S-web-7 NC & CAPA front-door epic**; surfaces the two lightweight front doors that feed the 7a board. **FRONT-END ONLY — NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key, NO `openapi.yaml` change** (the `/complaints*` + `/ncrs*` surface [S-capa-1, `api/capa.py:493-617`] was already shipped + contracted). Owner fork (1, via `AskUserQuestion`): the page structure — **tabbed sub-routes under `/capa`** (vs local-state tabs / separate nav entries). **A thin `CapaLayout`** (a Mantine `Tabs` strip Board·Complaints·NCRs + `<Outlet/>`, active tab from `useLocation().pathname`, `onChange`→`useNavigate`) wraps three child routes — `/capa` index (**`CapaBoardPage`**, keeps its own title), `/capa/complaints`, `/capa/ncrs`; the board's existing flows stay unchanged (it gained only one additive `?capa=<id>` deep-link seam — see Codex below); `LeftRail` stays a single "Nonconformity & CAPA" entry, each tab deep-linkable. **Complaints** (`ComplaintsPage` + `ComplaintForm`): a table (Identifier/Customer/Channel/Severity/Description/CAPA) over `useComplaints` (`GET /complaints`, `{data}`, `forbidden`-flag calm-403); a `record.create`-gated "Log complaint" modal (description\* + customer + channel + optional severity); and a per-row **idempotent spawn-CAPA** — the `_complaint` row's **`spawned_capa_id` drives the affordance**: null → a `capa.create`-gated "Spawn CAPA" button → a **`SpawnCapaModal` severity-confirm** step (pre-filled from the complaint, **required** — a CAPA needs a severity, the backend 422s without one, and a complaint can be logged severity-less; also the backend's "request severity = late triage" intent), set → a "View CAPA" link to `/capa` (no process picker — the 7b deferred Raise-scope decision). **The spawn's 201-new / 200-replay distinction is surfaced as STATE, not the HTTP status** — `api.send` discards the status, so the row flips via `spawned_capa_id` after the invalidate; a racing replay just resolves (`["complaints"]` + `["capas"]` both invalidated). **NCRs** (`NcrsPage` + `NcrForm` + `DispositionModal`): a table (Identifier/Source/Severity/Description/Disposition) over `useNcrs` (`ncr.read` calm-403); an `ncr.create`-gated "Raise NCR" modal (source\* + severity\* + description\*); and a per-row **one-shot ISO 8.7 disposition** — an undisposed NCR with `ncr.record_correction` gets a "Record disposition" modal (the 6 dispositions `use_as_is/rework/scrap/return/concession/regrade` + notes; `PATCH /ncrs/{id}/disposition`), a **disposed NCR renders its disposition read-only with NO action button** (the one-shot is structural in the UI), and a `409 ncr_already_dispositioned` (a race) is surfaced **calmly** in the modal, never a crash. All affordances gate via `usePermissions().can(key)` at **SYSTEM** scope (the 7b precedent — v1 grants ride SYSTEM overrides). Free-form text (descriptions) renders via Mantine `Text lineClamp` (**XSS-safe**, no `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`). Filters/summary tiles **deferred** (YAGNI — intake lists are bounded + scannable). **Per-key gating diverges from the board:** complaints ride `record.read`/`record.create`/spawn=`capa.create`; NCRs ride `ncr.read`/`ncr.create`/`ncr.record_correction` — the **`demo` System-Administrator holds NONE** (both tabs calm-403, like the board), and **`ncr.create` + `ncr.record_correction` are seeded but granted to NO role** (SYSTEM-override-only in v1). Fixtures pinned to the real `_complaint`/`_ncr` serializers (NOT the mockup — the #1 false-PASS lesson). **Tests: +35 web → the full suite = 429 web tests** green (lint + tsc-strict + build all clean). - **S-web-8** the trailing **drift-family UI** — surfaces the completed D1–D5 backend (S-drift-1…3) in the SPA (**FRONT-END ONLY: NO migration [head stays `0047`], NO new permission key, NO endpoint, NO `openapi.yaml` change** — consumes exactly `GET /admin/drift/status` + `GET /admin/drift/superseded-copies` [`drift.read`, R41] and the S-drift-1 read surface). Design calls settled in brainstorming (none register-level): **(1)** the drift surface = a main-`AppShell` **`/drift`** route + a `can("drift.read")`-gated LeftRail entry (the S-ing-4b `/ingestion` precedent — NOT the token-threaded AdminShell) with a `DriftLayout` tab pair (Status · **Superseded copies as a PAGE, not a drawer** — it's a paginated recall list, server `offset`/`limit`, no virtualization); **(2)** the `PERIODIC_REVIEW` task leg is **front-end-only** — the task detail already carries `subject_type`/`subject_id` (S-web-7b), the doc context loads **BEST-EFFORT** via `GET /documents/{id}` with **graceful 403 degradation that never blocks the decision card** (ownership is the server-side authority — the CAPA-path lesson generalized) and **never touches `GET /workflow-instances/*`** (spy-proven); **(3)** review-period editing = rows in the Control-metadata card + a **conditionally-rendered modal** gated on **`doc.capabilities.manage_metadata`** (the server-computed per-doc answer; clear = an **explicit `null`** — `model_fields_set`). **Four surfaces:** `features/drift/` (StatusPage = two DP-7-badged scan cards rendering `counts` as a **generic sorted OPEN bag** [unknown-key test; §10a] + the `blob_coverage.failing` re-alarm Alert + the D4 headline; SupersededCopiesPage = the 7-col recall table + Mantine `Pagination` driving the server offset; both calm-403); the `ReviewApprovePage` third branch (+`PeriodicReviewContext`, the obsolete-is-a-LINK note per S-drift-1 §5); the `DecisionCard` `PERIODIC_REVIEW` variant (outcomes **`complete` | `changes_requested`** via per-subject OUTCOMES tables — DOCUMENT/CAPA **byte-identical**, regression-pinned; the signature checkbox = "meaning: review confirmed"); the doc page's **deferred-since-S-web-1 "Next review" tile** (`daysUntil` days + date + `ReviewStateBadge` [server-derived, org-tz authoritative]) + `ControlMetadata` review rows; the compliance checklist's **overdue-review leg** (plain-text rollup counter + a per-row DP-7 badge — orthogonal to status, never a 4th coverage state). **Tests: +52 web → the full suite = 551** (lint + tsc-strict + build clean). Method: brainstorm → spec+plan (`docs/superpowers/.../2026-06-10-*s-web-8*`) → **subagent-driven TDD** (11 tasks, fresh implementer + two-stage spec→quality review per task; per-task reviews caught real bugs: a `retry: opts.retry` spread that would CLOBBER QueryClient defaultOptions with `undefined`, a reopen-pristine test that couldn't distinguish remount from persistence until the field was dirtied first, the DP-7 badge idiom on every new badge, an error-branch heading spine) → **diff-critic = 3 confirmed MINORs, all folded**: the periodic 409 now disambiguates by problem title (a stale double-decide ["Task already decided", a 2nd tab with its own per-mount idempotency key] no longer reads as "obsoleted"); `PeriodicReviewContext` passes `retry:false` (an EXPECTED 403 must not re-hammer the deny 3× under production QueryClient defaults — plus a **production-defaults test** pinning exactly one request, since the global test wrapper's `retry:false` masks retry regressions); the PATCH fixture dropped `clause_refs` (the real write response is bare `_document`). **Live smoke (the inherited S-drift-3 obligation DISCHARGED):** both drift endpoints hit authed-200 as the logged-in `demo` with real data — the status page rendered the REAL beat scans whose MIRROR counts carried keys the fixture never had (`baseline`/`pointer`/`build_name`/`symlink_divergent` — the open-bag contract proven live), and the smoke caught a **fixture-vs-serializer drift** (the real BLOB_REHASH key is **`sample_limit`**, not the spec's `sample_size` — pinned); superseded-copies = the honest **empty state** (this install has NO Superseded versions; minting one needs the full 3-persona FSM loop — the row rendering is CI-integration-proven, accepted residual). Full D5 loop live: backdate → sweep (`tasks_created: 1`) → checklist `⏰ Review overdue: 1` + the 8.4 row **COVERED + ▲ OVERDUE** (orthogonality live) → the periodic task page → **complete + review-confirmed signature** (the `signature_event` + `REVIEW_CONFIRMED` audit verified in PG) → the tile reset to **365 days ✓ CURRENT** → the PATCH modal (24 months → **731 days / 2028-06-10**, server-recomputed) → checklist cleared to 0. ⚠ **Live-login trap (new flavor):** the demo login's **System Administrator ROLE sat on the OLD bootstrap `app_user` row** — a re-created Keycloak `demo` JIT-mints a new row that holds NO role, so `drift.read`/import keys vanish from the rail; check `role_assignment` (not just overrides) against the LIVE subject's row and re-assign. **Honest deferrals:** a live D4 table row (above); the Library "Next review" column (mockup 2196); DCR deep-link prefill on `changes_requested` (no SPA DCR UI exists); the `/tasks` inbox row label stays the raw `action_expected` token. **The PDCA dashboard remains the web track's open item** (deferred until acks/objectives land).
